--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: I need to cancel a booking I accidentally accepted - what are the fees? ---
Owner cancellation fees depend on timing and cause:

**For Cause cancellations (unavoidable circumstances):**
- Up to 2 cancellations per 6-month rolling window without fees
- After that: $50 if cancelled 7+ days before rental, $100 if less than 7 days

**Without Cause cancellations (inaccurate listing, poor maintenance, failure to meet renter):**
- Minimum 30% of booking rental amount

Fees are deducted from future payouts. Any cancellation after rental has started will be denied.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: I received a circumvention penalty - what does this mean? ---
Circumvention occurs when you receive a booking through Neighbors Trailer but attempt to complete part or all of the rental outside the platform. This includes sharing direct contact information or arranging payment outside the system before an accepted booking.

The penalty is typically $200 (reduced from the full policy amount). The policy applies whether the rental actually happens or not.

**Why this policy exists:**
- Off-platform rentals are high risk for damage, theft, liability
- Platform provides safety measures like ID verification and fraud detection
- Protects investments and maintains fairness for other owners

--- [Renter] [damage-claims] Q: I need to file a fraud report about my credit card being charged incorrectly ---
For elevated fraud risk transactions, renters may be asked to provide verification by sending a photo of their credit card showing their name, with all numbers except last 4 digits blocked out.

For legitimate fraud concerns about incorrect charges, direct them to contact their credit card company to dispute the charge while also contacting Neighbors Trailer support to investigate the booking in question.

--- [Both] [damage-claims] Q: What should I check before towing a trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-should-I-check-before-towing-a-trailer--203
Before towing, take a few minutes to complete this safety checklist. A proper pre-trip inspection can help prevent accidents, equipment damage, and roadside issues.

Download our printable Pre-Trip Tow Safety Card (PDF) for a quick glovebox version of this checklist.

 

1. Verify Your Tow Vehicle

• Confirm your vehicle's towing capacity is sufficient for the loaded trailer.
• Check that your receiver hitch size matches your ball mount.
• Ensure your vehicle has a brake controller if required.
• Inspect mirrors and adjust for proper rear visibility.
 

2. Confirm Proper Hitch & Coupler Connection

• Verify you are using the correct hitch ball size (1-7/8", 2", or 2-5/16").
• Ensure the hitch ball is properly torqued and tightened.
• Insert the ball mount fully into the receiver and secure it with a hitch pin and clip.
• Open the trailer coupler latch before lowering it onto the hitch ball.
• Lower the coupler completely onto the ball.
• Close and secure the coupler latch.
• Insert a safety pin or coupler lock, if available.
• Perform a gentle pull test to confirm the trailer is securely attached.
 

3. Attach Safety Chains & Wiring

• Cross the safety chains underneath the trailer tongue (forming an "X").
• Attach chains securely to the tow vehicle.
• Ensure chains have enough slack for turning, but do not drag.
• Connect the trailer light plug.
• Test:• Brake lights
• Turn signals
• Running lights
• Hazard lights

 

4. Inspect Tires & Brakes

• Check tire pressure on both the trailer and tow vehicle.
• Inspect tires for visible damage or excessive wear.
• Confirm lug nuts appear secure.
• Verify trailer brakes are functioning properly (if equipped).
 

5. Check Load & Weight Distribution

• Confirm the trailer is not overloaded (verify GVWR on the VIN sticker).
• Follow the 60/40 rule:• 60% of weight toward the front
• 40% toward the rear

• Ensure cargo is evenly distributed side-to-side.
• Secure all cargo with straps or tie-downs.
• Double-check that nothing can shift during transit.
 

6. Final Walk-Around

• Raise and secure the trailer jack fully.
• Remove wheel chocks.
• Confirm ramps or doors are closed and latched.
• Make sure license plates are visible.
• Perform one last visual inspection before driving away.
 

Pro Tip:
After driving a short distance (5–10 miles), pull over and recheck your hitch connection, straps, and load security.

Taking a few extra minutes before departure can significantly improve safety and reduce the risk of towing-related issues.

Want a deeper breakdown of towing capacity, braking requirements, and real-world safety examples?
Read our Ultimate Trailer Towing Safety Guide.

--- [Both] [damage-claims] Q: What are the 3 most important trailer safety tips? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/3-Most-Important-Safety-Tips-165
Before towing, take a few minutes to review these essential safety tips to help reduce the risk of accidents and equipment damage.

1. Make sure you have the right tow vehicle and equipment

• Verify your vehicle's towing capacity.
• Use the correct hitch and ball size for the trailer.
• Confirm you have a brake controller, if required. If your vehicle is not equipped with one, consider using a wireless Bluetooth brake controller.
Using the proper equipment is critical for safe towing.

2. Understand the trailer's weight limits and setup requirements

• Choose a trailer with enough weight capacity to support your load.• Weight Capacity = GVWR – Empty Weight

• Never overload a trailer.
• Follow the 60/40 loading rule: place approximately 60% of the load toward the front of the trailer and 40% toward the rear to maintain proper tongue weight.
When connecting the trailer:

• Ensure the coupler latch is open before lowering it onto the hitch ball.
• Securely close and lock the coupler latch.
• Attach safety chains (crossed underneath the tongue).
• Connect the light plug.
• Perform a full pre-trip inspection, including tires, lights, brakes, hitch connection, and load security.
Always double-check all connections before driving away.

3. Practice safe towing habits on the road

• Drive at a safe, controlled speed.
• Stay in the right lane when possible.
• Maintain extra distance from other vehicles.
• Take wider turns to avoid curbs and obstacles.
• Inspect the trailer and load at each stop.
• Use a spotter when backing up whenever possible.
These quick safety tips are a great starting point before towing.

For a detailed breakdown of towing capacity limits, braking requirements, speed safety, and real-world examples, review our Ultimate Trailer Towing Safety Guide.

You can also watch our safety video: Prepare Your Rental | Neighbors Trailer.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: What happens when a renter disputes my damage claim? ---
When a renter disputes a damage claim, Neighbors Trailer will review the circumstances and supporting documentation before making a determination. Inform the owner they will be contacted to provide feedback and additional information. Common examples include disputes over whether damage was pre-existing, normal wear and tear, or caused during rental. --- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: Can I file a damage claim after the rental has ended? ---
Explain that late damage claims (filed days after rental completion) have limited options. If more than a few days have passed since rental ended, the best option is to ask the renter to pay voluntarily. If the renter disputes it, there's limited recourse unless the owner has clear before photos showing no damage existed prior to rental. For this reason, emphasize the critical importance of thoroughly inspecting the trailer immediately upon return and filing any damage claims when ending the rental in the system. Late-discovered damage like bent axles or structural issues should still be reported, but may require renter cooperation for resolution.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: How do I handle a major accident or significant damage during a rental? ---
For major accidents or significant damage (like crashes, bent frames, etc.), instruct the owner to contact Neighbors Trailer Support immediately if they're having trouble ending the rental in the system. Support can assist with uploading photos, entering remarks, and completing the rental ending process when damage estimates are substantial (e.g., $6,300+). If the trailer owner has existing MBA insurance coverage, note that they will not be covered under Neighbors Trailer's policy due to MBA's double coverage restrictions - their rentals are still eligible under their MBA policy instead. Direct owners to contact MBA Insurance for questions about their existing coverage.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: What should I do if a renter damages my trailer's brakes or electrical system? ---
When renters tamper with or damage brake wiring, electrical connections, or related systems, treat this as a serious safety issue. Document any renter admissions of modifying wiring or brake systems. If the renter replaced components with used parts or altered wiring, the owner may be entitled to have the system properly restored to factory specifications. For issues with exposed brake wires, damaged plugs, or electrical modifications, recommend having the trailer serviced by a qualified technician to ensure safety and proper function. Note that brake system integrity is critical for safety and proper repairs should not be compromised.

--- [Internal] [damage-claims] Q: How do I handle tire age disputes in damage claims? ---
When reviewing tire damage claims, always request the 4-digit DOT date code from the tire sidewall. Tires 3 years old or older (based on DOT code) should be considered owner responsibility due to age-related wear. For newer tires (like date codes 2422, 2122), the damage is more likely renter responsibility if caused by impact, overloading, or improper use. Consider factors like: tire age, mileage on trailer, storage conditions, and specific cause of failure. Even with newer tires, if damage was caused by speed, overloading, or road hazards during rental, the renter should be responsible. Document the tire date code verification in your review.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: How do I prove damage was caused by the renter and not pre-existing? ---
Emphasize the critical importance of taking detailed photos before and after each rental. Time-stamped photos are essential evidence - note that some devices allow timestamp manipulation, so consider this when reviewing evidence. For disputed claims, gather: before photos clearly showing undamaged condition, after photos showing damage, any GPS or tracking data showing trailer location/usage, communications with renter, and witness statements if available. Common pre-existing conditions that may be disputed include: normal wear and tear on aluminum panels, age-related component failure, and manufacturing defects. If you cannot prove the renter caused specific damage, you may need to accept a reduced claim or compromise.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: What constitutes normal wear and tear vs. renter damage? ---
Normal wear and tear that is typically owner responsibility includes: screws coming out of aluminum skin due to vibration and manufacturing issues, age-related tire failure (3+ years old), worn brake components from normal use, and minor cosmetic issues from regular operation. Renter damage typically includes: impact damage from collisions or striking objects, overloading damage, damage from improper hitching or unhitching, electrical damage from incorrect connections, and damage from failure to follow operating instructions. Borderline cases (like curb rash on tires) may require compromise between owner and renter. Manufacturing defects that manifest during rental may not be renter responsibility even if they occur during the rental period.

--- [Policy] [damage-claims] Q: When should I hold a renter's deposit vs. process through NT Protect? ---
For eligible damage during verified rental periods, process through NT Protect coverage (up to $25,000 with $500 deductible). Place temporary $500 holds on renter's credit card while gathering information to determine cause of damage. For late returns, assess late fees separately from damage claims. For cases where damage exceeds deductible or involves coverage questions, coordinate with the claims process. Note that trailer owners with existing MBA insurance cannot use Neighbors Trailer coverage due to double coverage restrictions - their claims should go through MBA instead. Always verify coverage eligibility before processing damage claims.


## CANCELLATION ##

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: What happens when a renter disputes a charge/does a chargeback? ---
When a renter initiates a credit card dispute/chargeback, explain that:
- Neighbors Trailer responds to every credit card dispute with an experienced team
- If the bank decides in favor of the renter and refunds them, the owner payout will be reversed per the Owner Payout Policy in the Terms of Use (https://neighborstrailer.com/terms)
- This applies regardless of Neighbors Trailer's cancellation policy - financial institutions have their own policies that take priority
- Neighbors Trailer covers the chargeback fee charged by the credit card company
- If the owner has already been paid, the payout amount will be deducted from their account or future payouts
- To avoid chargebacks, owners should embrace the policies at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms

Also asked as: Payout Reversal Notice

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What are the exact cancellation policy details and refund percentages? ---
Provide the detailed cancellation policy:
- 72+ hours before rental start: 75% refund
- 48-72 hours before rental start: 50% refund  
- 24-48 hours before rental start: 25% refund
- Less than 24 hours before rental start: No refund
- Same-day bookings: No refund
- Platform fees are non-refundable once booking is accepted
- No-show is treated as renter cancellation without notice (no refund)
- All cancellations must be done through the renter's account using "Cancel Booking" - phone, text, email or other methods will NOT cancel a booking
- Refunds processed within 10 days to original payment method

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Can I get a refund for early return of the trailer? ---
Early return refunds have specific rules:
- Early return refunds are only processed for full rental days (24+ hours)
- No refunds for partial days or hours returned early
- For completed rentals, partial refunds are at the owner's discretion and not guaranteed
- If processed manually after rental completion, there is a $25 processing fee deducted from the owner's payout
- Maximum refundable amount for early returns is 80% of base rental amount for unused portion
- Owner must approve through their account or contact support to process manually

POLICY: Refunds are only issued for full unused rental days. Partial-day early returns (e.g., returned 4 hours early) do not qualify for a refund. If a renter returns a full day or more early, a refund for the unused full day(s) may be processed. Owners can also initiate partial refunds from their account at their discretion.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How do I help a renter get a full refund when the rental didn't happen due to my fault? ---
Ask for the reason the rental did not take place. If it was due to owner issues (mechanical problems, trailer unavailability, etc.), this should be processed as an Owner Cancellation:
- Owner should go to Booking Details page and select "Cancel Booking"
- This automatically issues the renter a full refund of all amounts paid
- Standard 30% Owner cancellation fee will apply per Terms
- For mechanical issues, advise owner to have equipment repaired before relisting

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: How do I deactivate my owner account? ---
To deactivate an owner account:
- Confirm the user wants to proceed with deactivation
- Explain that once deactivated, their listing will no longer be visible to renters or receive booking requests
- Process the account deactivation on the backend
- Let them know they can reach out in the future if they want to reactivate
- No action needed from the user - support handles the deactivation

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: The owner told me the trailer isn't available but I need to cancel myself - will I get charged? ---
This situation should be handled as an Owner Cancellation, not a renter cancellation:
- The owner should have cancelled the booking themselves through the platform
- When owners instruct renters to cancel due to owner unavailability, this is improper
- Investigate the situation and if confirmed as owner's fault, process as Owner Cancellation
- Renter should receive full refund, and owner pays the 30% cancellation fee
- Correct the situation by processing additional refund if renter was incorrectly charged

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I was told the booking wasn't accepted but I see a charge on my account? ---
Explain the payment authorization process:
- Payment is only authorized (not charged) until booking is accepted
- If booking is never accepted or is rejected, only a temporary hold was placed
- The hold is immediately released when booking is cancelled/rejected
- May take up to 24 hours to reflect on bank statement depending on financial institution
- No actual charge was processed

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: Can I get an emergency cancellation refund? ---
For emergency cancellations:
- Emergency cancellations may not qualify for full refund beyond standard policy
- First recommend trying to reschedule instead of cancel if possible
- Rescheduling conditions: owner must be notified 24+ hours before original start, only one reschedule allowed, new date within 60 days, owner must agree
- If rescheduling isn't possible, standard cancellation policy applies
- Contact owner as soon as possible through booking platform
- In extreme circumstances, escalate to human support for review

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Can I get a waiver of cancellation fees? ---
Cancellation fee waivers are very limited:

- New user confusion or emergencies typically do not qualify for fee waiver

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How should support handle disputed cancellation situations? ---
For cancellation disputes:

- When reviewing edge cases, escalate to management if staff discretion is needed

- Allow reasonable time for party-to-party resolution before platform intervention

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: When should cancellation fees be waived? ---
Based on staff responses, waive cancellation fees in these situations:

1. Severe weather conditions that make pickup unsafe
2. Trailer listing inaccuracies (wrong dimensions, flat tires, incorrect hitch size)
3. Owner offers different trailer than listed and renter declines
4. If customer books a different trailer immediately and the new booking is accepted
5. Mechanical failures or safety issues that make the trailer unusable

Do NOT waive fees when:
• Customer's vehicle is incompatible with properly listed trailer specifications
• Customer needs equipment not included in listing (like winches)
• Customer made booking error (wrong location)

Note: Original booking fees are always non-refundable even when cancellation fees are waived.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How to handle no-shows and unresponsive owners? ---
If an owner doesn't respond to a booking request:
• Contact the owner to notify them of the pending booking
• If still no response after multiple attempts, reject the booking due to lack of owner response
• Process full refund to renter (12-24 hours to reflect)

If a renter doesn't show up:
• Owner can start and end the rental as a "no-show"
• No-shows are treated as renter cancellation without notice (no refund)
• If renter claims they cancelled but it still shows active, verify cancellation was not completed properly

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: What if the trailer doesn't match the listing? ---
If the trailer has significant discrepancies from the listing (wrong size, flat tires, incorrect hitch, missing safety equipment), this qualifies for a full refund.

Request the booking ID and review the specific issues. Common problems that warrant full refunds:
• Incorrect dimensions that affect usability
• Flat or damaged tires making trailer unsafe
• Wrong hitch ball size preventing pickup
• Missing essential safety equipment

Cancel the booking and process a full refund, allowing a few days for the refund to reflect on their bank statement.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: A renter wants to cancel but the owner supports waiving fees - what happens? ---
POLICY: Owners cannot override or waive the platform cancellation fee policy. However, owners CAN voluntarily issue partial refunds from their own payout at their discretion via their account. These are two different things — cancellation fees are platform-level, partial refunds are owner-level.

Explain that trailer owners do not have the authority to independently waive cancellation fees as this bypasses Terms of Service. However, owners can process partial refunds from their account at their discretion.

If the owner wants to provide additional compensation beyond what the cancellation policy allows, they can use the partial refund feature within the booking details before ending the rental.

If they need fewer days, their options are:
1. Keep the booking as-is and return early (ask owner for partial refund)
2. Cancel and rebook for correct dates (subject to cancellation fees)

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Who should cancel when both parties want to cancel the booking? ---
The party responsible for the cancellation must cancel the booking. If the renter wants to cancel, they must do it through their account to receive their refundable deposit back. Owners cannot cancel on behalf of renters without taking the owner cancellation fee. If an owner can't fulfill the rental, they should cancel from their end so the renter receives a full refund.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How do I provide a partial refund to a renter after a completed rental? ---

If they want to void their entire payout and return it to the renter, this can be done but will incur processing fees deducted from the refunded amount. If the rental has already ended, they cannot process a partial refund themselves and must contact support.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Can cancellation policies be adjusted or exceptions made? ---
The cancellation policy is not adjustable and is based on how close to pickup date the cancellation occurs. Staff cannot waive cancellation fees as they cover actual booking fees and transaction costs. However, in cases where the owner was unable to fulfill the rental due to circumstances beyond the renter's control (owner no-show, trailer unavailable, etc.), support may authorize full refunds on a case-by-case basis.

From App: Bookings > Select booking > Tap "Change Trailer"

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: When will I get my refund after canceling? ---
For pending bookings that are canceled or rejected: Payment is only authorized, not charged. The hold releases immediately and money returns to the card, but may take 12-24 hours to reflect on the statement.

For accepted bookings that are canceled: Refunds are processed within 10 days from approval date to the original payment method.

For deposit refunds: Automatically initiated when owner ends rental (if no damages/late fees), takes 4-7 business days to appear on statement.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Can I get a full refund due to an emergency? ---
Emergency cancellations do not automatically qualify for full refunds beyond the standard cancellation policy. However, offer these options:

1. Rescheduling (if conditions met): Owner must be notified 24+ hours before start time, rental can only be rescheduled once, new date within 60 days of original, owner must agree.

2. Request owner use partial refund feature (max 75% of rental amount, booking fees still non-refundable).

3. If owner agrees to cancel the booking themselves, renter gets full refund but owner pays 30% cancellation fee.

For genuine emergencies with documentation, escalate to human support for case-by-case review.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: A renter wants to cancel - how do I help them? ---

From web: Dashboard > My Bookings > select 3 dots under "Action" > Upcoming Booking > Cancel Booking
From mobile: Bookings > "More" at top-right of booking > Cancel Booking

If you cancel instead of the renter, you will be charged the owner cancellation fee (30% of rental amount). Only cancel yourself if the cancellation is your fault (trailer unavailable, broken, etc.).

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Can I give a renter a full refund? ---
Full refunds are not possible once a booking is accepted because booking fees are non-refundable. Options available:

1. Partial refund feature: You can issue up to 75% of rental amount (must be done before ending rental). Booking fees, tax, and insurance remain non-refundable.

2. Cancel the booking yourself: This gives renter a full refund but charges you a 30% cancellation fee.

For partial refunds processed after ending rental, there's an additional $25 processing fee deducted from renter's refund.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: My trailer is broken/unavailable - what do I do? ---
If your trailer is not available due to mechanical issues, damage, or other problems on your end, you must cancel the booking from the booking details page by selecting "Cancel Booking." This will process a full refund to the renter but you will be charged a 30% cancellation fee.

Do NOT tell the renter to cancel if the issue is on your end - this violates the cancellation policy and can result in additional fees being assessed to your account.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: The renter doesn't have the right hitch/vehicle - who cancels? ---
If the renter arrives without proper equipment (wrong hitch size, inadequate towing vehicle, etc.), this is typically the renter's responsibility since equipment requirements are listed in your listing. The renter should cancel and pay the applicable cancellation fee.

However, once funds are settled after rental completion, support cannot assist with refunds - you would need to contact the renter directly if you choose to reimburse them.

If there are legal safety concerns (like exceeding legal towing limits), document this and contact support for guidance.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Renter is unresponsive - can I cancel? ---
If a renter books but becomes completely unresponsive to messages about pickup coordination, document your attempts to contact them. If they continue to be non-responsive and the rental time passes, this constitutes a no-show by the renter.

Do not cancel preemptively. If concerned about communication, contact support for assistance. If renter actually no-shows, they receive no refund per policy.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: The owner wants me to cancel but said I'd get a full refund - is this true? ---
IMPORTANT: If an owner tells you that you'll get a full refund by canceling, this contradicts the cancellation policy. Standard cancellation fees will apply based on timing. 

If an owner makes promises about full refunds that contradict policy, they may be attempting to circumvent proper procedures. The owner should cancel themselves if the issue is on their end, which would give you a true full refund but charge them a fee.

Report situations where owners give incorrect policy information to support.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: Can I exchange my booked trailer for a different one from the same owner? ---
Yes, if both you and the owner agree, you can exchange trailers without canceling the booking. This can be done from either account:

From website: Dashboard > Bookings > select booking > Change Trailer
From mobile app: Bookings > tap booking > Change Trailer

There's no fee to exchange trailers. If there's a price difference, you'll see either a refund or additional charge during the process, shown as "Transferred Adjustment Amount" on the receipt.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Renter wants early return refund - can I provide this? ---
You can provide partial refunds for early returns using the partial refund feature, subject to these terms:
• Maximum 75% of rental amount can be refunded  
• Must be processed before you end the rental
• Booking fees, tax, and insurance are non-refundable
• If processed after ending rental, $25 processing fee applies

The refund must be authorized and processed by you from the booking details. Support cannot override these limits or fees.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I was charged for tolls after canceling - why? ---
If you see unexpected charges after canceling, check if they're related to toll fees from a completed rental, not the canceled booking. Toll charges appear separately and can be viewed in Past Bookings under the "Tolls" tab for the relevant booking ID.

If you believe the charge is incorrect, provide the booking ID for investigation.

--- [Policy] [cancellation] Q: What happens when renters circumvent the platform after getting owner contact info? ---
When owners share contact information before an accepted booking and encourage off-platform rentals, assess a circumvention fee (typically $60, reduced from full policy amount). The fee applies regardless of whether the rental actually happens.

Circumvention violates Terms of Use and puts both parties at risk by bypassing platform protections. Repeat violations may result in account deactivation.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: When can we make exceptions to cancellation policy? ---
Exceptions may be made for:
• Established owners with good history facing unavoidable circumstances
• Clear owner fault situations (broken trailer, no-show owner)
• Safety/legal issues documented by owner
• Situations where owner contradicts policy causing company losses

Do NOT make exceptions for:
• General inconvenience or change of plans
• Weather (unless extreme circumstances)  
• Financial hardship alone
• Renter equipment issues

Always document reasoning for exceptions and consider owner relationship/history.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How to handle chargeback situations after cancellation? ---
When banks dispute charges and rule in favor of renters:
• Owner payout is reversed per Terms of Use "Chargebacks" policy
• We respond to all disputes but bank policy may override ours
• Owner is not entitled to payout if chargeback is lost
• Company absorbs the chargeback fees

Inform owners that financial institutions have their own policies that sometimes contradict ours, and their policy takes priority.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: How do I cancel a booking? ---
Direct the user to cancel through their account using these exact steps:

From the Web:
• Go to your Dashboard
• Select My Bookings
• Select the 3 dots under "Action"
• Select "Upcoming Booking"
• Select "Cancel Booking"

From the Mobile App:
• Select "Bookings"
• Select "More" at the top-right corner of the upcoming booking
• Select "Cancel Booking"

IMPORTANT: Do NOT process cancellations through phone, text, email, chat, or any other method. Only cancellations completed by the renter through their account will actually cancel the booking.

Note that cancellation fees may apply according to the cancellation policy.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What is the cancellation policy? ---
Explain the refund structure based on timing before rental start:

• 72+ hours before rental start time: 75% refund
• 48–72 hours before rental start time: 50% refund
• 24–48 hours before rental start time: 25% refund
• Less than 24 hours before rental start time: No refund
• Same-day bookings: No refund

Additional rules:
• Platform fees are non-refundable once a booking has been accepted
• A no-show is treated as a renter cancellation without notice and is not eligible for a refund

Refunds are processed within 10 days to the original payment method.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What if I need to cancel due to an emergency? ---
Explain that emergency cancellations may not qualify for a full refund, but rescheduling may be possible with these conditions:

• The trailer owner must be notified through the booking platform at least 24 hours before the original rental start date and time
• The rental may only be rescheduled once
• The new rental date must be within 60 days of the original rental start date
• The trailer owner must agree to the rescheduled date

Direct the user to contact the owner as soon as possible through their booking and reach out to Neighbors Trailer support if additional assistance is needed.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: How can I exchange a booked trailer for a different one? ---
Direct users to the trailer exchange process when they want to switch to another trailer from the same owner without canceling:

From the Website:
• Go to your Dashboard
• Select Bookings
• Choose the booking ID to open the booking details page
• Click Change Trailer
• Complete the exchange process

From the App:
• Select Bookings
• Open the applicable booking
• Tap Change Trailer
• Complete the exchange process

Important details:
• There is no fee to exchange one trailer for another
• If there's a price difference, it's based solely on the rental rate of the new trailer
• Price differences appear as "Transferred Adjustment Amount" on the receipt
• Either the renter or owner can process the exchange

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: When will I get my deposit refund? ---
Explain that the deposit refund is automatically initiated when the trailer owner has ended the rental, provided there were no damages or late fees filed. The refund takes 4-7 business days to appear on their statement.

Also asked as: "How long does it take to refund the deposit?", "When will I receive my deposit refund?"

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: Why does my receipt show $0.00 for deposit refund? ---
Explain that the deposit refund is automatically initiated once the trailer owner has ended the booking and may take 4-7 business days to appear on their statement. The $0.00 on the receipt doesn't mean they won't get the refund - it will be processed separately.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: My booking request wasn't accepted and I want a refund ---
Explain that their payment is only authorized (not actually charged) until a booking is accepted. If they cancel a pending booking or it is rejected by the owner, the hold is immediately released and the money will go back to their card. However, it may take 12-24 hours to reflect on their statement.

Also asked as: "I want my money back because you cancelled my reservation", "The request was not answered, I am waiting for a refund", "The renter rejected the rental, will I get my money back?"

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: The owner said the trailer is broken/unavailable and I need to cancel ---
If the owner says the trailer is broken or unavailable, inform the user that the trailer owner should cancel the booking themselves. If the owner does not cancel by the specified deadline, Neighbors Trailer will reject the booking so the money is refunded.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT tell the renter to cancel themselves in this situation, as they will be charged cancellation fees. The owner should cancel to avoid fees for the renter.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I need to cancel because I don't have the right hitch/connection type ---
Explain that it is the renter's responsibility to ensure they have the correct connection type and ball size to tow the trailer, as this information is provided in the trailer listing description.

For same-day bookings, there is typically no refund unless provided by the trailer owner. Suggest contacting the trailer owner to request a partial refund, as owners can process partial refunds at their discretion.

Also asked as: "Wrong connection for towing", "Can't pickup because truck has no trailer brake controller"

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: The owner never showed up for pickup ---
If the owner failed to show up at the agreed pickup time, this is grounds for a full refund. Cancel the booking and process a full refund immediately. The refund will take 4-7 business days and may appear as two separate refunds. Send the user a receipt.

Note that you will fully review this trailer owner for this behavior.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I need to cancel/rebook due to insurance issues ---
When a booking has insurance problems (wrong driver age, etc.), guide them through the cancel and rebook process:

1. Have the correct account holder cancel the original booking
2. Have the correct account holder book the trailer 
3. Once the trailer owner accepts the new booking, provide the new Booking ID# and Neighbors Trailer can refund the cancellation fees from the original booking

This ensures proper insurance coverage while minimizing financial impact.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I want to return the trailer early and get a partial refund ---
Explain that early return refunds are completely at the owner's discretion. If the owner agrees to refund for an early return, it can only be processed from their account.

The deposit is separate from early return refunds and should still be refunded normally when the owner ends the rental, provided there are no damages.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: I cancelled but was still charged a large fee ---
For cancellations with significant fees, explain the breakdown: The trailer owner receives a portion of the cancellation fee as compensation, and they have the authority to refund part of that amount to the renter at their discretion.

Suggest contacting the owner to ask if they're willing to process a partial refund. If the owner authorizes it, Neighbors Trailer can assist in processing the refund.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How can I cancel a booking without penalty? ---
Direct owners to cancel from the booking details page by selecting "Cancel Booking" and following the prompts.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT select "End Rental" - this is different from cancelling.

Warn that Owner Cancellation Without Cause results in a minimum fee of 30% of the booking rental amount. This includes cancellations due to inaccurate listing details, inadequate maintenance, or failure to meet the customer.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: The renter wants a refund - should I provide one? ---
Explain that providing refunds is entirely at the owner's discretion. Owners can process partial refunds through the "Partial Refund" process in the booking details (up to 75%) or choose to refund their full payout amount.

If they agree to provide a refund, they can specify any amount and Neighbors Trailer will process it to the renter.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Can I refund a renter one day if they returned early? ---
Request the Booking ID number to investigate the specific situation. Owners can process partial refunds for early returns at their discretion through their account.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: I need to cancel due to trailer damage from previous rental ---
If a trailer sustained damage during a previous rental and cannot be repaired before the next booking, you can cancel the upcoming booking. The renter will be fully refunded, and the refund may appear as two separate transactions taking 4-7 business days to process.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: When should we process full refunds outside normal policy? ---
Process full refunds in these situations:
- Owner no-shows or fails to meet renter at agreed time
- Technical issues on Neighbors Trailer's side
- Trailer is actually unavailable/broken but owner accepted booking
- Severe safety issues or misleading listing information

For emergency situations or when renters have legitimate complaints about owner behavior, consider full refunds as customer service gestures.

IMPORTANT: Platform fees can sometimes be refunded in exceptional circumstances, contrary to the standard "non-refundable" policy.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How do we handle cancellation disputes? ---
When renters dispute cancellation fees:

1. Review the specific circumstances (insurance issues, owner problems, etc.)
2. If the owner is willing to refund their portion, process it
3. For technical issues or owner fault, consider full refunds
4. Ask for Booking ID# to investigate specifics
5. Explain the fee breakdown (what goes to owner vs. platform)

Document owner behavior issues for review when they cause cancellations.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: Can I get a full refund for issues with the trailer? ---
If a renter reports trailer safety issues (broken lights, bad tires, missing tags, mechanical problems), gather specific details about the problem and booking ID. Tell them you will need to verify the information with the trailer owner and allow 24-48 hours for resolution.

If the owner agrees the issue was their fault or negligence, this becomes an owner cancellation and the renter may receive a full refund. However, if the issue is deemed the renter's responsibility (like not having proper towing equipment or brake controller), the standard cancellation policy applies.

For safety-related issues that make the trailer unroadworthy, escalate immediately to human support for review.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: The owner didn't show up or wasn't available for pickup - what do I do? ---

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How do I cancel a booking as an owner? ---
Inform the owner that if they cancel a booking after accepting it, 30% of the rental amount will be withheld from their next payout according to the Terms of Use.

To cancel the booking, direct them to:
• Go to the booking page and select "Cancel Booking"

Important policies to explain:
• Owners can cancel multiple bookings, but if they have an unpaid cancellation fee, they must enter payment information and pay the fee
• All trailer owners must accept and complete a minimum of 70% of bookings to maintain active account status
• Refer them to the Booking Cancellation By Owner Policy in the Terms of Use at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: What are the different types of owner cancellations and fees? ---
Explain the two categories:

OWNER CANCELLATIONS FOR CAUSE:
• Only for unavoidable circumstances
• Allowed up to 2 rental cancellations For Cause within a 6-month rolling window without fees
• Subsequent cancellations incur $50 fee if cancelled at least 7 days prior to rental start, or $100 fee if cancelled less than 7 days prior

OWNER CANCELLATIONS WITHOUT CAUSE:
• Include: inaccurate trailer listing details, failure to perform adequate maintenance/inspections making trailer unsafe, failure to meet customer at agreed time/location
• Subject to minimum fee of 30% of booking rental amount
• Company uses reasonable judgment to determine what constitutes reasonable cause
• Fees deducted from future payouts

Any cancellation request after the rental has started will be denied.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Can I give a renter a partial refund for early return? ---
Explain that early return refunds can only be processed if the trailer owner authorizes it. The owner must email service@neighborstrailer.com on the same day the booking is marked complete to authorize the refund.

If the owner has already received their payout, early return refunds cannot be processed. Within approximately 2 weeks, owners will have the ability to process their own refunds directly.

Early return refund policies:
• If booking was at weekly/monthly discounted rate, renter charged based on actual time used at daily rate
• Booking fees, tax, and insurance are non-refundable
• Maximum refundable amount will not exceed 75% of rental period
• 10% refund processing fee ($20 minimum) deducted from refundable amount

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: A renter wants me to give them a full refund - should I? ---
Review the specific circumstances. If the issue was due to owner negligence (trailer not roadworthy, inaccurate listing, owner not present for pickup), this should be processed as an owner cancellation.

If the owner agrees to forfeit their payout to provide a full refund, explain they can do so, but they will be subject to the 30% owner cancellation fee. If they want to ensure the renter gets a completely full refund including fees, they would need to pay the 30% fee to cover the non-refundable booking fees.

If the issue was the renter's fault (improper towing vehicle, lack of brake controller, etc.), the renter should follow standard cancellation procedures and be subject to regular cancellation policies.

Consider full refunds in these scenarios:
• Owner negligence (trailer not roadworthy, safety issues, no-show by owner)
• Inaccurate listing information
• Platform or system errors
• Loyal customer with genuine emergency (use discretion)

IMPORTANT: Do NOT approve exceptions for renter errors like wrong trailer type selected, lack of proper towing vehicle, or change of plans without extenuating circumstances.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: A renter didn't show up for pickup - what should I do? ---
If the renter requested cancellation same-day but didn't complete it through the platform, reach out to the renter with cancellation instructions. If they don't cancel by end of day, the owner can start and end the rental marking it as a no-show. For same-day cancellation attempts, the owner gets full payout regardless.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Can I cancel if the renter doesn't have proper insurance coverage? ---
This would typically be considered an owner cancellation "without cause" since insurance requirements should be clarified before accepting the booking. A 30% cancellation fee would apply unless there are extraordinary circumstances that qualify it as "for cause."

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How should staff handle owner cancellation fee disputes? ---
Apply the terms strictly: 30% fee for cancellations without cause (double booking, maintenance issues that should have been caught, failure to meet renter, inaccurate listings). For cancellations for cause, allow up to 2 free cancellations in 6-month window, then apply $50 (7+ days notice) or $100 (less than 7 days notice) fees. Use reasonable judgment for edge cases and document reasoning.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: When can booking fees be refunded? ---
Booking fees are generally non-refundable once a booking is accepted. Exceptions: Owner double-booking or other owner fault requiring full refund; Admin-rejected bookings due to owner non-responsiveness; Emergency situations where owner forfeits payout. May require manual processing and separate refund transactions.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How to handle partial refund requests from owners? ---
If owner requests to refund a renter but doesn't want to forfeit full payout, explain that standard cancellation policies apply. Owner can only authorize full refund by forfeiting their payout, or the renter receives whatever percentage the cancellation policy allows based on timing.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT allow phone, text, email, or chat cancellations for renters. Only cancellations completed through the renter's account dashboard are valid. Do NOT override cancellation policies without owner authorization to forfeit payout or clear qualifying circumstances for "for cause" cancellation.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: How do I cancel a booking? ---
Direct the user to cancel their booking directly from their account using these exact steps:

From the Web:
• Go to your Dashboard
• Select My Bookings
• Choose Upcoming Bookings
• Select the booking you want to cancel
• Click Cancel Booking

From the Mobile App:
• Tap Bookings
• Select the booking you want to cancel
• Tap Cancel Booking

IMPORTANT: Do NOT accept cancellation requests made by phone, text, email, chat, or any other method. All cancellations must be completed by the renter through their account by selecting "Cancel Booking" on the Booking Details page.

Also asked as: "How to cancel my reservation", "Need to cancel my trailer rental"

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What is the cancellation policy? ---
Provide the exact refund structure based on when they cancel:

• 72+ hours before the rental start time: 75% refund
• 48–72 hours before the rental start time: 50% refund
• 24–48 hours before the rental start time: 25% refund
• Less than 24 hours before the rental start time: No refund
• Same-day bookings: No refund

Important additional details:
• Platform fees are non-refundable once a booking has been accepted
• A no-show is treated as a renter cancellation without notice and is not eligible for a refund
• If a refund is due, it will be processed within 10 days from the date it is approved
• Refunds are issued to the original form of payment used at booking

The cancellation policy is displayed on every listing, prior to booking and also at the time of booking.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What if I need to cancel due to an emergency? ---
Explain that emergency cancellations may not qualify for a full refund, but we'll try to help with rescheduling when possible.

Rescheduling conditions:
• The trailer owner must be notified through the booking platform at least 24 hours before the original rental start date and time
• The rental may only be rescheduled once
• The new rental date must be within 60 days of the original rental start date
• The trailer owner must agree to the rescheduled date

If experiencing an emergency, instruct them to contact the owner as soon as possible through their booking and reach out to Neighbors Trailer support if additional assistance is needed.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How can I cancel a booking as an owner? ---
Inform the owner that if they elect to cancel a booking, they will be charged according to the owner cancellation policy:

OWNER CANCELLATIONS FOR CAUSE:
• Owners are allowed up to 2 rental cancellations For Cause within a 6-month rolling window without fees
• Subsequent cancellations incur a fee of $50 if cancelled at least 7 days prior to rental start, or $100 if cancelled less than 7 days prior

OWNER CANCELLATIONS WITHOUT CAUSE:
• Subject to a minimum fee of 30% of the booking rental amount
• Include but not limited to: inaccurate trailer listing details, failure to perform adequate maintenance or inspections, failure to meet customer at agreed time or location

Additional rules:
• The Company will use reasonable judgment to determine what is reasonable Cause for cancellation
• Fees are deducted from the Trailer Owner's future payout
• Any cancellation request after the rental has been started or sent out will be denied
• Any owner cancellation with intent to rebook at a higher rate is prohibited

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: A renter wants to cancel - how do I help them? ---
Explain that if the renter wishes to cancel their booking, they must do so on their end. Do NOT cancel bookings for renters as an owner.

Provide the renter with these cancellation steps:

From the Web:
• Go to your Dashboard
• My Bookings
• Select the 3 dots under "Action"
• Select "Upcoming Booking"
• Select "Cancel Booking"

From the Mobile App:
• Select "Bookings"
• Select "More" at the top-right corner of the upcoming booking
• Select "Cancel Booking"

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: How can I exchange a booked trailer for a different one? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-exchange-a-trailer-I-have-booked--161 (Renter version)
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-a-renter-exchange-a-trailer--162 (Owner version)

Explain that if a booking has already been accepted and the user wants to switch to a different trailer from the same owner, they can complete a trailer exchange without canceling the booking.

There is no fee to exchange one trailer for another. If there is a price difference, it is based solely on the rental rate of the new trailer.

Exchange steps:

From the Website:
• Go to Dashboard
• Select Bookings
• Choose the booking ID to open the booking details page
• Click Change Trailer
• Complete the exchange process

From the App:
• Select Bookings
• Open the applicable booking
• Tap Change Trailer
• Complete the exchange process

Pricing Adjustments:
If there is a price difference between trailers, the user will see either a refund or an additional charge during the exchange process. The difference will appear on the booking receipt as "Transferred Adjustment Amount."

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: When will I receive my cancellation refund? ---
If a refund is due based on the cancellation policy, it will be processed within 10 days from the date it is approved. Refunds are issued to the original form of payment used at booking.

If the user says their refund was processed but disappeared from their account, explain that refunds may take a few additional days to appear on their statement after being processed. Provide them with the refund receipt for their records.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: What about early return refunds? ---
Explain that early returns are non-refundable unless the Trailer Owner authorizes the refund and provides written consent to Neighbors Trailer.

Early return refund terms:
• Maximum refundable amount will not exceed 75% of the unused rental period
• There is a 10% admin processing fee (minimum $20) deducted from the refund amount
• Early return refunds will not be granted after the Trailer Owner has already received their payout
• Booking fees, insurance fees, deposit processing fee, and other fees are non-refundable for early returns

The renter must reply "I accept" to confirm they want to proceed with the early return refund after being informed of the admin fee.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: The renter didn't show up - what do I do? ---
If you need to request a booking ID to investigate a no-show situation, ask for the Booking ID number so support can look into the details.

Mark the booking as a no-show if the renter fails to appear. A no-show is treated as a renter cancellation without notice and is not eligible for a refund.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: Can I cancel because the renter is sending someone else to pick up the trailer? ---
If the renter is sending a third party to pick up the trailer and you have concerns about insurance coverage, this would likely be considered an owner cancellation "for cause" if the renter failed to add the third party as an authorized driver when requested.

However, if you elect to cancel, you may still be subject to the 30% cancellation fee unless it qualifies as a cancellation "for cause." The Company will use reasonable judgment to determine the classification.

--- [Both] [cancellation] Q: What happens to the deposit when a booking is cancelled? ---
For renter cancellations: The deposit is refunded according to the cancellation policy timeline (within 10 days of approval).

For owner-initiated deposit refunds: If an owner requests a deposit be refunded to the renter, check the booking details to confirm the deposit amount and any withholdings the owner may have requested.

If there are discrepancies between what the customer expects and what was actually refunded, provide them with the booking receipt showing the exact amounts.

--- [Internal] [cancellation] Q: How to handle owner cancellation fee disputes? ---
When an owner wants to cancel and disputes the fee, provide them with the exact terms from the cancellation policy, including the distinction between "for cause" and "without cause" cancellations.

For situations involving trailer damage from previous rentals, inaccurate listing information, or safety concerns, these may qualify as "for cause" cancellations. The Company uses reasonable judgment to make this determination.

Always reference the specific booking ID and clarify whether this would be their first, second, or subsequent cancellation within the 6-month rolling window.


## BOOKING ##

--- [Internal] [booking] Q: How to handle platform circumvention violation notices ---
These are standardized violation notices sent to owners who attempt to book rentals outside the platform. There are two main violation notice formats used by staff:

Format 1 (Friendly tone):
"Greetings, We're reaching out to let you know about a recent interaction that appears to be in violation of the Neighbors Trailer Terms of Use. We kindly ask you to read this notice completely, as it explains the situation and what steps need to be taken.

***Reason for Violation Notice*** It looks like there was an attempt to manage a booking outside of the Neighbors Trailer platform involving [renter name/chat ID].

***What action do I need to take?*** To resolve this, please contact the renter and guide them through the process of creating a booking directly on our platform [within 48 hours when specified].

***What if I can't get the renter to book via the platform?*** Please understand that the consequence for this violation is not dependent on the renter's actions and will still apply.

***What happens if I don't comply?*** If this issue is not resolved, your account may be subject to suspension. At a minimum, there may be a deduction of up to $200 (or 30% of the rent amount) from your next payout, as outlined in our Abuse of Services Policy."

Format 2 (Formal tone):
"The purpose of this email is to notify you that you are in violation of the Neighbors Trailer Terms of Use. Please read this notice in its entirety.

*Reason for Violation Notice:* Circumvention or attempted circumvention of the Neighbors Trailer platform with [renter name].

*What action do I need to take?* You must contact the renter and instruct them to create a booking on the platform.

*What if I can't get the renter to book via the platform?* The violation consequence is not contingent upon the renter and will still be enforced.

*What happens if I don't comply?* If there is no compliance, your account is subject to suspension or at a minimum there will be a deduction of up to $200 (or 30% of the rent amount) from your next payout as stated in our Abuse of Services Policy."

Both formats reference the Terms of Use at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms and specify that violations can only be discussed via email reply, not phone or chat. Some notices include specific deadlines (48 hours) and penalty amounts ($200, $300, or 30% of rent amount).

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I need help with date selection issues or app functionality problems when trying to help customers book ---
When owners report they cannot select dates for customers or the app isn't working properly, provide these troubleshooting steps:

1. Check calendar availability first:
   - Select "More" from bottom menu
   - Select "My Trailers" 
   - Select "More" next to the specific trailer
   - Select "Block Dates" to review blocked dates

2. Try these technical fixes:
   - Close app completely and reopen
   - Log out and log back in
   - Ensure latest app version is installed
   - Try website at neighborstrailer.com instead of app

3. Use "My Reservations" feature as alternative:
   - Select "More" from bottom menu
   - Select "My Reservations"
   - Select "Add Reservation"
   - This allows creating bookings for customers while keeping 100% rental rate

If technical issues persist, escalate to support team for further investigation. Direct owners to Help Center at neighborstrailer.com/help-center for additional assistance.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Owner wants to arrange cash payment or off-platform transactions ---
Direct the owner that cash payments are NOT permitted on Neighbors Trailer. Explain that all payments must go through the platform to ensure both owner and renter are fully protected under:
- Deposit protection
- NT Protect Protection Package

Recommend the "My Reservations" feature as the solution:
- Owner can send booking invitation directly through platform
- Renter creates free account and completes ID verification through CLEAR
- Renter pays through platform with card
- Both parties receive full platform protection

Direct to Help Center for My Reservations details: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-is-My-Reservations-149

IMPORTANT: Do NOT allow cash transactions as they violate platform terms and remove protections for both parties.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: My booking is stuck in "pending" status and I need to pick up soon ---
Explain that "pending" means the owner has not yet accepted the booking. Key points:
- No set timeframe for owner acceptance
- Payment is only authorized (held), not charged while pending
- Renter can cancel pending bookings anytime with no penalty
- If owner accepts, renter receives confirmation notification

For urgent situations:
- Most owners respond quickly, typically within 2 hours
- After 2 hours, support team reaches out to owners
- Recommend messaging owner through platform to speed up process
- If no response and pickup time has passed, booking may be cancelled with full refund

Assure renter that if booking is cancelled or rejected, the hold is immediately released and funds return within 24 hours.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How to handle toll charges from completed rentals ---
For toll charges incurred during rentals, owners can request reimbursement by replying to support emails with the toll bill. Support will attempt to charge the renter on owner's behalf.

IMPORTANT: Before submitting toll bills, owners should enroll in the free toll program to prevent future toll bills:

Toll Program Enrollment Steps:
1. Login to Neighbors Trailer account (app or web)
2. Go to dashboard
3. Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" 
4. Select "Click Here" (web) or "Tap Here" (app)
5. Select "Enroll Now"
6. Select "Add License Plate"
7. Select "Enroll"

The toll program is completely free with no subscription costs and automates toll collection from renters for future bookings.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How to modify booking dates ---
To change booking dates, renters can submit date change requests:

From Website:
- Sign in and go to Dashboard
- Select "My Bookings"
- Locate the booking
- Click three dots (•••) under Action column
- Select "Change Date Request"
- Enter new dates and submit

From Mobile App:
- Open app and select "Bookings"
- Find the booking
- Tap More (•••) button in top-right corner
- Select "Request Change Date"
- Enter new dates and submit

IMPORTANT: The total number of rental days must remain the same (e.g., 2-day rental can only be changed to another 2-day period). Owner must accept the request for changes to take effect.

If having technical issues, try logging out/in or using different browser/device.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: How to exchange or change to a different trailer ---
If booking is already accepted and renter wants a different trailer from the same owner:

Trailer Exchange Process (Renter only):
1. Select "Dashboard"
2. Select "My Bookings" (web) or "Bookings" (app)
3. Select booking ID number
4. Select "Change Trailer"
5. Complete booking process

Price differences will show as refunds or additional charges during exchange process.

If the desired trailer is from a different owner, the booking must be cancelled and rebooked with the correct trailer.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Booking shows "validating" status and won't let me start rental ---
If booking is stuck in "validating" status, this typically resolves automatically. Check if status has updated to "On Rent" before escalating.

If technical issues persist with starting rentals:
- Try refreshing the app/website
- Log out and log back in
- Check for app updates
- Try accessing from different device

If owner confirms renter is present and ready for pickup but cannot start rental due to technical issues, escalate to support for backend processing. Recommend taking before/after photos to upload when system allows.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Renter is late or not responding for pickup ---
If renter is significantly late or not responding:
1. First check for any pending date change requests on the booking
2. Check platform messages for any communication from renter
3. If no communication and renter is very late, owner can reject the booking

For no-shows or non-responsive renters, owners are within rights to reject bookings when renters fail to show up at scheduled times.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Owner not responding to booking request and pickup time is approaching ---
If owner is not responding to booking requests:
- Support team contacts owners after 2 hours of no response
- Support continues trying to reach owner until they respond
- Send message through platform to potentially speed up process

For same-day bookings where pickup time has passed:
- If owner cannot be reached, booking will be rejected
- Full refund issued automatically
- Refund appears within 24 hours

Encourage rebooking with different available trailer if urgent.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How to handle extension refunds when renter doesn't use approved extension ---
If owner sent extension request, renter approved it, but renter didn't actually need the extra time:

Owner should provide the exact refund amount for the renter. This amount will be:
- Deducted from owner's next payout
- Returned to renter within 4-7 business days

Support needs the specific dollar amount to process the refund correctly.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Issues with date change requests or booking modifications ---
If date change was approved but system shows different dates or reverts:
- System cannot update bookings to past dates
- If renter had trailer on earlier date than booking shows, run Deposit Deduction Claim for extra days after trailer return
- Date changes must maintain same number of rental days

For technical issues with date changes:
- Try logging out/in
- Update app to latest version
- Try website instead of app
- Contact support if problems persist

IMPORTANT: Date changes cannot be backdated. If renter took trailer early, handle through deposit deduction after return.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Missing payout for completed booking ---
If owner reports missing payout for completed booking:
1. First check if bank account is properly linked:
   - Navigate to Neighbors Trailer account
   - Select "Bank Account"
   - Link bank account if not already done
   - Payouts automatically initiate once account is linked
   - Funds reflect in 1-3 business days

2. If bank account is linked but payout missing, this may indicate technical error with automatic payout initiation. Support can re-submit payout manually, which takes 1-3 business days.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: Account deactivated for non-compliance with booking responses ---
When owner accounts are deactivated for not responding to bookings:

Standard deactivation notice explains:
- Owners must accept, reject, or message renter within 12 hours of booking placement
- Must maintain 70% acceptance rate
- Platform provides tools to prevent unwanted bookings:
  * Active/inactive toggle removes listing from search
  * Block dates calendar prevents booking on specific dates

To reactivate: Owner must reply to deactivation email requesting reactivation. Support will assist with reactivation process.

If owner reports app issues preventing response, this can be considered during reactivation review.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Requesting same trailer from previous rental ---
For returning renters wanting to book same trailer:
1. Check rental history in account to find previous booking
2. Use previous booking to locate the same listing
3. Search for available trailers in same area for desired dates

If trailer is still listed and available, renter can book directly through platform.

Direct to login and check rental history first, then search platform if needed.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: Booking general information for first-time users ---
For first-time users asking about availability and booking process:

To check availability and book:
1. Go to specific trailer listing page
2. Select desired rental dates from calendar
3. Choose pickup time
4. Click "Book Now" to start booking process

Requirements during booking:
- Complete all required fields
- Complete ID verification through CLEAR
- Enter payment information
- Card is authorized but NOT charged until owner accepts

After booking submission:
- Owner receives booking request
- Renter can message owner through listing page
- Upon acceptance, renter receives owner contact info and pickup address
- If rejected, no charge and hold is released

For questions about what's included (straps, equipment), message owner directly through listing page before booking.
