--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I received a payout deduction - what is it for and how was it calculated? ---
When an owner asks about a payout deduction, check if it's related to circumvention/abuse of services. Explain that circumvention deductions are applied when owners attempt to take bookings off-platform by sharing contact information or arranging meetings before an accepted booking. The deduction amount is typically reduced from the full penalty stated in the Abuse of Services Policy (up to $200 or 30% of rental amount). Direct them to read the full Abuse of Services policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms. The deduction is not contingent on whether the rental actually happened - it's based on the attempt to circumvent.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: A renter left an unfair or retaliatory review - can it be removed? ---
If an owner reports an unfair or retaliatory review, investigate the booking details and conversation history. If the review is deemed unfair, retaliatory, or inaccurate based on the actual booking circumstances (like a no-show situation), remove the review so it will no longer be visible on the owner's profile. Confirm the removal to the owner.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: My booking is still pending and I need it confirmed soon - can you contact the owner? ---
For pending bookings where renters need quick confirmation, notify the trailer owner of the pending request. Explain that you cannot guarantee the owner will accommodate last-minute bookings, but you have reached out on their behalf. Remind the renter that their payment is only authorized (not charged) while pending, and they can cancel at any time with no penalty if they need to make other arrangements.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Has my renter paid for the booking? When do I get paid? ---
When a renter submits a booking request, they have successfully authorized the funds. The payment is processed once you accept the booking. For confirmed bookings, explain the payout timing and process according to your payment schedule.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: How do I request or approve a rental extension? ---
Direct users to the extension request process: 1. Go to Dashboard > My Bookings (web) or Bookings (app), 2. Select "Current" tab for on-rent bookings, 3. Click the booking ID to get to booking details, 4. Select "Extension Request", 5. Enter additional days and remarks, 6. Select "Send Request" and complete payment. If the renter requests it, the owner can accept/reject. If the owner requests it, the renter can accept/dispute. Both parties can submit unlimited extension requests.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I can't approve a booking request - it keeps showing as pending even after I accept it ---
If an owner reports technical issues with accepting bookings (says "accepted" but reverts to "pending"), ask them to confirm whether they can see a "Begin Rental" button. If the issue persists, request a screenshot to investigate potential glitches. Try troubleshooting steps like signing out/in or switching between app and website.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Why don't I see tax amounts collected on my booking details? ---
Explain that tax amounts are only visible to the renter, not the owner. Neighbors Trailer takes responsibility for collecting sales tax when required, so owners don't need to track or report these amounts separately.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I contact the owner about a pending booking? ---
Direct renters to use the "Send Message" button on the trailer listing page to contact owners about pending bookings. Remind them that sharing contact information prior to an accepted booking is prohibited.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: How do I change the dates on an existing booking? ---
For accepted bookings, use the "Date Change Request" feature: Go to Bookings, select the booking, locate "Date Change Request" button, enter new dates. The new dates must match the original number of days (e.g., 3-day booking must change to another 3-day period). For additional days, submit both a date change request and an extension request. For time changes within the same date (AM to PM), this also uses the date change process.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I'm trying to book for multiple days but it only lets me select one day ---
Explain the booking calendar process: Select the first date (pickup date) and the last date (return date) of the rental period. Don't select the dates in between - selecting the first and last dates automatically creates the rental window for the entire period.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Why is my booking showing "Payment Error" status? ---
When a booking shows "Payment Error" status, it means the renter's payment information was not charged successfully and the booking request didn't go through fully. These bookings cannot be accepted or rejected since they weren't fully submitted due to the payment error. The renter would need to attempt to rebook with valid payment information.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I can't close out a rental because there's a pending extension request ---
Ask the owner if the renter has officially returned the trailer. If not, notify the renter to accept the pending extension request. The rental cannot be closed while extension requests are pending approval.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: The renter says they accepted my offer but it still shows pending on my side ---
Review the system to verify if the pending offer has actually been accepted by the renter. If no acceptance is found, ask the renter to attempt the acceptance again or contact support for assistance with the technical issue.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I need confirmation about my booking status ---
Check the booking status in the system. If the owner has accepted the request, inform the renter that they can message the owner using the "Send Message" button on the listing page or in the booking details for pickup information and coordination.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I have a pending booking request but need to reject it because I'm not available ---
If an owner needs to reject a booking due to unavailability, process the rejection. The renter will receive a full refund (funds were only authorized, not charged). Inform the renter that their refund should appear within 24 hours.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: How do I cancel a booking? ---
From Web: Go to Dashboard > My Bookings > Select 3 dots under "Action" > "Upcoming Booking" > "Cancel Booking". From Mobile App: Select "Bookings" > "More" at top-right corner > "Cancel Booking". Remind users of any applicable cancellation policies and timing.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I haven't received my payout for completed bookings ---
Check the specific booking IDs and payout status. Common explanations: 1) Payouts don't process on weekends/holidays - funds may be delayed, 2) "Success" status means funds have been sent to their connected Stripe account, not that it's in their bank yet, 3) Bank holidays can cause delays of 2-3 business days, 4) Some "error" statuses are actually just holiday-related delays, not true errors.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Are there vehicle requirements or restrictions for towing? ---
Direct renters to contact the trailer owner directly for information about towing requirements and restrictions using the "Send Message" button on the trailer listing. Each owner may have different requirements based on their specific trailer.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: I need to report excessive mileage charges ---
For owners reporting mileage overages, require proof of mileage before processing charges to the renter. Explain that a 5% admin fee will be deducted from the amount charged to the renter to cover transaction fees. For renters disputing charges, investigate the documentation provided.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: My listing is pending approval and I'm losing potential rentals ---
Check why the listing is pending. Common reasons include: 1) Photos showing company contact information (prohibited - will be edited by moderation team, allow 90 minutes), 2) Recent changes requiring manual review, 3) VIN discrepancies or other listing details needing verification. Provide specific feedback on what needs to be corrected.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: A renter received a traffic violation while using my trailer - what do I do? ---
Escalate traffic violation issues to appropriate team for handling. These involve liability and legal considerations that require case-by-case review and specialized handling procedures.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I need to browse available trailers in my area ---
Direct them to enter their city and state in the search bar on the homepage at https://neighborstrailer.com. Once they find a suitable trailer, they can book instantly online or message the owner using "Send Message" for more information. Remind them that trailers must be picked up and returned at the same location.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I add discounts or coupons to a pending booking? ---
Explain that all coupons or discounts must be applied at the time of booking and cannot be added to pending bookings. To apply a discount, the booking needs to be cancelled and rebooked while applying the coupon at checkout.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: My account is blocked due to alleged circumvention - how do I resolve this? ---
For circumvention violations, the owner must review and acknowledge the Abuse of Services section of the Terms of Use. They need to respond via email stating they understand and agree to abide by these terms. Explain that circumvention includes sharing contact information, arranging meetings, or using contact information shared by renters prior to accepted bookings. If renters have booking issues, owners should direct them to the help center or customer service, not provide alternative contact methods.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Does Neighbors Trailer have API integration capabilities? ---
Currently there are no API integration capabilities, but plans exist to introduce this in the future. As an alternative, recommend the "My Reservations" feature for bringing external leads onto the platform. Direct them to resources at Bing Videos and https://neighborstrailer.com/blog/neighbors-trailer-launches-my-reservations-the-ultimate-free-trailer-rental-software. Explain that My Reservations allows creating reservations for external renters with a 10% booking fee ($20 minimum) plus 3% deposit processing fee.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I handle an overdue rental when the renter isn't responding? ---
Provide the escalation steps: 1) Contact renter through NT message portal asking when trailer will be returned, 2) If no response, text the renter (get phone number from support if needed), 3) Give a specific deadline through messages/calls with consequences stated, 4) If missed, send written termination notice with short deadline (1 hour) before contacting police, 5) Contact police to report stolen if final deadline missed. Important: Once reported stolen, stop charging rental fees as it becomes a criminal matter. Laws vary by jurisdiction - some may require specific notice periods.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: Where can I buy promotional materials or stickers? ---
Direct users to the Neighbors Trailer shop at https://resources.neighborstrailer.com/shop/ for available promotional materials and merchandise.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Why doesn't my booking show insurance coverage? ---
Insurance coverage depends on renter eligibility. If a booking shows as "not insured," it's typically because the renter doesn't meet the minimum age requirement of 25 years old. All trailers with insurance available require coverage, but renters must qualify for the insurance program.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I get confirmation that my trailer is enrolled in the toll program? ---
Check the owner's account settings and confirm toll program enrollment status. Provide verification of enrollment when requested.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: I'm having technical issues with date change or extension approvals ---
For technical glitches with approvals, suggest troubleshooting steps: 1) Sign out and sign back in, 2) Switch between app and website platforms, 3) If issues persist, provide screenshots for further investigation. Some approval problems may be due to platform glitches rather than user error.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: The owner returned my trailer early but I still need to return it officially ---
If an owner isn't present during scheduled return and the renter needs to leave the trailer, notify the owner of the situation. Explain that you cannot authorize when trailers can be returned - this must be coordinated between renter and owner. The renter can use their discretion but should continue attempting to reach the owner for proper return confirmation.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How long should I wait for a booking response? What if it's urgent? ---
Most owners respond quickly to pending requests. If no response within 2 hours, the support team reaches out and continues trying to contact them until they respond. Recommend sending a message through the platform to speed up the process. Payment is only authorized (not charged) until acceptance, and pending bookings can be cancelled anytime with immediate hold release (though it may take up to 24 hours to reflect on statements).

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I find my booking after I've made a reservation? ---
Direct the user to go to the "Bookings" tab within the main menu options, then ensure they check the "upcoming" bookings tab to locate their booking.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I change the dates of my booking? ---
Instruct the user to go to "Bookings" and select the booking they wish to adjust, then locate the "Date Change Request" button and enter the new dates. IMPORTANT: The adjusted rental dates must match the number of days that were originally placed (e.g., if original booking was 3 days, new dates must also be 3 days). If they want to add more days, they need to submit an extension request in addition to or instead of the date change request.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I rejected a booking but want to accept it instead. Can this be reversed? ---
Inform the owner that once a booking is rejected, it cannot be reversed. The renter will need to submit another booking request for the owner to accept it.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: My booking was rejected. What should I do? ---
Explain that if their booking request was rejected, it may be due to the owner being unable to accommodate their request. Suggest they message the trailer owner by selecting "Send Message" on the trailer listing page for more information, or they can attempt to book a different trailer.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I book a trailer? ---
Direct them to enter their city and state into the search bar on the homepage at https://neighborstrailer.com. Once they find a trailer, they can book instantly online by entering pickup dates and time, then following the booking process. Alternatively, they can message the trailer owner directly by clicking the "Send Message" button on the listing page. Remind them that sharing contact information prior to an accepted booking is prohibited.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I accept a booking request that's been created for a renter? ---
NOTE: There are two booking flows. Normal flow: renter requests a booking, owner accepts or rejects. Reverse flow (owner-initiated): owner creates a reservation for a specific renter, renter confirms via email notification. Both are valid. If a user describes the reverse flow, do not correct them — it is a supported feature.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I need to change my booking dates but already submitted one date change request. Can I submit another? ---
Inform them that only one date change request can be submitted per booking. If they do not wish to continue with the current dates, they would need to re-book. If they wish to proceed with rebooking, support can cancel their current booking and refund the entire booking except the booking fees.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I have a pending booking and the owner hasn't responded. What should I do? ---
Inform them that support will notify the trailer owner regarding their request. If the trailer owner does not respond within 1-2 hours, they may need to seek alternatives. Assure them that cancelling a pending booking will result in a full refund and the hold on their card will be released (may take 12-24 hours to reflect on their statement).

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Can I change the driver information on my booking? ---
Explain that driver information is associated with the Neighbors Trailer account that books the trailer. They will need to cancel and have the actual driver create an account and book. Once they have cancelled and successfully rebooked with the driver's account, support can fully refund them for the original booking.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I handle damage claims or deductions from a rental? ---
When an owner reports damage, support will process deductions and provide payout information including trace ID and deposit details. Deductions may be combined with other payouts. Support can provide screenshots for reference.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I'm looking for a specific type of trailer in my area. How do I find availability? ---
Direct them to browse trailers by entering their city and state into the search bar on https://neighborstrailer.com. They can book instantly online or message trailer owners using the "Send Message" button on listing pages. Remind them that trailers must be picked up and dropped off at the same location.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I handle toll bills from rentals? ---
First, instruct them to enroll in the free toll program if they haven't already:
1. Login to Neighbors Trailer account and go to dashboard
2. Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" and select "Click Here" (web) or "Tap Here" (app)  
3. Select "Enroll Now"
4. Select "Add License Plate"
5. Select "Enroll"
Once enrolled, support will handle the toll bill. For future rentals, the toll program automates the process and collects fees from renters.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Why can't I book dates that show as available? The dates appear crossed out. ---
Explain that crossed out dates are in the past and cannot be booked. They need to select current or future dates only.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I change a booking to a different trailer for the same renter? ---
Inform the owner that the renter must switch trailers from their side of the system. Provide these instructions to send to the renter:
1. Select "Dashboard"
2. Select "My Bookings" (web) or "Bookings" (app)
3. Select the booking ID number to get to booking details page
4. Select "Change Trailer"  
5. Complete the booking process
If there's a price difference, it will show as "Transferred Adjustment Amount" on the receipt.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I need to offer a different trailer because the booked one isn't available. How do I handle this? ---
Support can help facilitate the rental quickly. If the owner can get the new trailer's information and create a listing, support can expedite the approval process. The owner may need to put "placeholder" information initially to secure the booking, then correct the listing information once they have the actual trailer.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I need to contact support about my booking but want a phone call. ---
Inform them that for documentation purposes and to provide the best assistance, all support must be handled by email. Ask what specific issue they need help with.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: A renter wants to contact me about an unresponsive pending booking. What should I do? ---
Support will notify the trailer owner regarding pending booking requests. If owners don't respond, support may remove them for negligence. Payment is only authorized (not charged) until booking acceptance, so canceling a pending booking releases the hold immediately.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I block out dates on my calendar? ---
Instruct them to use the app:
1. Click "More" button on bottom main menu
2. Select "My Trailers"
3. Select the small "More" button on the trailer they want to block dates for
4. Click "Block Dates"
5. Select dates to block from booking calendar
6. Click "Save"

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I have a double booking situation due to incorrect dates. How can I contact the second renter? ---
Ask for the booking number and confirm if they need contact information to resolve the scheduling conflict.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I submitted a booking but haven't heard from the owner. How long does response usually take? ---
Support will send a text message to the trailer owner to notify them of the pending booking. There's no set timeframe but owners should respond as quickly as possible.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I have an error when trying to accept an add-on request. How do I fix this? ---
Suggest troubleshooting steps:
1. Try signing out and back in
2. Try using the app instead of website or vice versa  
3. Ensure stable internet connection and app is up to date

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: A renter reported problems with my trailer during the rental. What are my options? ---
Support will ask for details about when the renter contacted the owner (what date) and request screenshots of the messages to review the situation.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: A renter wants to cancel an extension they requested errantly. Can I reject it? ---
If the extension has already been accepted, it cannot be rejected. However, the owner can provide a partial refund to the renter using the "Provide partial refund" option.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I want to rent a trailer for one-way transport. Is this possible? ---
Inform them that trailers must be picked up and dropped off at the same location. One-way rentals are not supported.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I need to cancel a booking after accepting it. What are the consequences? ---
Inform them that canceling after acceptance results in 30% of the rental amount being withheld from their next payout per the Terms and Conditions. Reference the Booking Cancellation By Owner Policy on the Terms of Use page at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms. Owners must maintain a 70% completion rate to keep active account status.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I returned a trailer early. How do I get a refund for unused days? ---
The owner needs to initiate a partial refund. Support will ask the owner how much they want to refund, then process it. Refunds take 4-7 business days and appear separately from deposit refunds.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I sync my calendar with other rental platforms to avoid double bookings? ---
Inform them that Neighbors Trailer is not partnered with other trailer websites and there's no way for calendars to sync. They must manually block trailer dates if listing on multiple platforms.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I accidentally hit accept when I meant to reject a booking. How do I cancel it? ---
Explain the cancellation policy: 30% of rental amount will be withheld from next payout. To cancel, go to booking page and select "Cancel Booking". If there's an unpaid cancellation, they'll need to enter payment information. All owners must maintain 70% completion rate. Reference full Booking Cancellation By Owner Policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: I'm having trouble with the website when trying to book a trailer. ---
Ask for specific details: Are they receiving error messages? Where exactly are they having trouble on the website? Need more information to assist properly.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I received a toll bill for a previous booking. How do I get reimbursed? ---
For owners enrolled in toll program: Support will handle reimbursement. For new toll bills, support charges the toll amount plus $30 admin fee to the renter's account and notifies them. 

For owners not enrolled: Direct them to enroll first, then support will assist with the toll bill.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: My pending booking is taking too long and I need the trailer urgently. ---
Support will contact the owner. If no response within reasonable time, advise the renter to cancel and book an alternative trailer. Pending bookings can be canceled with no penalty and funds are released immediately (12-24 hours to show on statement).

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I update my email address to accept pending booking requests? ---
Support can update email addresses in the system. Ask them to confirm which email address they want associated with their account if there have been multiple change requests.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Where can I see my bookings and their status? ---
Direct the user to go to "Bookings" and click on the "Upcoming" tab at the top of the screen to see their booking information.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: What happens with address verification issues during booking? ---
If a user reports address issues during the booking process (such as old address showing up instead of new address), first verify what address is showing in their account on your end. If the address appears correct in the system but the user is seeing something different, ask them to provide a screenshot of the screen showing the incorrect address. For verification issues where someone has moved but doesn't have an updated license yet, the user must contact support directly - owners cannot handle address verification issues on behalf of renters.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I adjust the rental amount after a booking is accepted due to incorrect pricing? ---
If an owner needs to adjust the rental amount after booking acceptance (such as discovering they listed the wrong trailer size), they cannot change the amount during the active booking. The owner must wait until the booking is completed, then immediately contact support by email on the day the rental is completed. Support can process a manual refund to the renter to adjust the final amount charged. The owner should reach out the same day they complete the rental to process this request.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I get the pickup address and owner contact information? ---
Once the trailer owner has accepted the booking, they will provide their address and phone number automatically. If the booking is still pending or if the renter needs additional information, they can message the owner using the "Send Message" button on the listing page.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I block out dates to make my trailer unavailable? ---
Direct the owner to the app: click the "More" button on the bottom main menu, then select "My Trailers". From there, select the small "More" button on the trailer they want to block dates for and click "Block Dates". They can then select which dates to block from the booking calendar and click "Save".

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I search for and inquire about specific trailer types? ---
Direct the user to browse trailers by entering their city and state into the search bar on the homepage at https://neighborstrailer.com. Once they find a suitable trailer, they can either book instantly online or message the trailer owner directly using the "send message" button on the listing page for more information. Remind them that the trailer must be picked up and dropped off at the same location.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How can I get reimbursed for additional costs incurred due to renter issues? ---
If a renter causes issues that result in additional costs to the owner (such as requiring the owner to drive to retrieve a trailer due to legal violations), support can attempt to charge the renter for fuel and time. Note that this is limited by the deposit amount. Have the owner specify exactly how much they want to charge the renter, keeping in mind the deposit limit.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: What if there are booking discrepancies or missing bookings in the dashboard? ---
If a user sees bookings counted in their dashboard but cannot find the actual booking details, first check if there are any pending bookings or booking requests on the backend. If no bookings are found on the system side, the booking request likely did not go through properly. Advise the user to attempt to book the trailer again and report any error messages they receive.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I handle toll charges incurred by renters? ---
If a renter incurs tolls during the rental period, the owner can provide the toll bill to support, and support will charge the renter on their behalf and process a payout to the owner. The owner should email the toll bill to support. For ongoing toll management, direct owners to the automated toll program enrollment: "Toll Transfer Program Enrollment by Neighbors Trailer" link. This program automates the entire toll process and is completely free with no subscription cost.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: What happens if my booking is still pending close to the rental start time? ---
Explain that bookings require owner acceptance and there is no set timeframe for this. For same-day bookings, advise that Neighbors Trailer recommends booking at least 24 hours in advance to give both parties time to communicate and to allow for alternatives if needed. If the owner is unresponsive for a same-day booking, the renter may need to cancel the pending booking and seek alternatives. Remind them that pending bookings can be cancelled with full refund as long as they haven't been accepted.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: What if the owner isn't responding and I need the trailer soon? ---
If an owner is unresponsive, especially for time-sensitive rentals, and the booking hasn't been accepted yet, the renter should consider cancelling the pending booking to seek alternatives. Remind them that as long as the booking hasn't been accepted, they can cancel with full refund and the hold on their card will be released (appearing in 12-24 hours).

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: What happens if I complete a rental but the booking shows as rejected? ---
If an owner completed a rental successfully but the booking shows as rejected, this is typically due to non-compliance with rental procedures. Owners must begin the rental from their account when the renter receives the trailer and end it from their account when the rental period ends. Failing to start and end rentals properly can lead to rejected bookings. Support will still issue a payout for completed rentals, but it won't show in the Neighbors Trailer account. If there's any renter dispute due to the rejected booking, the owner may forfeit their payout. Direct the owner to read the "Owner Rental Procedures" and "Non-Compliance of Owner Rental Procedures" in the Terms of Use at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms and the "Rental Process" in their account Library.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I use "My Reservations" for renters who originally came through the platform? ---
No. The "My Reservations" system is designed for creating bookings for renters that owners bring from outside sources (like their own company advertising). While owners can use "My Reservations" for returning renters that were originally brought by Neighbors Trailer, they cannot reject a platform booking and then use "My Reservations" for the same first-time renter. This violates the commission structure since Neighbors Trailer depends on the 20% commission to provide services and generate leads. If this occurs, a commission fee will be deducted from the owner's payout.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How do I handle early returns and partial refunds? ---
For early returns, owners should complete the booking normally (start and end the rental as usual). After closing out the booking, contact support immediately. Support can provide the renter with a 75% refund of the unused amount, with a 10% administration fee (minimum $20). The owner must close out the booking first, then notify support to process the partial refund.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: Can I change my booking dates multiple times? ---
Booking date changes can only be made once. If a renter needs to make a second date change, they must cancel their current booking and re-book for their preferred dates. After they make these changes and contact support, support will provide a full refund excluding the booking fees.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I cancel a renter's booking at no cost to them to accommodate another booking? ---
Yes, but you need to provide the specific booking ID to support for processing. Support can cancel the existing booking at no cost to the original renter to allow them to rebook for different dates.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How far in advance can I book a trailer and when is payment due? ---
There is no limit to how far in advance you can book a trailer - even close to a year out is possible. However, the entire cost of the rental including rent amount, deposit, taxes, and fees are due at the time of booking, not at pickup.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: What should I do if a trailer is reported stolen during a rental? ---
For stolen trailer situations, the owner should submit a deposit deduction claim (DDC) once the trailer is returned. When ending the rental, select the "Deposit Deduction Claim" box at the bottom and upload images displaying any damages. If damages exceed the deposit amount, include estimated damages in the claim notes. The renter has 24 hours to respond before the claim is approved. If damages exceed $500, the owner can file an insurance claim (if the booking included insurance coverage) using the Neighbors Trailer claims form. Required documentation includes: pictures of damages, pictures of all 4 sides of the entire trailer, picture of the VIN sticker, and repair estimates. Direct them to the insurance claim form link when ready to file.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: How do I switch between renter and owner account types? ---
Support can switch account types upon request. If switching to an owner account, the user will need to download the separate "Neighbors Trailer- Owner" app and sign in with their existing login credentials. The regular app is for renters only.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: I have questions about my first booking - what should I do? ---
Encourage new owners to reach out with their specific questions. Support is available to walk through any concerns about their first booking experience.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How do I check trailer availability for specific dates? ---
When attempting to book a trailer, check the calendar on the trailer listing. Any crossed-out dates show when the trailer is not available. Users can also message the trailer owner directly using the "Send Message" button on the listing for more information about availability. Remind them that sharing contact information prior to an accepted booking is prohibited.

--- [Both] [booking] Q: What happens when someone reports a trailer or there are legal issues during rental? ---
For situations involving police reports or legal complications during a rental, support needs the booking ID to properly assist. These situations require case-by-case handling and immediate support intervention.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: When will my refund be processed after cancelling a booking? ---
For pending bookings that are cancelled: The hold is immediately released and money returns to the card, but may take 12-24 hours to reflect on the statement. For accepted bookings that are cancelled: It takes 3-5 business days for funds to be processed and returned to the account.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: How long does listing approval take? ---
Listings are approved as soon as possible, typically within 4-6 business hours. However, depending on the number of listings in queue, it may take 1-2 business days. If owners make edits and resubmit in the future, the listing will be approved much quicker. If there's an urgent situation requiring immediate approval, owners should contact support.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: When and how do I receive payment for completed rentals? ---
For standard completed rentals, payment is automatically processed. If there are questions about a specific payout, provide the booking ID. Support can verify when payments were initiated, which bank account they were sent to, and provide trace IDs if needed for the owner to check with their bank. Payments typically arrive within 1-2 business days via Stripe processing.


## LISTING ##

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I use marketing materials with the Neighbors Trailer logo to promote my listing? ---
When a trailer owner asks about using Neighbors Trailer branding or logos for marketing materials (flyers, bumper stickers, etc.), explain that they should contact customer service to discuss specific marketing material requests. Do not provide a definitive yes or no answer - direct them to reach out for approval and guidance on what promotional materials are permitted.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why doesn't my rental pricing match what the renter was charged? ---
When an owner questions why the booking amount differs from their expected calculation, explain that the amount shown represents what the renter was actually charged based on the listing's pricing structure. The discrepancy may occur due to:
• Weekly or monthly rates being applied instead of daily rates
• Platform pricing algorithms that differ from simple daily rate multiplication
• Other pricing factors applied through the platform

To review or update pricing structure:
From the app: Select More → My Trailers → More (on the listing) → Update Rate
From the website: Dashboard → Trailer → Trailer List → click the 3 dots → Update Rate

Direct them to these steps if they want to adjust their rates for future bookings. Updated rates take effect immediately after submission.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why does my listing need at least 4 photos? ---
When an owner's listing is pending due to insufficient photos, explain that Neighbors Trailer requires a minimum of 4 high-quality photos of the trailer from multiple angles. If they currently have fewer than 4 photos uploaded, they must add additional photos before the listing can be approved. The listing will remain in pending status until this requirement is met.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How long does listing approval take and can it be expedited? ---
Explain that listing approval typically takes 1-2 business hours during normal business hours, but may take 1-2 business days depending on the queue volume. If an owner requests expedited approval, staff can manually approve listings that are complete and meet requirements. When asked about expediting, check if their situation is urgent and approve if appropriate.

For faster approval in the future, ensure listings have:
• Complete information in all required fields
• At least 4 high-quality photos
• Correct 17-character VIN
• Full address in Location field
• No contact information visible in photos
• Completed profile and ID verification

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I list my trailer if it has business logos or contact information visible? ---
Yes, trailer businesses can absolutely list on the platform. If trailers have phone numbers, company logos, or business information visible, the review team will blur or edit this information rather than rejecting the listing entirely. The listing can still be approved with these edits made during the review process.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT tell owners they cannot list business trailers. The correct answer is that they can list them and the review team will handle removing visible contact information.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I switch from a renter account to an owner account? ---
To switch account types, the user must first complete all required fields in their profile. Once the profile is complete, they should contact customer service to request the account switch. 

After switching:
• They must download the correct "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app (not the renter app)
• Sign in with their existing login credentials
• The switch will reset current account information and may remove existing data

Alternative: If they want both account types, they must use separate email addresses - one email cannot be used for both owner and renter accounts.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I can't find my listing when I search the platform ---
Direct them to check their listing status first:

From the Owner App:
• Select More → My Trailers
• View the status shown with light green or red highlight

From the Web:
• Go to Dashboard → Trailer → Trailer List
• View the status shown with light green or red highlight

Status definitions:
• Approved - Listing is live and can receive bookings
• Pending - Under manual review, should be approved soon
• Draft - Not submitted for review yet
• Rejected - Did not meet minimum requirements

If they can't find their trailers in search results for weeks, ask for the Trailer ID number to investigate further.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Someone says they booked my trailer but I don't see it on my end ---
Check for pending or submitted bookings under their account. If no booking is found, explain that the renter may not have fully submitted the booking request. Direct the renter to contact customer service directly for assistance if they're experiencing issues completing the booking.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My calendar shows dates as unavailable when they should be available ---
This typically occurs when there's a pending booking request covering those dates. To make the dates available for a different renter, the owner must first deny/reject the pending booking request from the original renter. Only then will the dates become available for new bookings.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I get my listing approved after making updates? ---
After making any changes to a listing (description, photos, add-ons, etc.), the listing must be resubmitted for review. Simply notify customer service that updates have been made and request approval. Listings with updates are typically approved quickly once reviewed.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why isn't my listing visible in Google search results? ---
New listings can take several weeks to be indexed by Google and other search engines. This timeline is not controlled by Neighbors Trailer. Rankings vary based on location, competition, and search history.

To help find their listing:
• Search using key phrases from the listing title
• Search using title phrases plus city and state
• Not all listings will appear on the first page of results

If the listing doesn't appear after a reasonable indexing period, they can contact customer service for review.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My listing won't submit - what should I check? ---
Common reasons a listing won't submit:
• Description needs at least 200 characters (character counter turns from red to green when minimum is met)
• Missing required fields
• Fewer than 4 photos uploaded

Direct them to verify all these requirements are met before attempting to submit again.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I research competitive pricing in my area? ---
Direct them to go to the NeighborsTrailer.com homepage and search for trailers in their area to review pricing from similar listings. This allows them to see what other trailer owners are charging and set competitive rates accordingly.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can businesses list trailers on the platform? ---
Absolutely - businesses are welcome and encouraged to list on the platform. Business partners are seen as key to growing reliable inventory. Whether they have a few trailers or a large fleet, they can list on the platform to access renters and generate additional revenue from their inventory.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I set up my account after switching from renter to owner? ---
After the account switch is completed:
1. Download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app (not the renter app)
2. Sign in with existing login credentials
3. Complete the trailer listing process
4. Fill out all required fields and upload at least 4 high-quality images
5. Submit for review
6. Connect bank account to receive payouts
7. Complete ID verification

The commission structure is 20% of each rental, and listing is completely free.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why is my trailer title being changed during review? ---
For best visibility in Google search results, trailer dimensions and type must appear at the beginning of the title. If promotional text (like discounts) is placed before the trailer specifications, the review team will reorder the title to put dimensions and type first.

For example: "50% Off Monthly Rate" would be changed to "5' x 8' Enclosed Trailer (50% Off Monthly Rate)"

If dimensions and type are removed from titles again, the listing will be rejected for not meeting guidelines.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I'm having issues enrolling in the toll program ---
If they receive an error when trying to enroll, check if their trailer is already enrolled in the toll program. The error may appear because they were automatically enrolled before the self-enrollment option was released. Confirm their enrollment status and explain that the error message will be updated to show they're already enrolled.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I set up bank account information to receive payouts? ---
Direct owners to add their banking information through their account settings. Once the bank account is connected, payouts will be processed within 2-3 business days after rentals are completed. Bank account setup is required before any payouts can be issued.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I updated my listing but it's been pending for a week ---
Ask for the Trailer ID number to investigate the specific listing. Normal approval time is 1-2 business hours during business hours, so a week-long delay indicates an issue that requires individual attention.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What are the requirements for listing my trailer? ---
To list a trailer:
• Download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app
• Complete all required listing fields
• Upload minimum of 4 high-quality images
• Enter correct 17-character VIN
• Provide full address in Location field
• Complete profile and ID verification
• Connect bank account for payouts

Listing is free, with a 20% commission on rentals. The platform provides advertising, toll management, claim management, and protection coverage.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How can I get assistance beyond email support? ---
For documentation purposes, customer service assistance is only available through email or live chat. Phone consultations are not provided - all support must be handled through written communication channels.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My account appears inactive after deleting the renter app ---
If they deleted a renter account and tried to create an owner account, reactivate their account and switch it to owner type. They must then download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app and sign in with their existing credentials.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I need to withhold deposit for damages - how do I claim it after the rental? ---
Explain that when the rental is properly ended in the system, they'll have the option to submit a deposit deduction claim. For claims exceeding $500, they may also be eligible for NT Protect coverage. Direct them to the existing KB entry "How Do I Get Paid for Loss or Damages?" for complete procedures.

For amounts above the deposit, they need to provide invoices/receipts for repair costs and inform the renter through the message portal on the platform.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Which of my trailers has a VIN issue? ---
When an owner asks about VIN issues without specifying which trailer, ask them to provide the specific Trailer ID number so you can identify which listing has the VIN discrepancy. Once identified, request a clear photo of the VIN on the trailer or the trailer's registration to verify the correct VIN.

--- [Renter] [listing] Q: The owner offered me an alternative trailer - how do I book it? ---
Direct renters to message the trailer owner directly through the platform to discuss alternative options. They can also browse similar listings and book directly through the platform. Provide the "Send Message" option on listing pages or within booking details to facilitate communication.

--- [Both] [listing] Q: How do I ask specific questions about a trailer's features? ---
Direct users to message the trailer owner directly for specific information about trailer features, equipment, or specifications. Use the "Send Message" button on the listing page to contact the owner directly. This ensures accurate, up-to-date information about the specific trailer.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I handle a rental that was started incorrectly due to technical issues? ---
If a rental experienced technical issues during the start process but the booking was valid and payment was processed, the owner should complete the required platform steps: mark the booking "On Rent" when picked up and "End Rental" when returned. If they missed taking initial photos, they can upload any photo to start the rental if the trailer is still with the renter. Return photos are strongly encouraged when ending the rental.

IMPORTANT: All rentals must be properly managed through the platform to ensure protection coverage and proper documentation.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: A renter wants to modify dates after the rental has started ---
Ask for the Booking ID number to review the specific situation. If equipment issues caused the need for rescheduling and the rental was already marked as started, customer service will need to review the circumstances and provide guidance on how to handle the date modification.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I have a VIN that's already in the system from a previous account ---
If a trailer was transferred between business accounts and the VIN already exists in the system, customer service can adjust the original listing to allow the trailer to be listed under the new account. Provide details about the ownership transfer and the accounts involved.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I access the rental contract that renters agree to? ---
Renters do not manually sign a contract, but a digital contract is automatically generated when the booking is accepted. This rental contract can be found under "Documents" in the Booking Details section of each booking.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I convert my renter account to an owner account? ---
Also asked as: "How can I rent my trailer on your site?", "How do I change my account to a renter account?", "I downloaded the owners app to list my trailer, but it won't let me register"

Tell the user that Owner and Renter accounts are separate account types that cannot use the same email address. If they want to convert their existing renter account to an owner account, they need to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com and request the conversion.

Important: Converting an account will reset current account information - any existing data may be removed during the transition.

After conversion, direct them to download the correct Owner app:
- "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" (not the Renter app)
- iOS: https://apps.apple.com/us/app/neighbors-trailer-owner/id1667847016
- Android: https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.neighbourstrailerowner

If they want to operate as both owner and renter, recommend creating a second account with a different email address rather than converting the existing account.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How long does listing approval take? ---
Also asked as: "When will my trailer be approved?", "Why is my trailer approval still pending?", "How long will it take to go live?"

Tell the user that listings are typically approved within 4-6 business hours, but may take 1-2 business days depending on the review queue. Reviews are conducted during normal business hours only.

If they have an urgent situation requiring immediate approval (such as a customer waiting to book), they can contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com to request expedited review.

Note: If they make edits and resubmit in the future, subsequent approvals will be much quicker.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why won't my listing submit for review? ---
Also asked as: "New listing won't submit", "I can't seem to submit my listing for review"

Tell the user to check these requirements:
- Listing description must contain at least 200 characters (character counter turns from red to green when minimum is met)
- All required fields must be completed
- At least 4 high-quality photos must be uploaded
- Complete address must be entered in Location field
- Correct 17-character VIN must be entered
- Weight capacity should list load weight only (not trailer's total weight)
- Profile and ID verification must be completed

If all requirements are met but submission still fails, suggest these troubleshooting steps:
1. Sign out and sign back in
2. Try switching between website and mobile app
3. Contact support if issues persist

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I'm getting a "VIN already exists" error when listing my trailer ---
Tell the user this means the VIN is already in the system, possibly from a previous listing. Direct them to:
1. Save their trailer as a draft
2. Take a photo of the VIN plate on their trailer
3. Contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com with the photo and the Trailer ID number from their draft

Support will investigate and resolve the VIN conflict.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My VIN is only 10 digits long and won't be accepted ---
Tell the user that older or specialty trailers may have shorter VINs. Ask them to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com with their VIN and whether their trailer is restored, salvaged, or has special status. Support can manually process listings with non-standard VIN lengths.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why can't I see my listing when I search for it? ---
Also asked as: "When I search for my trailer it doesn't show up", "Is my trailer active?"

First, direct them to check their listing status:

From Owner App:
- Select More > Trailers
- Look for green (approved) or red (pending/rejected) highlighting

From Website:
- Go to Dashboard > Trailers > Trailer List
- Check status: Approved (live), Pending (under review), Draft (not submitted), or Rejected

If status is Approved but they still can't find it in search, explain that search results vary based on location, competition, and filtering. Their listing is live and available to renters even if it doesn't appear in their specific search.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Only some of my trailers are showing as listed ---
Tell the user this typically means the missing trailers have "Pending" status and are under review. Once approved, all trailers will be visible. Direct them to check status using the steps above.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What does "clean title" mean when listing my trailer? ---
Explain that clean title means:
- No liens (no lenders or financial institutions with legal claim)
- Not reported as stolen
- No salvage, rebuilt, or junk branding
- Straightforward ownership history with no major insurance incidents

If their trailer meets these requirements and doesn't fit other status categories, they should select "clean title."

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I expedite approval for an urgent listing? ---
Also asked as: "I have a customer waiting to book", "Can you push this through ASAP?"

Tell the user to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com explaining the urgent nature of their request. Support can expedite approval for time-sensitive situations where customers are waiting to book.

Important: If expedited with minimal photos, they must update the listing with at least 4 high-quality photos after the booking to maintain active status.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I add videos to my listing? ---
Tell the user that video uploads are not currently supported on the platform. They can only upload photos. This feedback has been submitted for future consideration.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Does Neighbors Trailer provide QR codes or promotional materials for my trailer? ---
Also asked as: "Will you send me a QR code for my trailer?", "Do I get promotional materials?"

Tell the user that QR codes and promotional materials are not automatically provided. However, they can create their own promotional materials using their public listing URL, which can be found by:

Website:
- Search for their trailer on NeighborsTrailer.com
- Copy the URL from the listing page
- Or use Dashboard > Trailer > Trailer List > select trailer > use share icon

Mobile App:
- More > My Trailers > select listing > tap share icon

They can create their own QR codes linking to this URL for display on their trailers.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I'm getting error messages when trying to activate my trailer ---
Tell the user to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com with:
- Their Trailer Listing ID number
- The exact error message they're receiving

Support needs these details to diagnose and resolve the specific activation issue.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I enroll my trailer in toll automation after receiving a toll bill? ---
Tell the user to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com with:
- Photo/copy of the toll bill received
- The booking ID associated with the rental period
- Confirmation that they've now enrolled in the toll program

Support will handle toll bills that occurred before enrollment in the program.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I'm having trouble enrolling in the toll program ---
Also asked as: "Getting an error when enrolling in toll automation", "Toll enrollment shows pending"

Tell the user to:
1. Enter license plate number without spaces or dashes
2. Ensure they have the correct Trailer Listing ID

If still experiencing issues, have them contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com with:
- Trailer Listing ID number
- License plate number
- Screenshot of any error messages

--- [Internal] [listing] Q: How should support handle toll bills received before toll program enrollment? ---
When owners contact support about toll bills received for rentals that occurred before they enrolled in the toll automation program, forward the toll bill information and booking ID to the appropriate team for processing. The toll program should cover bills for rentals even if enrollment happened after the fact.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I handle late pickup by renters? ---
Also asked as: "What if customer is late to pickup?", "When is trailer due back if pickup is late?"

Explain that rental periods are based on the originally agreed dates and times, not actual pickup time. If pickup is delayed, the return is still due at the original end time unless an extension is processed.

For late returns, direct them to:
1. Contact renter through NT message portal asking for return timeline
2. If no response, text the renter (support can provide phone number)
3. Set a deadline: "Your rental was due back at [date/time]. I will give you until [time] today to contact me or I will escalate the matter."
4. If deadline passes, send final notice with 1-hour deadline before contacting authorities

Always process extension requests before the original end time if the trailer won't be returned on schedule.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What do I do if my trailer isn't returned on time? ---
Also asked as: "Renter is late returning trailer", "What are the steps for theft?"

Tell the owner not to panic - this is usually due to forgetfulness or irresponsibility, not theft. Direct them to follow the escalation process:

1. Message renter through NT platform asking when trailer will be returned
2. If no response, text the renter (support can provide phone number if needed)
3. Send written deadline: "Your rental was due at [date/time]. Contact me by [deadline] or I will escalate this matter."
4. If no contact by deadline, send final notice with short deadline (1 hour) before involving authorities
5. Contact support for assistance with serious cases

Document all communication attempts through the platform.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I collect sales tax on my rentals? ---
Tell the user that Neighbors Trailer automatically handles sales tax collection on applicable bookings. They don't need to collect or remit sales tax themselves - this responsibility is handled by the platform.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My listing is pending review but I have a customer waiting to book ---
Tell the user to contact support at service@neighborstrailer.com immediately, explaining that they have a customer waiting and need urgent approval. Include any relevant booking details or customer information.

Support can expedite approval for time-sensitive situations where customers are actively trying to book.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I share my business documents with renters? ---
Tell the user they can request the renter's email address to share business documents ONLY after the booking has been accepted. Sharing contact information or business details before booking acceptance is strictly prohibited and violates platform terms.

Once booking is accepted, they can ask the renter for their email to share additional contracts or business documents.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I create My Reservations for off-platform rentals? ---
Direct the user to the "My Reservations" feature mentioned in existing KB entry about logos and company names. Explain that My Reservations allows them to process rentals with their own contracts while keeping 100% of rental fees, while still providing renters with insurance, ID verification, credit card processing, and claims management.

This is recommended over cash rentals which are extremely high risk.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I list a trailer without a VIN number? ---
If the trailer is a manufactured trailer but the VIN is less than 17 characters, ask if the trailer is manufactured or homemade. If it's manufactured and has a short VIN, instruct the owner to enter a fake VIN that is 17 characters long and change the title status to "Salvage".

If the trailer is homemade but titled, inform the owner they can list it but it will not be eligible for Protection Package coverage. All trailers must be registered, titled, and equipped with a license plate to be listed.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My listing won't submit due to VIN requirements ---
Also asked as: "VIN has to be 17 characters long but my VIN is only 7 characters"

Check if the trailer is manufactured or homemade. For manufactured trailers with short VINs, instruct the owner to enter a fake VIN that is 17 characters long and change the title status to "Salvage". This is a workaround for older trailers that didn't have standardized 17-character VINs.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My trailer has business logos/contact information visible - can I still list it? ---
Inform the owner they can still list their trailer. Neighbors Trailer will photoshop out business logos, company names, phone numbers, and other contact information from photos during the review process if they are present. The owner does not need to remove these themselves.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How long does listing approval take? ---
Also asked as: "My listing says pending", "How long until my listing is active"

Inform the owner that listings are typically approved within 4-6 business hours, but depending on the queue, it may take 1-2 business days. Listings are reviewed during normal business hours only. If they make edits and resubmit in the future, approval will be much quicker. Ask if there's an urgent situation requiring faster approval.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My listing submission is stuck on the city/location field ---
Instruct the owner to save their listing as a draft and contact support for manual review. This appears to be a technical issue that requires staff intervention.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I have both a renter and owner account? ---
Yes, but they must use separate email addresses. An owner account and renter account cannot share the same email address. If they plan to operate as both, recommend creating a second account with a different email rather than converting their existing account.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I convert my renter account to an owner account? ---
Contact support to request the account type change. Warn the owner that changing account type will reset current account information and any listings, profile details, or data associated with the existing account may be removed during the transition. If using the app, they'll need to download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app after conversion.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I update the deposit amount for my trailer? ---
To update the deposit amount, the owner needs to update their trailer listing:

On the web:
1. Go to "Trailers" and then "My Listings"
2. Select the 3-dots icon next to the trailer you want to update
3. Select "Update Listing"
4. Make your changes and select "Submit for Review"

On the App:
1. Select "More" at the bottom app menu
2. Select "My Trailers"
3. Select "More" next to the trailer you wish to update and select "Update Listing"
4. Make your changes and select "Submit for Review"

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I list trailers in multiple locations? ---
Yes, owners can list trailers in separate locations. Simply adjust the "Location" field in each trailer listing to accurately reflect where that specific trailer is located.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I handle a repeat customer who wants to rent outside the platform? ---
Encourage the renter to book the trailer through the platform. If the renter contacts you outside the platform, you can use the "My Reservations" feature to create a reservation for them. All rentals should stay on the platform to maintain protection and proper documentation.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What is Neighbors Trailer's commission rate? ---
Neighbors Trailer takes 20% of each rental. This means they only make money when the owner makes money. Listings are free and unlimited.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Does Neighbors Trailer provide a rental contract for renters to sign? ---
No, Neighbors Trailer does not send renters a rental contract. Instead, renters agree to the Terms of Use before booking, which covers many situations and helps protect the renter, trailer owner, and company. If an owner wants renters to sign an additional rental agreement, they can have them sign the form provided in the Owner Library.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I enroll my trailer in the toll program? ---
Provide these steps:
1. Login to your Neighbors Trailer account on the app or web and go to your dashboard
2. Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" and select "Click Here" (web) or "Tap Here" (app)
3. Select "Enroll Now"
4. Select "Add License Plate"
5. Select "Enroll"

If they receive an error message, ask if they enrolled in the older toll program. If not, suggest:
1. Sign out and sign back in
2. Try the opposite platform (if using website, try mobile app and vice versa)
3. Ensure the app is up-to-date

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I handle contactless pickup when I'm not available? ---
Warn the owner that while some may participate in contactless pickup, if the trailer is damaged, not being present at pickup can result in Deposit Deduction Claims or insurance claims being denied. Neighbors Trailer will never advise or encourage contactless pickup due to complications that can occur. If they must do contactless pickup, they can ask the renter to send photos before taking the trailer.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Can I update photos without going through review again? ---
No, when updating a trailer listing (including photos), it needs to be manually reviewed by the team before being accepted. There is no way to update listings without having them reviewed.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My trailer was supposed to be returned but the renter is not responding - what do I do? ---
Also asked as: "My trailer is overdue", "Late return and can't contact renter"

Provide these steps:
1. Try to submit an extension request from within the booking details first
2. If extension doesn't work, try to contact the renter through the Neighbors Trailer message portal asking when they will return the trailer
3. If no response, try texting the renter (contact support for their phone number if needed)
4. If still no response, contact them again through NT message portal and phone/text giving a deadline such as: "Your rental was due back at [date/time]. I have reached out many times and have not heard back from you. I will give you until [time] today to contact me or I will have to escalate the matter and terminate the rental."
5. If the renter doesn't contact you by your deadline, reach out in writing again telling them you are terminating the rental and give them a short deadline (maybe 1 hour) to contact you or you will escalate further

Contact support if the situation continues to escalate.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I remove/deactivate my listing? ---
Explain that they can deactivate or archive, but this should be done with caution as listings build organic search rankings over time. If only temporarily unavailable, recommend blocking dates instead.

To deactivate (hide):
Mobile App: Select More > My Trailers > Toggle the Visibility switch off
Web: Go to Dashboard > Trailer > Trailer List > Toggle the Visibility switch off

To archive completely:
Mobile App: Go to My Trailers > Select More on the listing > Select Archive Trailer
Web: Go to Trailer List > Click Action (3 dots) > Select Archive Trailer

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What taxes do I need to handle for trailer rentals? ---
Inform the owner that they do not need to pay state sales tax for bookings via Neighbors Trailer. The system will automatically charge renters for sales tax and Neighbors Trailer pays it to the state. The owner does not need to worry about sales tax.

For income tax, recommend checking state laws. If gross payments exceed $20,000 and more than 200 transactions per year, Neighbors Trailer will send a 1099-K form. Direct them to the IRS website for more information about Form 1099-K.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Where can I view the customer rental agreement? ---
Direct the owner to view the Terms of Use at: https://neighborstrailer.com/terms

Explain that renters agree to these terms instead of signing a separate rental contract. If they want renters to sign an additional agreement, they can use the rental contract form provided in the Owner Library.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I can't complete my listing submission due to license plate error ---
Ask the owner to provide an image of their license plate. This allows support to manually update the listing with the correct information and approve it.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What information should I provide about listing my trailer for rental? ---
Direct inquirers to the standard owner benefits information:

1. Free Listings - Create unlimited trailer listings with editorial review. Set your own prices, deposit, and requirements. 20% commission only when you make money.
2. Free Advertising and Promotion - Marketing team uses search engines, social media, trade shows, events, and more for exposure.
3. Free Tools to Manage Bookings - Communication, booking management, photo uploads, deposit refunds, owner payouts, and more.
4. Resources - Owner Library contains rental contract, guides, maintenance guides, forms, FAQs.
5. Free Credit Card Processing and secure payments.

--- [Renter] [listing] Q: I'm looking to purchase trailers - do you sell them? ---
Explain that Neighbors Trailer does not purchase or own trailers, so they would not be interested in buying or selling trailers. Direct them to browse available rental listings by entering their city and state in the search bar on the homepage.

--- [Renter] [listing] Q: I need help finding specific trailer types in my area ---
