Once they find a suitable trailer, they can book instantly online or message the trailer owner using the "Send Message" button on the listing page for more information. Note that trailers must be picked up and dropped off at the same location.

--- [Both] [listing] Q: I'm trying to respond to a message from a trailer owner/renter ---
Direct them to respond through the platform by either:
1. Selecting "Send Message" on the trailer listing page
2. Going to "Messages" in their Neighbors Trailer account
3. If they have a booking, going to the booking details and selecting "Send Message"

Do not respond via email to platform notifications.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I upload photos when marking a trailer as out on rent? ---
When an owner reports they cannot upload photos to mark a trailer as "out", direct them to try again. If the photo upload functionality continues to fail, escalate to human support as this appears to be a technical issue that requires investigation.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Why haven't I received payment for a completed rental? ---
First check if the owner has set up their bank account information for payouts. Direct them to go to Account Settings and set up their bank account details. Once the bank account is configured, inform them that the payout process can be initiated. If bank details are already set up and payment is still missing after a reasonable time, escalate to human support for investigation.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I get a copy of the signed rental contract? ---
Ask the owner to provide the Booking ID number, then escalate to human support to retrieve the signed rental contract. The contracts are not directly accessible to owners through the portal.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I changed my prices but the listing hasn't updated ---
Check if their listing is still in draft mode. If the listing is in draft, instruct them to submit the listing for review first before price changes will take effect. If the listing is already approved and prices still haven't updated, escalate to human support.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How long does it take for a new listing to be approved? ---
Inform the user that listings are manually reviewed and typically approved within 4-6 hours during business hours. However, depending on the review queue, approval can sometimes take 1-2 business days. If they have an urgent situation requiring faster approval, they should contact support. Future edits and resubmissions are typically approved much faster than initial submissions.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How do I switch from a renter account to an owner account? ---
This requires human support intervention. Escalate to support and they will switch the account type from renter to owner. Important: Inform the user that after the switch, they must download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app (not the renter app) and sign in with their existing credentials. The account conversion may reset some account information.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Do you provide 1099 tax forms for rental income? ---
Inform the owner that Stripe (the third-party payment processor) automatically provides 1099 forms if they reach the required revenue threshold. The 1099 will be sent automatically by Stripe if the threshold is met. Neighbors Trailer itself does not issue 1099s.

--- [Internal] [listing] Q: Owner feedback about slow photo uploads and listing approval times ---
Log the feedback about slow photo upload performance and lengthy listing approval times as areas for internal review and improvement. Standard response is to acknowledge the feedback and inform them it will be submitted to the internal team for review, while explaining current approval times (4-6 hours typical, up to 1-2 days depending on queue).

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: Getting "Invalid VIN" error when trying to submit listing ---
Ask the owner to provide the VIN they're trying to enter so human support can investigate the specific issue. Even if they've double-checked against their title, there may be a system issue preventing submission.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My trailer has a non-standard VIN that's not 17 characters ---
Ask the owner to clarify whether their trailer was homemade or purchased from a dealer, as this affects how VIN issues are handled. Escalate to human support for trailers with DMV-issued replacement VINs or non-standard VIN formats.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: My listing is still pending after making requested corrections ---
Check if the listing title or description still indicates hauling services rather than regular rental. Listings cannot be approved if they primarily advertise hauling services like "You load, We haul." These services can be offered as add-ons, but the owner must also be willing to offer regular self-service rentals. If the listing has been corrected and still shows pending, escalate to human support.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How long will my listing stay in pending status? ---
Also asked as: "How long will my listing pend for?"
Inform the user that the approval process for new listings typically takes 24-48 hours. If it's been longer than this timeframe, they should contact support for an update.


## GENERAL ##

--- [Renter] [general] Q: How do I find and book a trailer for specific needs? ---
Direct users to browse trailers by entering their city and state in the Location search field on neighborstrailer.com homepage and clicking Search. Once they find a suitable trailer, they can book instantly online or message the trailer owner using the "Send Message" button on the listing page for more information.

For specific trailer requirements (motorcycle transport, car haulers, dump trailers, equipment trailers, etc.), advise users to review listing details for size, weight capacity, pricing, and pickup location. Users can message owners directly to ask about specific features like wheel chocks, tie-downs, or other specialized equipment before booking.

Also asked as: "Looking for a stock trailer", "Need to rent a car hauler", "Looking for a 14 foot dump trailer", "I need to rent a trailer for tomorrow"

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Can I see or inspect a trailer before booking? ---
Inform users that for privacy and safety reasons, Neighbors Trailer does not allow in-person meetings with trailer owners before a booking is confirmed. If they want more details before booking, they can message the trailer owner to request additional photos or measurement information.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Where do I pick up the trailer? When will I get the address? ---
Explain that after the trailer owner accepts the booking, the pick-up address will be shared automatically. In most cases, it appears in the message portal and on the booking details page. If the owner has auto-share turned off and the address doesn't appear after acceptance, instruct the user to send a message requesting the pick-up location.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Do you offer delivery or one-way rentals? ---
Inform users that Neighbors Trailer does not currently offer one-way rentals. All trailers must be returned to the original pick-up location unless otherwise specified in the trailer listing description. The trailer must be picked up and dropped off at the same location.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Do you offer discounts or military discounts? ---
Explain that rental rates are set by individual trailer owners on the platform. Neighbors Trailer does not provide first rental discounts or military discounts. Any discounts are provided at the trailer owner's discretion. Recommend that users message the trailer owner directly by selecting "Send Message" on the listing page to ask if any discounts are currently available.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: What should I do if I'm having trouble with driver's license verification? ---
If users report license verification issues (like "driver license is blocked" or verification loops), provide these troubleshooting steps:
1. Try signing out and signing back in
2. Ensure the app is up to date
3. Try using the website instead of the app or vice versa

If the issue persists, ask for clarification about whether this is an error during the Identity Verification process and escalate to human support for further investigation.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Can someone else pick up or return the trailer for me? ---
For Protection Package coverage to apply, the individual picking up and operating the trailer must be the renter named on the booking. If someone other than the named renter picks up or operates the trailer, Protection Package coverage may not apply.

The driver must:
• Be listed on the booking
• Complete required ID verification  
• Meet all renter eligibility requirements

If someone else needs to be the driver, they would need to create their own account and complete the booking process themselves, including ID verification.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: How do I get help or contact customer service? ---
Direct users to these support options, recommending Live Chat or the Contact Form for fastest response:

Live Chat: Access by selecting the chat icon in the bottom-right corner of any page on NeighborsTrailer.com or the Dashboard within the mobile app.

Contact Form: Submit a message at Contact Us | Neighbors Trailer

Phone number is available upon request through Live Chat or contact form.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: What's the complete booking process step-by-step? ---
Provide the complete booking process:
1. Visit neighborstrailer.com and enter your city and state in the Location search field, then select Search
2. Browse available trailers and choose one that fits your needs
3. Select your desired rental dates and pick-up time, then select Rent
4. Complete the required fields and confirm your email address or phone number
5. Upload a photo of your driver's license for identity verification
6. Enter your payment details and select Pay (you won't be charged until the trailer owner accepts your booking)
7. You'll be notified by text and email once the booking is accepted
8. If the trailer is returned without incident, your deposit refund will be initiated and typically appears on your statement within 3–5 business days

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I switch from a renter account to an owner account? ---
Inform users that they cannot use the same email address for both renter and owner accounts. Offer to switch their existing renter account to an owner account. After switching, note that if they're using the app, they'll need to download the owner app named "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" and sign in with their existing credentials.

Also asked as: "I created a renter account but want to be an owner", "I made an account and meant to make it as an owner account"

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I list my trailer for rent? ---
For users who created renter accounts instead of owner accounts, switch their account type to owner and provide these instructions:

Listing is completely free (Neighbors Trailer takes 20% commission per rental). Download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app and register with email, Facebook, or Google. Complete the trailer listing process with all fields filled out and upload 4 high-quality images. Select "Submit for Review" to submit for approval. Connect a bank account for payouts and complete ID verification.

Recommend watching: How To List A Trailer On Neighbors Trailer (YouTube video)

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Is there an age limit for trailers I can list? ---
Inform users that there is no age requirement for trailers listed on the site.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I handle toll bills from rentals? ---
Before submitting toll bills for assistance, ensure all trailers are enrolled in the Neighbors Trailer Toll Program (enrollment is required for toll recovery assistance).

To submit a toll bill, email a copy of every page to service@neighborstrailer.com including:
• The booking ID
• The rental dates  
• A copy of the toll invoice

Neighbors Trailer will attempt to collect toll charges from the renter. If payment is successfully collected, the owner receives a payout for the toll amount. Note that successful collection cannot be guaranteed.

Recommend enrolling in the free toll program to reduce future toll bills:
1. Login to account and go to dashboard
2. Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" 
3. Select "Enroll Now"
4. Select "Add License Plate"
5. Select "Enroll"

Also asked as: "I have tolls from previous rentals", "I received toll notices from a renter"

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I expedite my trailer listing approval? ---
If an owner needs urgent approval (same day/next morning), escalate to human support. Note in staff replies that expedited approvals can be processed outside normal business hours when needed.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Can I update return times during an active rental? ---
Explain that pickup/dropoff times cannot be changed within booking details once the booking has begun. If charging for extra time due to late return, submit a Deposit Deduction Claim when ending the rental. If not charging for late return, end the rental normally when the trailer is returned.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Where do completed rentals appear after ending them? ---
Explain that once the End Rental process is completed, the booking moves from active bookings to completed rentals history and will no longer appear in active bookings.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I get additional Neighbors Trailer stickers? ---

2. Look for the "Shop" tab in the main menu
3. Place order for additional stickers

--- [Both] [general] Q: What are 1099 tax forms and when will I receive one? ---
Explain that tax requirements vary by state. If gross payments exceed $20,000 AND more than 200 transactions are completed in a calendar year, Neighbors Trailer will issue a Form 1099-K via email.

For more details, refer to: Understanding Your Form 1099-K | Internal Revenue Service (IRS)

To check if they met the threshold, users can run a Booking Report on their account. Reference: Help Center | How Do I Run A Booking History Report?

Also asked as: "Where can I find my 1099k?"

--- [Both] [general] Q: How does sales tax work on rentals? ---
Explain that Neighbors Trailer complies with applicable state and local tax laws and collects and remits sales tax where required (such as Illinois when marketplace tax thresholds are met). Sales tax is automatically collected on qualifying bookings and remitted to appropriate tax authorities.

For more details about marketplace tax collection, refer to Stripe's documentation:
- Tax for marketplaces | Stripe Documentation
- Monitor your obligations | Stripe Documentation

Note that tax requirements vary by state and may change over time. For specific tax obligations, recommend consulting a qualified tax professional as Neighbors Trailer does not provide tax advice.

For users needing to convert JPG files to PDF format for bank document upload, direct them to: JPG to PDF – Convert JPG Images to PDF Documents Online (jpg2pdf.com)

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Can I have both a renter and owner account? ---

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Can rental businesses use the Neighbors Trailer platform? ---
Confirm that many trailer businesses use the platform for rentals. There are no restrictions preventing rental businesses from listing multiple trailers on the platform.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do payouts work for long-term rentals? ---
If an owner wants to receive payouts before a long-term rental ends (e.g., 4+ months), advise them to request that the renter book month-to-month instead of one long booking. This allows the owner to receive payouts at the end of each monthly booking period rather than waiting for the entire rental to complete.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How long do payouts take to process? ---
Inform the user that payouts can take 1-3 business days depending on their bank and are completely out of Neighbors Trailer's control. If a payout is initiated before a weekend, it may take longer since banks are closed on weekends.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Why does my trailer show as "non-insured"? ---
If a trailer shows as non-insured, check if the trailer value exceeds $25,000. The NT Protect coverage has a maximum limit of $25,000. If the trailer value is above this limit, the owner needs to reduce the listed value to $25,000 or below to qualify for coverage.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I update my trailer's license plate number? ---
Request the trailer listing ID and the new license plate number. Support can update this information directly in the system. This is important for toll program enrollment and proper billing.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: Why was my trailer listing rejected for photo quality? ---
Listings require original, high-quality photos of the specific trailer. Screenshots, website images, or photos with borders are not accepted as they appear blurry and have reduced image quality. The listing needs 4+ original, high-quality photos of the actual trailer to be approved.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: What should I do if accessories are missing after a rental? ---
Unfortunately, deposit deduction claims must be submitted at the time of ending the rental. If accessories are discovered missing after the rental has been ended, recommend contacting the renter directly to inquire about retrieving the missing items or reimbursement.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How can I contact my renter during a booking? ---
Direct them to select "Send Message" in the booking details section of their booking, either through the app or website dashboard under "My Bookings."

--- [Both] [general] Q: What information do I need for support requests? ---
For booking-related issues, always request the Booking ID number. For listing issues, request the Trailer Listing ID number. For account issues, request the email address associated with the account. This allows support to quickly locate and assist with the specific issue.

--- [Internal] [general] Q: How should I handle incomplete support requests? ---

--- [Renter] [general] Q: Can I get a partial refund for early return? ---
Explain the partial refund policy: 1) Partial refunds require trailer owner authorization and can only be processed before the owner ends the rental, 2) Booking fees, tax, and insurance are non-refundable, 3) Maximum refund is 75% of rent amount, 4) A $25 processing fee applies to manual refunds processed after the owner ends the rental. Direct them to the Refunds Policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms.

They would not be able to complete a booking without this verification. Suggest they could ask someone else with a valid ID and camera access to create an account and handle the rental on their behalf.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How often will my trailer be rented? Can you estimate rental frequency? ---

1. Create standout listings with great photos, comprehensive descriptions that answer common questions, and consider offering add-ons and delivery
2. Build reviews by initially dropping rental rates for first few rentals to establish trust
3. Post listing links on social media to increase traffic and visibility in search results
4. Create coupons (found in owner app: More > Coupons > Create Coupon) and share codes on social media or military discount sites
5. Use "My Reservations" feature for off-platform rentals to maintain protection while keeping 100% of rental rate

## PROFILE ##

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How can I change my email address or no longer have access to my old email? ---
Ask the user for their current account information including name, phone number, and old email address if known. Search for accounts using the provided information. If multiple accounts are found with different emails, ask the user to clarify which account they want to update and which email address they want it changed to. Once confirmed, escalate to human support to make the email change. The support team can update email addresses manually.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I convert my renter account to an owner account? ---
Also asked as: "How do I change my account from a renter to owner?", "How do I switch my account type to owner?", "Can you change my account from renter to owner?"

Inform the user that you can convert their renter account to an owner account. First, ask them to ensure their profile is fully completed. Once confirmed, escalate to human support with the message "User requests renter to owner account conversion. Please switch account type and remind them to download the white 'Neighbors Trailer - Owner' app." 

Important: After conversion, the user must download the correct app - the white "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app (not the renter app). Their login credentials remain the same.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: Can I have both a renter and owner account? ---
No, you cannot use the same email address for both account types. Each email can only be used once on the platform. If the user wants both types of accounts, they must use a separate email address for each account type and download the appropriate app for each:
- Renter app: "Neighbors Trailer - Renter" 
- Owner app: "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" (white app)

Alternatively, offer to convert their existing account from one type to the other, but note that switching from owner to renter will delete any existing trailer listings.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: I signed up as a renter by mistake but want to be an owner. The system says my email is already registered. ---
This is because each email can only be used once on the platform. You cannot create a new owner account with the same email. Offer to convert their existing renter account to an owner account instead. Escalate to human support for the account type conversion. Remind the user they will need to download the white "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app after the conversion.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: My account is inactive/deactivated/suspended. How do I reactivate it? ---
Ask for the specific error message they're receiving and their account email address. Common reasons for deactivation include:

1. **Unresponded booking requests**: Account deactivated for not responding to booking requests within 12 hours. For reactivation, user must review and agree to Terms of Service.

2. **Business name in profile**: Accounts with business names instead of personal names are deactivated. The email is removed from the system so they can re-register with a valid first and last name.

3. **Policy violations**: Such as attempting to circumvent the platform or incomplete bookings. Review the specific violation before considering reactivation.

4. **Multiple failed login attempts**: May temporarily lock account.

5. **Incomplete profile**: Missing required information or ID verification.

For most cases, escalate to human support to review the deactivation reason and determine if reactivation is appropriate. Some accounts may require additional steps like connecting a bank account or acknowledging Terms of Service compliance.

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: Why was my profile or listing rejected? ---
Direct the user to check their listing status:

**From Owner App**: Select "More" > "My Trailers" > View status (shown with light green or red highlight)
**From Website**: Go to Dashboard > "Trailer" > "Trailer List" > View status

Common rejection reasons include:
1. Contact information visible in trailer photos (phone numbers, company names, etc.)
2. Incomplete address in the "Location" field  
3. Incorrect or missing VIN number
4. Incorrect weight capacity (should only be load weight the trailer can carry)
5. Incomplete profile or missing ID verification
6. Profile picture containing contact or business information

To resubmit: Complete all required fields, upload at least 4 high-quality photos without contact information, enter correct 17-character VIN, complete profile and ID verification, then submit for review. Direct users to Help Center at neighborstrailer.com/help-center for additional assistance.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I delete my account? ---
Also asked as: "Can you delete my account?", "How can I remove my personal information?", "Please close my account"

Ask for the email address associated with their account if not already provided. Escalate to human support with the message "User requests account deletion for [email address]." Account deletion typically takes 24-48 hours to complete. Note that account deletion will also remove all trailer listings and booking history.

If the user mentions receiving booking notifications after requesting deletion, escalate immediately as this indicates the deletion wasn't completed properly.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: I'm having trouble logging in. The site keeps going back to the login page or says my account is invalid. ---

1. Whether they're using the website or mobile app
2. Which app they downloaded (there are separate renter and owner apps)
3. Whether they're clicking "Sign in" rather than "Register"
4. The exact error message they're receiving

For owners, ensure they're using the white "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app, not the renter app. If using the wrong app, direct them to download the correct one.

If the account appears active but login fails, suggest trying the alternative platform (if using app, try website or vice versa). For password reset issues, try the opposite platform for the reset process.

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: How long does it take to approve my trailer listing? ---
Listings are typically approved within 4-6 business hours, but may take 1-2 business days depending on the queue. Approval times are usually faster for resubmissions after edits compared to initial submissions.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: I'm trying to use the wrong app type for my account. ---
There are two separate apps:
- **Renter App**: "Neighbors Trailer - Renter" 
- **Owner App**: "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" (white app)

If you're an owner trying to use the renter app or vice versa, you'll get login errors. Download the correct app for your account type. If you're unsure of your account type or need it converted, escalate to human support.

Escalate to human support for VIN verification. The listing cannot go live until the VIN is verified as correct.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I delete my account? ---
When users request account deletion, inform them that the support team will handle this process for them. There is no self-service account deletion feature. Delete the account as requested and optionally ask if they'd like to share feedback about what led to their decision. The user will no longer receive messages or notifications once the account is deleted.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I change my account type from renter to owner? ---
Users cannot change account types themselves - this requires support assistance. When switching from renter to owner:
1. Switch the account type in the system
2. Important: Inform the user they must download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app from the app store if using mobile
3. They can continue using the same login credentials
4. For incomplete profiles during the switch, some fields may be auto-filled with placeholder data - advise users to update their profile information immediately after the switch

Also asked as: "How do I register as an owner?", "I need my account switched to owner", "I want to become a trailer owner"

--- [Both] [profile] Q: My account is inactive or I can't log in - how do I reactivate it? ---
For inactive accounts, reactivate them in the system. These can occur for several reasons:
- User accidentally deactivated their own account
- Account was temporarily disabled due to technical issues
- Account was suspended for policy violations

Simply reactivate the account and confirm it's working. If the user mentions they were trying to add trailers or had activity scheduled, ensure they can proceed with their intended actions.

Also asked as: "My account says inactive", "I can't log in", "My account is locked"

--- [Renter] [profile] Q: I get an error saying "profile incomplete" when trying to book, but my profile is complete ---
This is a known technical issue that the development team is investigating. The current solution is to recreate the user's account:
1. Inform the user this is a technical error being investigated
2. Offer to delete and recreate their account (this requires their consent)
3. If they agree, deactivate the old account and remove the email from the system
4. They can then create a new account with the same email

For urgent bookings where the user needs immediate assistance, support can create a new account with temporary credentials and provide those to the user.

Also asked as: "Says I need to finish profile but everything is complete", "Profile incomplete error", "Can't complete booking due to profile error"

--- [Both] [profile] Q: Someone is trying to hack my account or I received suspicious messages ---
For security concerns:
1. Reassure the user that their account information is secure and there's no system breach
2. Explain that Neighbors Trailer will never ask for payment details, passwords, or sensitive information via messaging
3. If a fraudulent account contacted them, confirm it has been deactivated
4. If they clicked any suspicious links or provided credit card information, strongly advise them to contact their financial institution immediately
5. Remind them to report suspicious messages to service@neighborstrailer.com

Also asked as: "Received scam messages", "Fake support contacted me", "Security concern"

--- [Both] [profile] Q: Can I have both owner and renter accounts? ---
Users must use separate email addresses for owner and renter accounts. They cannot have both account types under the same email address. If they need both functionalities, they must create a second account with a different email address.

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: Can I use my LLC or business name on my account? ---
No, users may not use or display business information on their account, profile, or trailer listing. This is prohibited because it can cause renters to seek contact outside the platform, which violates the circumventing services policy. All accounts must use personal information only.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: I forgot my password - how do I reset it? ---
Direct users to the login page where they will see a "Forgot Password" button. This will guide them through the password reset process. The system handles password resets automatically.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I check if my account is still active? ---
Check the account status in the system using the email address they're contacting from. Confirm whether an active account exists under that email. If no account is found, suggest they may need to sign up again.

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: How long does trailer listing approval take? ---
Trailer listings are approved as soon as possible. Typical timeline:
- Standard approval: 4-6 business hours
- During high volume periods: 1-2 business days

If a listing is incomplete or requires corrections, users will be notified via email about missing information that needs to be updated.

3. Sensitive information is safe and secure

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: How do I update photos for my trailer listings? ---

5. Select "Submit for Review"

**On the Web:**
1. Navigate to "Trailers" and then "My Listings"
2. Select the 3-dot icon next to the trailer you wish to update
3. Scroll and select "Update Listings"
4. Update the photos associated with your trailer
5. Select "Submit for Review"

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: What does "Cost per km" mean in my trailer listing? ---
The "Cost per km" field is specifically for delivery charges and does not relate to mileage surcharges on the trailer when rented. This cost only applies if you participate in delivery services.

--- [Internal] [profile] Q: User's account was deactivated for policy violations ---
For accounts deactivated due to policy violations:
1. Explain the specific violations that occurred (e.g., sharing contact information before booking, ignoring pending bookings)
2. Reference the Terms & Conditions they agreed to upon account creation
3. For serious or repeated violations, the account will remain permanently suspended
4. Emphasize that all users must follow the same policies to maintain platform integrity

STANDARD TROUBLESHOOTING ORDER: 1) Log out, close the app completely, reopen, log back in. 2) If still failing, clear app cache or try the website instead. 3) If still failing, uninstall and reinstall the app. 4) Account recreation is the LAST resort — never offer it as a first step. IMPORTANT: Do NOT suggest account recreation until steps 1-3 have been attempted and failed.

--- [Both] [profile] Q: How do I switch my account from renter to owner? ---
Also asked as: "Change my account to owner", "Convert my profile from renter to Owner", "Switch my account type to an owner account"

When a user requests to switch from renter to owner account, follow these steps:

1. Check if their profile is complete. If incomplete, respond: "We'd be happy to switch your account to an owner account, but we noticed your profile is incomplete. We wouldn't be able to switch your account until your profile is completed. Let us know once you have done so!"

2. If profile is complete, inform them: "We have switched your account type to an owner account. It is important to note that if you're using the app, you will need to download the owner app named 'Neighbors Trailer- Owner'. From there, simply sign in with your login credentials."

3. Provide the owner app download links:
   - Google: https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.neighbourstrailerowner
   - Apple: https://apps.apple.com/us/app/neighbors-trailer-owner/id1667847016

Note: Users who accidentally created renter accounts when they meant to be owners are common. This is a standard request that can be fulfilled immediately if profile is complete.

The chat bot is able to look this up automatically by name. The email bot should direct users to log in at neighborstrailer.com and navigate to their profile/My Trailers section, or escalate to the support team who can provide the direct link.

2. Missing required tags when trying to submit for review.

For description issues, tell the user: "Your trailer was flagged due to the description containing inappropriate content. Please note that your trailer description is very important and what you put can contribute to the amount of potential renters you receive. Many renters determine if they want a trailer by the description. Please take the time to update your trailer description."

For missing tags, ask for a screenshot to help troubleshoot.

This gives new owners a complete understanding of the platform benefits and process.


## VERIFICATION ##

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: How do I complete ID verification? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-i-complete-ID-verification--178
ID verification is completed during the booking process through our verification partner, Clear. Follow the steps below:

• Select "Verify with Clear."
• Enter your phone number.
• Select "Get Started."
• Review and select "Accept and Continue" to agree to the terms.
• Enter the verification code sent to your phone.
• Select "Text me a link."
• Tap the link you receive by text message.
• Select "Continue."
• Allow camera access when prompted and follow the on-screen instructions.
• Take a selfie to complete verification.
Once your selfie is submitted, you will be returned to your booking to finish the process.

Why do I need to verify my ID?

ID verification helps protect both renters and trailer owners by:

• Confirming account identity
• Reducing fraud and unauthorized bookings
• Creating a safer rental experience for everyone
Verification is quick, secure, and required before completing a booking.

Is my information secure?

Yes. ID verification is handled securely through our trusted verification partner. Your information is encrypted and used only for identity verification purposes in accordance with applicable privacy standards.

If you experience any issues during verification, please contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: The CLEAR verification button is not working or appears blank when I click it ---
Also asked as: CLEAR ID not opening past the first popup screen, verification loop, CLEAR won't work

If the CLEAR verification button is not responding or the process is stuck in a loop, provide these troubleshooting steps in order:

1. **If using a web browser:** Perform a hard refresh (Ctrl+F5 on PC or Cmd+Shift+R on Mac), then log out completely and log back in before trying verification again
2. **If using the mobile app:** Make sure you have the latest version of the Neighbors Trailer Renter app (the green app) installed from your app store
3. **Try the other method:** If one isn't working, try the other (browser vs app) — sometimes one works when the other doesn't
4. **Different browser:** Try Chrome, Firefox, or Edge as they work best with CLEAR
5. **Clear browser cache:** Clear your browser cache and cookies, then try again
6. **Disable extensions:** Disable any browser extensions temporarily (ad blockers or privacy tools can sometimes interfere)
7. **Private/incognito window:** Try opening the verification link in a private/incognito window
8. **Different device:** Try logging in and completing verification from a trusted friend's or family member's device

Most verification issues are resolved with step 1 (hard refresh, log out, and log back in). 

IMPORTANT: Do NOT suggest alternatives to CLEAR verification. CLEAR ID verification is required for all renters with no exceptions.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: What types of identification are accepted for CLEAR verification? ---
Also asked as: I have a paper license, interim license, temporary license, state ID card, Real ID, passport

CLEAR verification requires a physical, non-expired driver's license. Inform users that:

**ACCEPTED:** Physical hard copy driver's license (standard or Real ID)

**NOT ACCEPTED:**
• Paper licenses or interim licenses 
• Temporary licenses
• State ID cards
• Expired driver's licenses
• Suspended driver's licenses

If the user does not have a valid physical driver's license, inform them that they cannot complete verification or rent a trailer until they obtain their physical license. This is a firm platform requirement with no exceptions.

If their license is suspended, they must wait until it's reinstated and they have the physical license in hand.

Alternative suggestion: If they don't have a valid license, a friend or family member with a valid license can create an account and book the trailer on their behalf, but that person must be present for both pickup and return.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: Can I use an alternative to CLEAR for ID verification? ---
Also asked as: I don't want to use CLEAR, can I email my driver's license, can I use ID.me instead, I don't have access to CLEAR

Inform the user that CLEAR ID verification is a firm requirement to book trailers on the platform with no alternatives or exceptions. Explain:

• CLEAR ID verification is required for all renters before completing a booking
• Safety and security is the platform's number one priority
• CLEAR is trusted by many airlines and major companies such as Uber, Public.com, and LinkedIn
• Their sensitive information is safe and secure
• For more information about CLEAR's security practices, direct them to: Support & Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) | CLEAR (https://www.clearme.com/support?search=safe)

IMPORTANT: Do NOT offer manual verification, alternative methods, or exceptions. There are no workarounds.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: I completed ID verification but the system says I'm still not verified ---
Also asked as: I did verification twice but still can't complete rental, verification completed but payment page won't work

Provide these troubleshooting steps:

1. **Sign out completely** and sign back in to your account
2. **Ensure the app is up to date** to the latest version
3. **Try switching methods** - use the website instead of the app or vice versa
4. **Try a different device** if the issue persists

If the user has completed verification successfully, check their account status. Some users may already be verified but experiencing a display issue.

If they continue having problems after these steps, escalate for manual review as there may be a technical issue preventing the verification status from updating properly.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: My antivirus or browser is blocking CLEAR as a dangerous website ---
Also asked as: Computer says CLEAR is dangerous, virus protection blocks CLEAR

Inform the user that:

• CLEAR is a legitimate, trusted verification partner used by major companies
• They need to add CLEAR to their antivirus whitelist/exceptions
• Advise them to look up how to add exceptions with their specific virus-protection software
• If they have anti-virus installed, they may need to run CLEAR as an exception

Direct them to CLEAR's security information page for verification of legitimacy: Support & Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) | CLEAR (https://www.clearme.com/support?search=safe)

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: I'm having camera or selfie issues during CLEAR verification ---
Also asked as: Too many selfie attempts, camera not working, large beard blocking selfie, photo verification problems

Ask the user what specific error message they are receiving. For general camera/selfie issues:

1. **Ensure proper conditions:** Camera should not be blurred, full face must be in view, adequate lighting
2. **ID verification:** Make sure the ID being used matches the user (not someone else's ID)
3. **Platform clarification:** Ask if they're using the web version or the app
4. **Camera permissions:** Ensure camera access is allowed when prompted

For "too many attempts" errors, the user may need to wait before trying again or contact support for assistance.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT suggest alternatives to completing the CLEAR process. All issues must be resolved within the CLEAR system.

--- [Renter] [verification] Q: I'm not receiving verification codes or text messages ---
Also asked as: Not getting text code, verification process stops at code entry

Provide these troubleshooting steps:

1. **Sign out and sign back in** to your account
2. **Update the app** to the latest version
3. **Try the website** instead of the app or vice versa
4. **Check spam/junk folders** for verification messages
5. **Verify phone number** is entered correctly

For users specifically having email verification issues with multiple warnings, recommend attempting verification using their phone number instead of email, or they may need to create a new account to resolve the issue.

--- [Owner] [verification] Q: What happens after I send a reservation to the renter? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-happens-after-I-send-a-reservation-to-the-renter--145
After you send a reservation through My Reservations, the renter will receive a text message prompting them to check their email and complete the booking.

The email will include instructions and login credentials (if needed).

What the Renter Must Complete

To finalize the reservation, the renter must:

• Complete ID verification
• Review and sign the rental contract (you can access the signed contract from the booking page)
• Submit payment

What Happens Next

Once the renter completes these steps:

• You will receive a notification that the booking is pending.
• You must go to the Bookings tab and accept the booking.
After acceptance, you will manage the rental as usual, including:

• Starting the rental at pickup
• Ending the rental at return
If you have questions about a reservation in progress, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Both] [verification] Q: Can a third-party driver pick up a trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Can-a-third-party-driver-pick-up-a-trailer--123
Also asked as: Someone other than the renter picking up, driver verification requirements

For Protection Package coverage to apply, the individual picking up and operating the trailer must be the renter named on the booking.

If someone other than the named renter picks up or operates the trailer, Protection Package coverage may not apply.

To ensure eligibility and proper documentation, the driver must:

• Be listed on the booking
• Complete required ID verification
• Meet all renter eligibility requirements

Inform users that the person picking up the trailer should be the same person who completed CLEAR ID verification and is listed on the booking. Protection Package coverage may not apply if someone else operates the trailer.

If you have questions about driver eligibility or coverage requirements, contact Neighbors Trailer Support before releasing the trailer.

--- [Owner] [verification] Q: Can the renter see the trailer in person before booking? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Can-the-renter-see-the-trailer-in-person-before-booking- --38
For your safety, Neighbors Trailer does not allow addresses to be shared before a booking is confirmed. If a renter asks to view a trailer prior to booking, please let them know that pickup details, including the address, can only be shared after you have accepted the booking.

In most cases, providing clear photos and detailed descriptions of your trailer gives renters all the information they need to book with confidence. It is uncommon for renters to request an in-person viewing before booking with a trailer rental company.

To help keep everyone safe, Neighbors Trailer does not allow direct contact or address sharing before a booking is confirmed.

--- [Owner] [verification] Q: I received a payout deduction notice for circumventing the platform ---
Also asked as: What is circumvention, why was I charged for circumvention

Circumvention occurs when you receive a booking or lead through the Neighbors Trailer platform and offer part or all of the rental services outside the platform. Key points to explain:

**What constitutes circumvention:**
• Sharing direct contact information before an accepted booking
• Attempting to move rental transactions off the platform
• Offering to rent outside the platform system

**Why it's enforced:**
• Renting off the platform is extremely high risk for damage, theft and other liability
• The Neighbors Trailer platform provides security measures including ID verification and credit card fraud detection
• ID verification is not completed until the booking is processed
• Platform investment protection and fairness to other trailer owners

**Policy details:**
• The policy applies whether or not the rental actually happens
• Deduction amounts are significantly reduced from the full amount stated in the Abuse of Services Policy
• Full policy details available at: https://neighborstrailer.com/terms

**If renters want to see the trailer:** All pictures and measurements can be shown in your listing or via message with the renter.

IMPORTANT: Do NOT suggest ways to circumvent the platform. All rentals must stay on the platform until booking is accepted.

--- [Internal] [verification] Q: User reports fraudulent messages requesting verification or payment information ---
Also asked as: Scam messages from fake support accounts, suspicious verification requests

When users report receiving suspicious messages claiming to be from Neighbors Trailer support requesting verification or payment information:

1. **Reassure the user:** There is no vulnerability or breach in the platform system. Personal and payment information has not been compromised.

2. **Explain the incident:** A fraudulent account was created on the platform attempting to contact users under false pretenses. The fake account has been deactivated.

3. **Clarify legitimate policy:** Neighbors Trailer will NEVER ask users to share payment details, passwords, or other sensitive information via direct message from another account.

4. **If they clicked the link:** Strongly urge them to contact their financial institution immediately to disable their card and report any fraudulent charges.

5. **Reporting:** Direct them to report any suspicious messages immediately through service@neighborstrailer.com.

Thank them for their vigilance in helping maintain a safe and trusted community.

Verification is required before completing any booking. The process is handled securely through Clear, with information encrypted and used only for identity verification purposes.

If the user experiences issues during verification, direct them to contact support.

If the renter confirms their license is actually expired, the renter will need to cancel the booking and would not be eligible to rent until they have a valid license.

--- [Owner] [verification] Q: What happens after I send a reservation to the renter? ---

After you send a reservation through My Reservations, the renter will receive a text message prompting them to check their email and complete the booking.

The email will include instructions and login credentials (if needed).

What the Renter Must Complete

• Complete ID verification

--- [Internal] [verification] Q: When can manual verification be performed and what are the requirements? ---
Manual verification can be performed in specific circumstances:
