## EXTENSION ##

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if I receive a non-compliance notice about not starting or ending a rental? ---
Also asked as: Non-Compliance Start / End Rental
When an owner receives a non-compliance notice about booking ID management, explain that this is sent when rentals are not properly started or ended in the system. The notice warns of potential $25 daily fees per the Terms of Use (https://neighborstrailer.com/terms).

Explain the importance of ending rentals immediately when trailers are returned:
1. Releases the renter's deposit money promptly
2. Expedites owner payout (initiated only when rental is ended)
3. Provides proof of damages timing
4. Documents actual rental completion date/time for late return fee purposes

If the delay was due to waiting for extension approval, inform the user that extensions must be approved before the rental can be properly closed. Direct them to process any pending extensions immediately to resolve the compliance issue.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if my trailer is overdue and the renter won't extend or communicate? ---
When a trailer is not returned by the scheduled end date and the renter is not responding or extending, provide this step-by-step escalation process:

**Initial Response:**
Almost 100% of late returns are due to renters forgetting to extend or irresponsibility, not theft. Don't panic initially.

**Escalation Steps:**
1. Contact renter through Neighbors Trailer message portal asking when they will return the trailer
2. If no response, try texting (request phone number from support if needed)
3. Send written message with specific deadline: "Your rental was due back at [date/time]. I have reached out many times and have not heard back from you. I will give you until [specific time] today to contact me or I will have to escalate the matter and terminate the rental."
4. If no response by deadline, send termination notice: Tell renter you are terminating the rental and give short final deadline (1 hour) or you will contact police and report trailer stolen
5. If still no response, contact law enforcement

**Important Notes:**
- Document all communication attempts
- Terminating the rental means formal written notice they no longer have legal right to possess the trailer
- Do NOT close the booking until trailer is returned or situation resolved
- Stop charging rental fees after reporting stolen
- Once reported stolen, matter becomes criminal
- Laws vary by jurisdiction - owners responsible for complying with local laws

If unsure how to proceed at any stage, contact Neighbors Trailer Support before escalating.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if I can't process an extension because of payment authorization failures? ---
When an extension request fails with "unable to authorize charge" or payment errors, this indicates insufficient funds on the renter's credit card or the renter hasn't saved their payment information for future transactions.

Actions to take:
1. Contact the renter and inform them the payment failed
2. Ask them to update their payment method or ensure sufficient funds
3. Have the renter contact their credit card company to authorize the charge
4. If the renter is uncooperative, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for escalatory next steps

Important: Neighbors Trailer cannot manually charge a card that has failed authorization. The renter must resolve the payment issue on their end before the extension can be processed.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How do I handle a situation where my trailer listing is under review and blocking extension processing? ---
If an extension request fails due to the trailer listing being under review, explain that certain actions like approving extensions may not process correctly while a listing is in review status.

Contact Neighbors Trailer Support immediately with the booking ID and extension request number. Support can temporarily remove the listing from review to allow the extension to complete, then return it to review status.

This typically occurs when a listing was recently edited and placed under review for photo or other requirements.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if I see multiple failed extension requests in the system? ---
When multiple extension requests show as "rejected" and the owner didn't reject them, explain that this occurs when the system repeatedly attempts to capture the renter's payment and fails. The renter's card will not be officially charged until they successfully accept and pay for an extension request.

Any temporary charges the renter sees will fall off within 24 hours. The owner cannot manually process these failed extensions - the renter must resolve their payment issues and submit a new extension request.

--- [Renter] [extension] Q: How do I extend my rental when the app isn't giving me the extension option? ---
If a renter cannot find the extension option, provide the step-by-step process:

**From Website or App:**
1. Select "Dashboard"
2. Select "My Bookings" (web) or "Bookings" (app)
3. Select "Current" tab if rental has started, or "Upcoming" if not yet started
4. Select the booking ID number to reach booking details page
5. Select "Extension Request"
6. Enter number of additional days
7. Enter comment in "Remarks" field
8. Select "Send Request" and complete payment

The trailer owner will be notified and can accept or reject the request.

If the option still doesn't appear, check that they have the latest app version or try using the website instead.

--- [Renter] [extension] Q: What should I do if I'm having trouble paying for an extension due to vehicle breakdown or being stuck out of state? ---
When renters are stuck due to vehicle breakdown or other emergencies and cannot complete extension payment:

1. First, get their booking ID to investigate the specific issue
2. Check if their payment method is failing authorization
3. If payment keeps failing, they need to contact their credit card company or update their payment method
4. Emphasize the importance of communicating with the trailer owner about the situation
5. If they continue having technical difficulties, escalate to support for manual assistance

The key is maintaining communication with the owner and resolving payment issues promptly to avoid escalation to theft situations.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: Do I need to wait for an extension to be approved before ending the rental? ---
Yes, if an extension is not approved before the original rental end time, it will not be processed or charged to the renter. You must wait for extension approval before ending the rental, otherwise the extension will be lost.

If you're having trouble with extension approval, provide the booking ID to support for assistance with manual processing.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: Why is my extension request showing a different rate than my original booking rate? ---
When extension rates don't match the original booking rate, explain that this can be a system issue. The development team investigates these rate discrepancies.

As a temporary solution, recommend sending the renter a custom offer with a discount to match the original rate they expected. This can be done through the "Send Offer" button in the message portal.

--- [Both] [extension] Q: Why don't extensions automatically apply discounted rates like weekly or monthly rates? ---
Extensions do not automatically apply pro-rated discounts for weekly or monthly rates. To receive weekly/monthly rates, the rental must be booked for the full period initially (7 days for weekly, 30 days for monthly).

For renters wanting discounted rates on extensions:
- Contact the trailer owner directly
- Owner can process a partial refund at their discretion (up to 75% of rental amount)
- Alternatively, the owner can send a custom offer with discount

Note: When a renter books additional days past achieving a weekly rate, they continue to receive the weekly rate for those additional days.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How do I charge for extra time when a renter returns late without extending? ---
If a renter returns the trailer late without processing an extension:

**Option 1:** Submit an extension request yourself (if renter has payment method saved)
**Option 2:** Submit a Deposit Deduction Claim for the extra time once the trailer is returned
**Option 3:** Create an add-on that the renter can add to cover the costs

Important: You cannot back-date extensions, so deposit deduction claims or add-ons are the preferred methods for charging post-return late fees.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if a renter disputes my deposit deduction for late return? ---
When a renter disputes a deposit deduction claim, Neighbors Trailer Support will review the dispute and contact the owner to confirm whether they want to proceed with the deduction.

Provide all documentation of:
- Original return date and time
- Communication attempts with renter
- Actual return time
- Any additional costs incurred (recovery costs, missed rentals, etc.)

Support will make the final determination after reviewing both parties' evidence.

--- [Internal] [extension] Q: How should support handle extension requests that cannot be back-dated? ---
When owners need to charge for time already passed without an extension, do not attempt to back-date extensions as this is not supported by the system.

Instead, recommend:
1. Creating an add-on that covers the costs of the extra rental time
2. Processing a deposit deduction claim if the trailer has been returned
3. Manual review and adjustment if the situation requires special handling

Document the specific booking ID and circumstances for proper resolution.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: Can I offer discounted extension rates to my renters? ---
Yes, owners can offer discounted extension rates through several methods:

1. **Custom Offer:** Use the "Send Offer" button in the message portal to send a customized discounted offer
2. **Coupons:** Create a coupon using the "Coupons" option in the "More" settings
3. **Partial Refund:** After extension is processed, issue a partial refund up to 75% of the rental amount (fees are not included in refunds)

Choose the method that best fits your situation and relationship with the renter.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if someone other than my original renter is responding to extension requests? ---
If someone other than the original renter responds to extension communications, this may indicate:

1. The renter has authorized someone else to handle the return
2. The account may be shared or managed by multiple people
3. Potential security concern

Request the booking ID to investigate the account details and communication history. Verify the identity of who you're communicating with and ensure all extension agreements are properly documented through the platform messaging system.

--- [Both] [extension] Q: What happens to Protection Package coverage during extensions? ---
Protection Package coverage only applies during verified and fully paid rental periods processed through the Neighbors Trailer platform.

For extensions:
- Coverage continues if extension is properly processed and paid before the original rental period ends
- If extension is not completed prior to original end time, NT Protect may not apply to the extended period
- Extensions must be processed through the system to maintain proper coverage and documentation

Always ensure extensions are completed before the original rental end time to maintain continuous coverage.

--- [Both] [extension] Q: How do I request an extension for a rental? ---
Both renters and owners can submit unlimited extension requests. To request an extension:

From the Website:
- Go to Dashboard
- Select My Bookings (renter) or Bookings (owner) 
- If rental has started, select Current tab; otherwise select Upcoming
- Select the booking you want to extend
- Choose Extension Request
- Enter number of additional days
- Add comment in Remarks field
- Select Send Request

From the Mobile App:
- Select Bookings
- Tap Current (if started) or Upcoming (if not started)
- Select the booking
- Select Extension Request
- Enter number of additional days
- Add comment in Remarks field
- Tap Send Request

If the user is a renter, they will be directed to complete payment for the extension. If the user is an owner, the renter will be notified and can accept or dispute the request.

IMPORTANT: Extensions must be processed before the original rental period ends to maintain NT Protect coverage. If an extension is not completed prior to the original end time, Protection Package coverage may not apply to the extended period.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How do I handle a late return without an extension? ---
When a trailer is not returned on time and no extension was submitted:

1. Process an extension request immediately for the extra days the renter kept the trailer
2. Contact Neighbors Trailer Support if the renter doesn't have a payment method on file
3. Support can manually charge the renter for the additional days once an extension is processed
4. End the rental only after the extension has been accepted and processed

Do NOT attempt to handle late returns through deposit deductions alone. Always process the extension first to ensure proper charging for the additional days.

If there are damages in addition to late return, you can submit a Deposit Deduction Claim for damages separately after processing the extension for the extra days.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if my renter asks for an extension but I have another booking? ---
You are NOT required to accept extension requests if you have another booking scheduled. Inform the renter through the platform messaging that you cannot accept the extension due to an existing booking and that they must return the trailer at the original scheduled time.

If the renter disputes your rejection, explain that you have a legitimate scheduling conflict. Contact Neighbors Trailer Support if the renter causes complications or fails to return on time.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How can I offer a free extension to a renter? ---
To offer an extension at no cost:

1. Update your trailer listing price to $0 temporarily
2. Submit the extension request while the price is $0
3. After the extension is accepted, change your listing price back to the original amount

This workaround allows you to provide a complimentary extra day when circumstances warrant it (such as complications on your end that affected the rental).

--- [Both] [extension] Q: Can I apply a coupon code or discount to an extension? ---
Coupons cannot currently be applied to extension requests. However, there are two workarounds:

For Owners: Temporarily update your listing price using the "Update Rent" button to a discounted rate, then process the extension at that lower rate.

For Owners (alternative): Use the partial refund option after the extension is processed to refund the discount amount to the renter.

Extensions always charge at the current listing price, so adjust the listing price if you want to offer a discount on the extension.

--- [Renter] [extension] Q: Can I get weekly rates if I extend a daily rental to 7+ days? ---
No, you cannot get weekly rates by extending a daily rental. Weekly rates only apply when the initial booking is made for 7 days or more from the start.

If you want something closer to a weekly rate, ask the owner to send you a discounted extension request by temporarily lowering their listing price, or request a partial refund after the extension if the owner agrees.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: Why is my payout different for extension days? ---
Extension payouts may calculate differently than the original booking rate. The payout structure for extensions follows the current listing price and payout percentage at the time the extension is processed.

If a user questions their payout amount, provide them with a breakdown showing:
- Original booking payout (80% of original rent amount)
- Extension payout (80% of extension rent amount) 
- Total payout

Direct them to contact support if they believe there's an error in the calculation.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How do I accept or reject an extension request from a renter? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Can-I-Accept-an-Extension-Request--163

From the App:
- Tap More
- Select Booking Adjustment Requests
- Choose My Extension Requests
- Tap View Details for the booking
- Enter message in Remarks field (optional but recommended)
- Tap Accept or Reject
- Select Inform Renter to send your response

From the Website:
- Go to Dashboard
- Select Booking Adjustment Requests
- Click My Extension Requests
- Select View Details for the applicable booking
- Enter message in Remarks field
- Click Accept or Reject
- Select Inform Renter to notify the renter

Once accepted, rental dates and charges will update automatically.

--- [Renter] [extension] Q: How do I respond to an extension request from the owner? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Do-I-Accept-an-Extension-Requested-by-A-Trailer-Owner--160

If an owner sends you an extension request:
- Select Dashboard (web) or More (app)
- Tap My Extension Requests
- Select View Details
- Enter comment in Remarks field
- Choose Accept or Dispute
- Select Inform Owner

Respond promptly to extension requests. If you dispute an owner's extension request, provide your reasoning in the remarks field.

--- [Both] [extension] Q: What happens if an extension isn't processed before the original rental ends? ---
If an extension request is not completed before the original rental end time:
- NT Protect Protection Package coverage may not apply to the extended period
- The request may need manual review by Neighbors Trailer Support
- Contact Support if the extension wasn't accepted in time due to system issues

Always submit extension requests as early as possible, ideally before the rental period expires, to ensure continuous coverage and proper processing.

--- [Internal] [extension] Q: How should I handle disputes about late returns and extensions? ---
When users contact about late returns:

1. First determine if an extension was processed for the extra days
2. If no extension exists, instruct the owner to submit one immediately
3. If payment method issues prevent extension processing, manually charge the renter after creating the extension
4. For damage claims on late returns, direct owner to process extension first, then submit separate deposit deduction claim
5. If owner has scheduling conflicts preventing extension acceptance, confirm they can reject the request
6. Always ensure proper documentation of actual return dates versus scheduled dates

Do NOT allow owners to handle late returns solely through deposit deductions - extensions must be processed for proper charging of additional days.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if my trailer is not returned on time? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-can-I-do-if-my-trailer-is-not-returned--166

You should always process an extension request or ask the renter to process one prior to the rental end if you think the trailer won't be returned on time.

If your trailer has not been returned by the scheduled end date and time, follow these steps:

Step 1: Attempt immediate contact
- Send message through Neighbors Trailer message portal requesting update
- Attempt phone/text contact if no response
- Document all communication attempts
- Contact Support for renter's phone number if needed

Step 2: Provide written notice
- Send written message with clear, reasonable deadline for response
- Example: "Your rental was due back on [date/time]. I have attempted to contact you and have not received a response. Please respond by [specific time] or the rental will be terminated and escalated."
- Always include specific date and time

Step 3: Terminate the rental
- Send final written notice terminating the rental if no response by deadline
- Provide short final deadline for immediate contact
- Document all termination notices in writing through the platform

IMPORTANT: Terminating the rental means formal written notice that they no longer have legal right to possess the trailer. Do NOT close the booking until trailer is returned or situation is resolved.

Step 4: Escalate if necessary
- After documented communication and deadlines, you may contact law enforcement to report trailer as stolen
- Stop charging rental fees after reporting stolen
- Laws vary by state - owners responsible for complying with local laws

Contact Neighbors Trailer Support before escalating if unsure how to proceed.


## PAYMENTS ##

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Why am I being charged for circumvention when the rental didn't happen? ---
Explain that circumvention charges apply regardless of whether the rental actually occurred. Send this standard response: "A circumvention is when you receive a booking or lead through the Neighbors Trailer platform and offer part or all of the rental services outside the platform. Our Abuse of Services Policy is not contingent on the rental happening or not. The deduction has been applied per our Terms of Use at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms." Note that deduction amounts vary ($25-$112) and may be reduced from the full policy amount. Also asked as: "Payout Deduction Notice"

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How do I submit toll bills for renter reimbursement? ---
Direct owners to email the toll bill directly to support. Before processing, confirm the trailer is enrolled in the toll program. Provide these enrollment steps: 1) Login to Neighbors Trailer account 2) Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" and select "Click Here" (web) or "Tap Here" (app) 3) Select "Enroll Now" 4) Select "Add License Plate" 5) Select "Enroll". Explain that enrollment is free and reduces future toll bills by automating the process. Ask them to confirm enrollment when sending the toll bill.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: How are toll charges calculated? ---
Explain that toll charges include both the actual toll amount plus a $7.00 administrative fee per transaction. For example: if a renter has 3 separate toll transactions totaling $13.46, the total charge would be $13.46 + (3 × $7.00) = $34.46. The administrative fee covers intercepting, processing, and managing toll charges through the toll program per the Terms of Use.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Do you charge sales tax on rentals? ---
Respond: "If sales tax is applicable to the transaction in your state, it is applied. However, we take full responsibility for any sales tax incurred and get it paid for you." For payment timing questions, request the Booking ID number to investigate further.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: I updated my bank account but haven't received payment ---
Inform the owner that when bank account information is updated, funds will be transferred to the new account. Allow up to 3 business days for processing. If the issue persists, investigate further with their booking details.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I'm seeing charges but my booking is still pending ---
Explain that payments are only authorized, not actually charged, until the booking is accepted. If a booking is cancelled or rejected, the authorization hold is immediately released and will return to the card within 24 hours. No actual charge occurs until acceptance.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I want a refund for a cancelled/declined booking ---
Confirm that only authorization holds are placed initially, not actual charges. When bookings are cancelled or declined, holds are automatically released within 24 hours. The funds will return to their card based on their bank's processing time.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: How do I get a copy of my rental invoice? ---
Direct users to navigate to "Bookings" in their account, select the specific booking, then select the "Documents" tab to view their booking invoice and related documentation.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Why is my payout less than the rental amount? ---
Explain the 20% platform commission structure. For example: Rental Amount of $150 minus 20% Platform Service Fee ($30) equals $120 owner payout. Note that renter-side fees (Deposit Processing Fee, Booking Fee, Protection Package) are not deducted from owner payouts. Reference the Terms of Service for commission details.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: When will I receive my rental payment? ---
Explain that payouts are automatically initiated when the rental is marked as completed and typically take 1-3 business days to appear in the bank account. If payment shows as "Paid" in the system but hasn't appeared after several business days, investigate potential bank account issues or contact information problems.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: What was this additional charge on my account? ---
For unexpected charges, direct users to navigate to Bookings, select the specific Booking ID, then check the "Additional Charges" tab for details. Most additional charges are toll-related. Request the Booking ID if they need further investigation.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: My bank account was closed but I had a recent rental ---
Request the Booking ID to investigate the specific payout. Explain that closed bank accounts prevent successful payout processing. Direct them to update their bank account information in account settings, then contact support to reprocess the payment to the new account.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I was charged twice for the same rental ---
Investigate whether multiple bookings were created. Sometimes this occurs when extension requests are submitted but users create new bookings instead. One charge will typically be refunded within 24 hours when duplicate bookings are identified.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: When will my security deposit be refunded? ---
Explain that deposit refunds are automatically initiated when the trailer owner ends the rental, provided no damages or late fees are filed. Refunds typically take 4-7 business days to appear on statements after initiation.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: I haven't received payment for completed rentals ---
Request booking numbers to investigate. Common issues include closed bank accounts, incorrect banking information, or recent bank account setup delays. If bank account was recently added, payments may be delayed and should process within 48 hours.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I see a $0.00 charge with negative refund description ---
Explain this is normal processing notation when refunds are initiated. The actual refund amount will appear separately and takes 4-7 business days to reflect on their account.

--- [Internal] [payments] Q: How to handle subrogation and insurance claims ---
For renters dealing with third-party insurance companies requiring confirmation about NT Protect subrogation rights, request the booking number to review claim details and coordinate with the claims department for proper documentation.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: My trailers disappeared from the rental platform ---
When owners report visibility issues combined with payment problems, first check if their bank account is showing as closed in the payment system. Closed bank accounts can affect both payouts and listing visibility. Direct them to update bank account information and confirm it's active.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: I need help with payment card blocks or authorization issues ---
For payment processing errors, check if the user was ultimately able to complete their transaction. Often temporary authorization holds resolve automatically. If persistent issues, escalate to technical support for payment gateway investigation.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I was charged for tolls months later ---
Explain that toll charges can be processed after the rental period when toll bills are received by owners and submitted for renter billing. Direct users to the "Tolls" tab in their booking details to review specific toll transactions and dates.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: I need specific payment details or trace numbers ---
For refund confirmations and bank references, provide system trace numbers when available (format example: 546628). Explain that refund processing timing depends on the user's financial institution, not Neighbors Trailer.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How to handle toll bills for rentals not in toll program ---
If the trailer wasn't enrolled in the toll program but received toll bills during rental periods, owners can still submit toll bills via email with the booking ID. Attempt to charge the renter on the owner's behalf, but emphasize enrolling in the toll program to prevent future issues.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Customer says they were charged but booking wasn't accepted or was rejected ---
Explain that payment is only authorized (not actually charged) until booking is accepted. If booking is rejected or canceled, the authorization hold is immediately released and money returns to their card within 12-24 hours (may take up to 24 hours to reflect on statement). This is standard authorization practice, not an actual charge. If customer insists they see a charge after 24 hours, ask for Booking ID to investigate further.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Payment error during booking attempt ---
Explain that if booking attempt ended in payment error, any pending charge will fall off within 24 hours as funds were not successfully captured. Ask customer to verify card information is entered correctly (all digits, expiration date, CVC code). If payment errors persist, advise contacting their financial institution to determine why payment is not processing successfully.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Multiple/duplicate charges appearing ---
Investigate the specific situation. Common scenarios: 1) Customer sees multiple payment attempts but only one actual charge (others are failed attempts that will fall off), 2) One charge is original rental, second is for tolls incurred during rental, 3) Multiple authorization attempts due to booking errors. Cancel any pending failed transactions and clarify which charges are legitimate.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Payout not received or delayed ---
Check if payout was successfully processed by system but not yet reflected in account (takes 1-2 business days after processing). Verify owner has connected bank account - if no connected account, payouts are on hold until account is connected. If payout shows as processed but owner hasn't received after 2 business days, investigate further. For specific booking inquiries, request Booking ID.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Payout failed due to bank account issues ---
Common issue is incorrect bank account number. Direct owner to update bank information: Owner app > More > My Bank Account > Enter correct routing and account number. Once corrected, failed payouts can be resubmitted and will arrive in 1-3 business days.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Payment status showing as "Error" ---
This typically indicates error when payout attempted to initiate. Re-submit the payout - funds will appear in owner's account in 1-3 business days. If error persists, investigate bank account connection status.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Stripe account questions ---
When creating Neighbors Trailer owner account, a Stripe account is automatically created to process payouts for rentals. This account is completely automated and separate. Owners need to create separate Stripe account for any personal payment processing outside of Neighbors Trailer.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Toll bills for renters ---
If owner receives toll bill for renter's usage, they can email the toll bill to support and we will attempt to charge the renter. IMPORTANT: Before processing toll bills, owners should enroll in the free toll program to prevent future toll bills. Enrollment steps: 1) Login to Neighbors Trailer account, 2) Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" > "Click Here" (web) or "Tap Here" (app), 3) Select "Enroll Now", 4) Select "Add License Plate", 5) Select "Enroll". Program is free with no subscription cost and automates toll collection from renters.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Charged for tolls after rental ended ---
Explain that charge is for toll bills incurred during their rental period. Provide toll activity breakdown if available, showing specific toll locations, dates, times, license plate, and amounts. These charges occur when renter used toll roads during rental.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Split payment across multiple cards not possible ---
Platform does not support using two different payment methods for a single transaction. Customer must use one payment method for entire booking amount.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Booking not showing in account despite charge ---
If customer was charged but booking doesn't appear in their account, first verify they're using the correct email address that matches the booking. If booking was rejected, explain authorization vs. actual charge (funds will return within 24 hours). If booking should be active but not showing, request Booking ID to investigate account linking issues.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Deposit refund issues ---
Deposits can only be refunded via original payment method. If customer's card is locked/closed, they must work with their bank for resolution. Neighbors Trailer cannot refund to alternative payment methods for security reasons.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Requesting rental contract or receipt ---
For rental contracts, attach PDF of the signed rental contract. Note that Documents tab location mentioned in help articles may not be visible to all users - provide contract directly via email when requested.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Payment processing issues during checkout ---
Troubleshooting steps: 1) Ensure payment information is entered manually (not auto-filled), 2) Sign out and sign back in, 3) Try website instead of app or vice versa, 4) Verify app is up to date. If "please enter valid card details" error persists, verify all card information is correct.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Missing delivery charges in payout ---
Due to technical issues, delivery charges may not apply to some bookings. Owner can request renter pay directly or we can charge renter with automatic 10% processing fee applied to the transaction.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Owner requesting additional credit card information ---
If owner is requesting credit card details despite customer already paying through platform, explain this may be owner's standard off-platform contract. Since payment is completed through Neighbors Trailer, additional credit card information is not necessary. Customer should inform owner of this.

--- [Policy] [payments] Q: Cancellation charges and fees ---
For renter cancellations: Encourage renters to go through proper cancellation process rather than having owner cancel (which results in $90 charge to owner). For weather-related cancellations, owners can request renter not be charged. For partial refunds: 1) Trailer owner must authorize, 2) Can only be processed before owner ends rental, 3) Maximum 75% of rent amount refundable, 4) Booking fees, tax, insurance are non-refundable, 5) $25 processing fee for manual refunds after rental ended. Reference Refunds Policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Account deactivation requests ---
For customers requesting account deactivation and credit card removal, process account deactivation as requested. Confirm completion to customer.

--- [Internal] [payments] Q: 1099 tax reporting questions ---
For any tax-related questions (sales tax, 1099 reporting, tax obligations), direct users to the Help Center article: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-It-Works-179. Key points: NT complies with state and local tax laws, sales tax is automatically collected in applicable states, and NT does not provide tax advice. For specific tax obligations, advise users to consult a qualified tax professional. Do NOT attempt to answer specific tax questions — escalate to human support if the Help Center article does not address their concern.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: NT Protection Package coverage ---
Protection Package only covers damages exceeding $500 deductible. Coverage is based on photos taken at pickup (showing condition before renter possession) and return (showing condition after renter possession). Photos are available in Booking Activity section of Booking Details.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Pending booking with unresponsive owner ---
When renter has pending booking with unresponsive owner and sees pending charge, explain authorization process. Request Booking ID to investigate owner responsiveness and potentially facilitate communication or process cancellation if needed.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Closed bank account with pending payouts ---
If owner closed bank account, payouts are held until new account is connected. Ask if owner is receiving errors when attempting to connect new bank account. Guide through bank account update process if needed.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Refund amount discrepancies ---
When customer questions refund amounts, explain that final charge shown is after refund was processed (original charge minus refund amount). Refunds typically appear in account within 4-7 business days.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Why is my payout amount different than expected or lower than the rental price? ---
When a user reports their payout is less than expected, ask for the Booking ID number to investigate. Direct them to check for a Payout Deduction Notice that would have been sent via email explaining any deductions. Common reasons for reduced payouts include: owner cancellation fees (30% of rental amount), toll charges, damage claims, or platform fees. Tell them to refer to the specific Payout Deduction Notice for their booking which contains the detailed breakdown.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How long does it take to receive payment after a rental ends? ---
Explain that owner payouts typically occur within 3-5 business days after a rental is completed. However, payments may be delayed due to bank holidays or if there are deductions that need processing. If an owner hasn't received payment after this timeframe, ask for the Booking ID to investigate the specific booking.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: What is the owner cancellation fee and when is it charged? ---
When an owner cancels an accepted booking, they incur a 30% fee of the rental amount. This fee is deducted from their next or future payout. The owner receives a disclaimer about this fee when they cancel. If the 30% fee exceeds the payout amount for their next booking, they may receive no payout or a reduced payout until the fee is covered. Direct them to their Payout Deduction Notice for specific details about how this fee was applied.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How do I get reimbursed for tolls from a rental? ---
To get toll reimbursement, the owner should: 1) First enroll in the free toll program to prevent future toll bills 2) Reply to the support email with the toll bill attached 3) Neighbors Trailer will attempt to charge the renter for the tolls. To enroll in the toll program: Login to account > Dashboard > Select "Enroll in Our Free Toll Program" > Click/Tap "Click Here"/"Tap Here" > Select "Enroll Now" > Select "Add License Plate" > Select "Enroll". The toll program is completely free and automates toll collection from renters.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How do I set up my bank account to receive payments? ---
To link a bank account for payouts, owners need to submit a PDF of a voided check. Direct them to their account settings where they can upload this document to complete the bank account setup process.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Why was I charged twice or why do I see duplicate charges? ---
When a renter reports duplicate charges, first check if they had multiple booking requests. Explain that funds are only authorized (not charged) when a booking request is submitted, and only actually charged when the owner accepts. If an owner rejects the booking, the authorized funds are released within 12-24 hours. For actual duplicate charges, staff can void the duplicate pending charge immediately.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Why haven't I received my refund yet? ---
For deposit refunds, explain the timing depends on the reason. If an owner rejected their booking, funds are released within 12-24 hours but may take longer to show on their bank statement. For other refunds (like extensions they didn't use), it typically takes 4-7 business days. If they claim it should have been refunded sooner, ask for the Booking ID and check if any uncaptured charges need to be canceled. Provide them with the refund receipt link when available.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: What charges might I see after my rental? ---
Renters may see additional charges for: tolls incurred during the rental (viewable under "Tolls" in Booking Details), late return fees, damage claims, or extension fees. Direct them to check their Booking Details for a breakdown of any additional charges and refer to specific sections like "Tolls" for toll-related charges.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: How do I get a receipt for my booking? ---
Direct users to: App users: Go to "Bookings" > select the booking > scroll down to "Receipts" and download. Website users: Go to "Bookings" > "Past Bookings" tab > select booking > "Documents" tab > download receipts. Note that refund receipts will show $0 until the refund is fully processed, which takes 4-7 business days.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Are there sales taxes charged and who handles them? ---
If sales tax is applicable, the renter is charged at checkout. Neighbors Trailer takes full responsibility for sales tax collection and remittance, so owners don't need to handle any sales tax obligations.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Can I give a free rental? ---
Free rentals are not possible because renters are still responsible for paying applicable taxes, insurance, and booking fees even if the daily rate is $0. These charges cannot be waived.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Can I give a renter extra time without charging them more? ---
The recommended approach is to process a date change request and extension (which will charge the renter), then use the "Partial Refund" feature to refund the extra day. Note that booking fees for the extra day are non-refundable. Alternatively, the owner can allow early pickup without going through the system, but insurance will not apply for that extra day.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: My credit card was declined or I'm having payment issues ---
For payment issues, first verify their profile information is complete and correct. If their name doesn't match their verification documents exactly, staff can update their account profile. For persistent payment problems with booking, the current workaround is to delete and recreate their account (only offer this if the user agrees to the process).

--- [Internal] [payments] Q: How to handle payout errors showing on owner accounts ---
If owners report "Error" messages on their payouts, especially on bank holidays, instruct them to disregard these messages. These errors are typically due to bank holidays and the payouts will process normally. No action is needed.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I was a victim of a phishing scam asking for credit card information ---
If a user reports they received messages asking for credit card verification or gave their information to a fraudulent account, explain that: 1) Neighbors Trailer never asks for payment details via direct message 2) Their platform remains secure - this was a fake account that has been deactivated 3) Strongly urge them to contact their financial institution immediately to disable their card and report any fraudulent charges 4) Direct them to report suspicious messages to service@neighborstrailer.com.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How to charge a renter for tolls from a specific booking ---
When an owner wants to charge a renter for specific toll amounts, first check if they're enrolled in the toll program. If not, provide the enrollment steps. Then have them reply to the email with the toll bill attached, and staff will attempt to charge the renter. Recommend they always cross-reference toll bills with the associated booking to verify if tolls were already charged.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: How to verify if an email about tax documents is legitimate ---
Emails from notifications@stripe.com regarding 1099 tax forms are legitimate. Neighbors Trailer partners with Stripe, and users who meet certain income thresholds through the platform will receive 1099 forms via Stripe for tax purposes.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: I have ongoing charges after returning my trailer ---
When renters report unexpected ongoing charges after returning a trailer, ask for the Booking ID number to investigate the specific charges. These could be related to tolls, damage claims, or other post-rental fees.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How to handle a no-show renter ---
If a renter doesn't show up at the designated pickup time, instruct the owner to start and end the rental in the system and mark it as a "No-Show". This prevents any charges or fees to the owner.

--- [Internal] [payments] Q: Account closure and credit card removal requests ---
For account closure requests, deactivate the account and submit a request to development to remove credit card information. Reference the Privacy Policy regarding data retention requirements - some information may need to be retained for legal compliance, fraud prevention, fee collection, dispute resolution, and audit purposes.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Customer says they were charged but booking was rejected or cancelled ---
Explain that payment is only authorized (not actually charged) until a booking is accepted by the owner. If a booking is cancelled or rejected before acceptance, the authorization hold is immediately released and money returns to their card within 12-24 hours (may take up to 24 hours to reflect on statement). No actual charge occurs until owner accepts the booking.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer can't complete payment or getting payment errors ---
Ask if they're receiving a specific error message when attempting to submit payment. If payment won't go through, they may need to contact their bank or try a different payment method. For technical issues during checkout, have them retry the booking process.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner asking about platform commission or fees ---
Explain that Neighbors Trailer takes 20% commission on every rental. In return, they provide rentals, advertising, ID verification, free toll program, damage claims management, insurance coverage, and an all-in-one rental tool. This is standard platform fee structure.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner hasn't received payout ---
Check that the rental has been marked as completed - payouts are automatically initiated when rental is ended and take 1-3 business days to reflect in bank account. If rental is completed but no payout received, investigate specific booking and provide payout timeline.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner payout failed due to incorrect bank information ---
Inform owner that payout failed because bank account information is incorrect. Direct them to: Owner app > More > My Bank Account > Enter correct routing and account number. Common issue is account number being wrong length for the bank. Offer to update manually if they provide correct information.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner wants to connect bank account or concerned about providing bank details ---
Explain that sensitive banking information is handled by Stripe (trusted third-party payment processor used by major companies) and is not accessible to Neighbors Trailer staff. Information is safe and secure. All payouts are electronic via Stripe - no checks are sent. Bank connection is required to receive payouts.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer seeing duplicate charges or multiple charges ---
Ask for Booking ID to investigate. Multiple pending charges may appear temporarily but only one actual charge should process. If duplicate charges confirmed, investigate and resolve based on booking details.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Early return refund requests ---
Explain early return refund policy: 1) Owner must authorize refund and can process it from their account, 2) Must be processed no later than rental end date, 3) Maximum 75% of rent amount refundable, 4) Booking fees, tax, and insurance are non-refundable, 5) $25 processing fee deducted if processed after owner receives payout. Direct to Early Return Refunds Policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner asking about sales tax responsibilities ---
Inform that Neighbors Trailer assumes responsibility for sales tax on bookings. Owners don't need to handle sales tax - the platform takes care of it completely.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Toll charges and toll program ---
For toll bills: Owner can email toll bill to support and NT will attempt to charge renter. Before sending bill, owner should enroll in free toll program to prevent future issues. Enrollment steps: Login to account > Enroll in Our Free Toll Program > Click/Tap Here > Enroll Now > Add License Plate > Enroll. Toll program is free with no subscription costs.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Corporate/government payment methods or purchase orders ---
NT can set up corporate accounts for organizations requiring purchase order payments. Ask if they have new supplier setup forms that need completion. Corporate billing arrangements are possible for qualified organizations.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Cancellation fees and who pays ---
If renter cancels, they pay cancellation fees. If owner needs to cancel due to renter's issue (like missing brake controller), renter should cancel from their end. If owner cancels, they forfeit payout unless partial refund is arranged. Booking fees are generally non-refundable.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Extension charges ---
Extensions cannot be placed without charges as they include booking fees, potential taxes, and insurance charges. Renter and owner must work out extension arrangements directly.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Deposit refund timing ---
Security deposits are refunded when owner marks rental as completed. Refunds typically take 3-5 business days to appear on credit card statement after processing.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Circumvention penalties and deductions ---
Owners are charged $25 deduction for attempting to take rentals off-platform (circumvention). This applies even if rental doesn't happen. Policy enforced to protect platform investments and be fair to other owners. Owners must keep all rentals on platform and not share direct contact info before booking acceptance.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Payment method management for renters ---
Renters can view and manage payment methods in their account under "My Payment Methods" which shows saved cards and default payment option.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Coupon code issues ---
Only owners can control coupon settings. If coupon appears used but transaction failed, renter must ask owner to reset coupon or create new one. Customer service cannot reset coupon usage.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Failed payment notifications and bank account issues ---
When multiple payout failures occur, check bank account information is correct. Common issues include wrong account number length. Provide step-by-step instructions to update bank info or offer to update manually with correct details.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Rental pricing and rate calculations ---
For pricing inquiries, direct customers to search trailers in their area on homepage. For specific booking cost breakdowns, can provide itemized receipts upon request with booking ID.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Account suspension for payment issues ---
Accounts may be suspended if bank account not connected within required timeframe after booking cancellation. Can reinstate account once proper bank connection is completed. Account compliance required for active status.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: ID verification payment issues ---
If customer has trouble with ID verification during payment process, have them contact support directly. Technical issues with photo verification need individual troubleshooting assistance.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Customer sees a charge on their credit card but booking is still pending ---
Explain that payment is only authorized (not actually charged) until a booking is accepted by the owner. If the customer cancels a pending booking or it is rejected by the owner without being accepted, the authorization hold is immediately released and the money will go back to their card. However, it may take 12-24 hours to reflect on their statement. If the booking has been accepted by the owner, the funds are fully processed and subject to the cancellation policy.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Customer asking about sales tax on rental ---
Sales tax requirements vary by state. States that have not met the required threshold do not require sales tax collection. For example, Idaho does not require sales tax for bookings. Confirm with the customer their state and explain whether sales tax applies to their booking.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer says they completed payment information but received no verification or confirmation ---
Check the customer's account for any reservation or payment under their name. If no reservation exists, recommend they try the booking process again. Ask for their booking ID number or other identifying information to investigate further.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner asking about payment for completed rental going to closed bank account ---
Ask for the booking ID number to investigate. Owner payouts are automatically initiated when a rental is marked as completed and may take 1-3 business days to appear in the updated bank account. If the payment went to a closed account, the owner will need to update their banking information in their account settings.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer asking about tax exemption or reimbursement for tax amount ---
Explain that there are no applied taxes to bookings for renters. The fees associated with bookings are: 1) Trailer Rental Fee (set by owner), 2) Deposit (set by owner, refundable), 3) Booking Fee (10% of rental fee with $20 minimum, non-refundable), 4) Deposit Processing Fee (3% of total rental, non-refundable). No sales tax is charged that would qualify for tax exemption.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer asking if charge will be released when booking is pending ---
If the booking is still pending and the owner hasn't accepted it, the authorization hold will be released within 24 hours if cancelled or rejected. If the owner has accepted the booking, the funds are fully processed and subject to the cancellation policy: Cancel 72+ hours prior = 75% refund, Cancel 48-72 hours prior = 50% refund, Cancel 24-48 hours prior = 25% refund, No refund for cancellations within 24 hours, No refund for same day bookings, Platform fees are non-refundable after booking acceptance, No-show = cancellation without notice.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer asking why deposit wasn't refunded ---
The deposit refund is automatically initiated when the trailer owner marks the rental as completed and may take 4-7 business days to appear on the customer's statement. The owner must end the rental in the system to trigger the deposit refund.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner requesting to remove add-on charges from customer's booking ---
Staff can process refunds for add-ons when the owner ends the rental. There is a 10% admin fee deducted from the refund amount. The owner should contact support via live chat or email when they want to process the add-on refund. Provide the booking ID number for processing.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Owner asking about additional charges for damages beyond deposit amount ---
When damage costs exceed the deposit amount, the additional amount will be charged to the renter's card. For example, if damage costs $241.40 and the deposit was $200, an additional $41.40 will be charged. The owner should provide documentation of replacement costs to support additional charges.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer getting credit card errors during booking process ---
Common payment errors include incorrect CVC code entry. If customer reports trying multiple cards from different banks, check the specific error messages. Most payment failures are due to incorrect CVC entry. Ask the customer to verify they are entering the correct CVC code.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: How owner payouts work ---
Once a rental is marked as completed by the owner, the payout is automatically initiated and may take 1-3 business days to reflect in the owner's bank account. There is no manual download or transfer option - payouts are automatic when rentals are completed.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Toll fees during rental ---
For toll charges incurred during a rental, the owner should provide the toll bill to support, who will charge the renter and process a payout to the owner to cover the toll fees. If the renter's card has insufficient funds, the owner can dispute the toll as a leased vehicle or contact support to invoice the renter. Owners can enroll in the automated Toll Transfer Program for free to automate this process. Some toll authorities may not participate in the program, and activation may take 2-3 days after enrollment.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Customer asking about purchase orders or vendor setup ---
Neighbors Trailer cannot accept purchase orders (POs) and requires a credit card to be charged upfront. While the company can complete vendor paperwork, payment must still be made via credit card at the time of booking.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer cannot login and unsure if payment went through ---
If customer cannot login, direct them to use the "Forgot Your Password?" option to reset their password. Ask for their booking ID number to verify payment status and booking details.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Late return and payment for additional time ---
For renters who return late beyond their paid time, recommend the owner submit a Deposit Deduction Claim (DDC) when ending the rental. This allows the owner to withhold some or all of the deposit amount to cover the cost of additional rental time. All payments must go through the app - cash payments are not permitted.

--- [Owner] [payments] Q: Circumvention policy and fees ---
Attempting to circumvent the platform by conducting business outside the app (such as offering direct contact or rentals outside the platform) results in fees. The policy applies regardless of whether the rental actually happens. There is a $20 minimum deduction from payouts for circumvention violations, though this may be reduced from the full amount stated in the Abuse of Services Policy. Direct owners to read the full policy at https://neighborstrailer.com/terms.

--- [Renter] [payments] Q: Customer asking about booking completion process ---
After entering booking dates and selecting a pick-up time, customers should see a "Book Now" button. If they don't see this button, ask them to send a screenshot of what they see to troubleshoot the issue. The booking can be completed on both the website and mobile app.

--- [Both] [payments] Q: Questions about platform fees ---
The platform takes 20% of each rental from owners. For renters, fees include: Booking Fee (10% of rental fee with $20 minimum, non-refundable), Deposit Processing Fee (3% of total rental, non-refundable). Credit card processing is free for owners.

--- [Internal] [payments] Q: Law enforcement requests for payment/booking information ---
For legitimate law enforcement requests regarding stolen trailers or other investigations, provide booking activity details, renter identification verification images, and any relevant communication logs. Include the renter's license verification image and address information that matches their driver's license. Document the timeline of booking acceptance, rental start, and expected return dates.

--- [Both] [damage-claims] Q: What should I check before towing a trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-should-I-check-before-towing-a-trailer--203
Before towing, take a few minutes to complete this safety checklist. A proper pre-trip inspection can help prevent accidents, equipment damage, and roadside issues.

Download our printable Pre-Trip Tow Safety Card (PDF) for a quick glovebox version of this checklist.

 

1. Verify Your Tow Vehicle

• Confirm your vehicle’s towing capacity is sufficient for the loaded trailer.
• Check that your receiver hitch size matches your ball mount.
• Ensure your vehicle has a brake controller if required.
• Inspect mirrors and adjust for proper rear visibility.
 

2. Confirm Proper Hitch & Coupler Connection

• Verify you are using the correct hitch ball size (1-7/8", 2", or 2-5/16").
• Ensure the hitch ball is properly torqued and tightened.
• Insert the ball mount fully into the receiver and secure it with a hitch pin and clip.
• Open the trailer coupler latch before lowering it onto the hitch ball.
• Lower the coupler completely onto the ball.
• Close and secure the coupler latch.
• Insert a safety pin or coupler lock, if available.
• Perform a gentle pull test to confirm the trailer is securely attached.
 

3. Attach Safety Chains & Wiring

• Cross the safety chains underneath the trailer tongue (forming an “X”).
• Attach chains securely to the tow vehicle.
• Ensure chains have enough slack for turning, but do not drag.
• Connect the trailer light plug.
• Test:• Brake lights
• Turn signals
• Running lights
• Hazard lights

 

4. Inspect Tires & Brakes

• Check tire pressure on both the trailer and tow vehicle.
• Inspect tires for visible damage or excessive wear.
• Confirm lug nuts appear secure.
• Verify trailer brakes are functioning properly (if equipped).
 

5. Check Load & Weight Distribution

• Confirm the trailer is not overloaded (verify GVWR on the VIN sticker).
• Follow the 60/40 rule:• 60% of weight toward the front
• 40% toward the rear

• Ensure cargo is evenly distributed side-to-side.
• Secure all cargo with straps or tie-downs.
• Double-check that nothing can shift during transit.
 

6. Final Walk-Around

• Raise and secure the trailer jack fully.
• Remove wheel chocks.
• Confirm ramps or doors are closed and latched.
• Make sure license plates are visible.
• Perform one last visual inspection before driving away.
 

Pro Tip:
After driving a short distance (5–10 miles), pull over and recheck your hitch connection, straps, and load security.

Taking a few extra minutes before departure can significantly improve safety and reduce the risk of towing-related issues.

Want a deeper breakdown of towing capacity, braking requirements, and real-world safety examples?
Read our Ultimate Trailer Towing Safety Guide.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: How do I change the booking date? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-I-change-the-booking-date--201
After a booking has been accepted, you can request a change to the pickup date. The trailer owner will receive your request and can choose to accept or reject it.

To complete the date change, the total number of rental days must remain the same.

How to request a date change

• From your Dashboard, select My Bookings.
• Open the booking you’d like to update.
• From the booking details page, select Request Date Change.
• Choose the new start date and submit your request.
Once submitted, the trailer owner will be notified and will respond to your request.

--- [Renter] [payment] Q: How Can I Update My Payment Method? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-to-Update-Your-Payment-Method-198
You can add or update a payment method in your Neighbors Trailer account at any time using the mobile app or website.

 

From the Neighbors Trailer App

• Open the Neighbors Trailer app and sign in.
• Tap More.
• Select Payment Methods.
• Tap the + (plus) button.
• Enter your new payment details.
• Tap Save.
Your new payment method will be available immediately for future bookings, extensions, add-ons, and other charges.

Tip: Make sure your default payment method is current to avoid booking interruptions or failed charges.

 

From the Neighbors Trailer Website

• Sign in to your account at NeighborsTrailer.com.
• Select Payment Methods from your account menu.
• Click Add Card.
• Enter your new payment details.
• Click Save.
Your updated payment method will be available immediately.

If you experience any issues adding or updating a payment method, please contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Owner] [how-to] Q: How Do I Run a Booking History Report? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-To-Run-a-Booking-History-Report-197
Owners can view and download their booking history by running the Revenue Classification report. This report provides a detailed breakdown of completed bookings and related revenue.

From the Neighbors Trailer App

• Open the Neighbors Trailer app and sign in.
• Tap More in the bottom navigation.
• Select Report.
• Tap Revenue Classification.
• Use any available filters (such as date range) to refine your results.
• View the report on screen or export/download it as needed.

From the Web

• Go to neighborstrailer.com and sign in to your owner account.
• From the main menu, select Report.
• Click Revenue Classification.
• Apply filters (for example, date range) to see the booking history you need.
• View the report or download it for your records.

Tips

Use date filters to quickly find bookings for a specific month, quarter, or year.

Downloaded reports are helpful for accounting, taxes, and performance tracking.

If you need additional help, contact Neighbors Trailer Support.

--- [Both] [general] Q: What is the Protection Package? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Protection-Package-196
Introducing the New NT Protect™ Protection Package

We’re excited to announce the launch of an all-new Protection Package from NT Protect, a Neighbors Trailer company, underwritten by our licensed insurance partner.

This updated Protection Package fully replaces the existing insurance coverage — bringing broader protection, simplified eligibility, and peace of mind for every trailer rental on Neighbors Trailer.

This change took effect November 10, 2025 on the web and November 12, 2025 on the mobile apps.  

What’s New

Coverage Limit: Up to $25,000 per covered loss
Deductible: $500 per claim
Expanded Eligibility:

• All trailer types are eligible, regardless of title status.
• Trailers already insured under another policy remain eligible for damage protection under NT Protect.
• Age Requirement for Coverage: 21 years of age or older
• Expanded Availability: Coverage now extends across all 50 U.S. states and Canada.
These changes are designed to provide broader, more flexible protection and make coverage accessible to more trailer owners across the Neighbors Trailer community.

Why NT Protect™

Accidents can happen — even with experienced drivers. The NT Protect™ Protection Package helps reduce the financial risk for both renters and owners when unexpected damage or theft occurs during a verified rental.

With every eligible rental:

• Renters enjoy peace of mind knowing covered incidents are handled quickly and fairly.
• Owners gain protection against out-of-pocket repair costs if a trailer is damaged or stolen.
• Everyone benefits from a streamlined claims process managed directly by NT Protect.

How It Works

When a rental is booked through Neighbors Trailer, NT Protect™ automatically applies to eligible reservations.
If a covered accident, theft, or damage occurs during the rental period, NT Protect™ helps cover repair or reimbursement up to the trailer’s Actual Cash Value (ACV) — subject to the $25,000 limit and $500 deductible.

NT Protect's insurance partners administer all claims directly, ensuring a fast, fair, and consistent experience for every user.

What’s Covered

• Accidental physical damage to the trailer during use
• Theft or vandalism during an active rental period
• Coverage across the U.S. and Canada
(See official program terms for complete details and exclusions.)

What’s Not Covered

• Routine maintenance or mechanical failure
• Normal wear and tear
• Unauthorized or illegal use
• Loss of use or downtime
• Fraudulent or intentional acts
(See official program terms for complete details and exclusions.)

A Program Built on Real Protection

NT Protect™ is not insurance sold to renters or owners.
Coverage is provided to NT Protect through licensed insurance partners, and benefits are extended to eligible users under the program’s terms.

This structure allows NT Protect to:

• Deliver protection benefits efficiently,
• Manage all claims internally, and
• Maintain compliance with insurance regulations.

When Does This Take Effect?

The new NT Protect™ Protection Package takes effect on November 10, 2025.
Exact program terms and full coverage details will be made available at that time.

If you have questions, please contact our customer service team at service@neighborstrailer.com.

How to File a Claim

You may file a claim from any On Rent or Completed booking by selecting the “File Claim” button on the booking details page.

NT Protect's insurance partners will evaluate and process the claim.

Transparency. Confidence. Protection That Travels With You.

Whether you’re renting to move, haul, or explore, NT Protect™ ensures every trip through Neighbors Trailer comes with trusted, built-in protection.

Rent with confidence.
List with protection.

--- [Owner] [payment] Q: How Can I Cancel a Booking? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Can-I-Cancel-a-Booking--182
If you choose to cancel a booking after it has been accepted, a cancellation fee may apply in accordance with our Terms of Use.

Owner-Initiated Cancellations

If you cancel a booking after accepting it:

• 30% of the rental amount will be withheld from your next payout.
• If you have an unpaid cancellation balance, you will be required to enter payment information and pay the cancellation fee before continuing to use certain features.

Renter-Initiated Cancellations

If the renter decides to cancel, they must cancel the booking directly from their own account. Owners cannot cancel on behalf of the renter to avoid penalties.

How do I cancel a booking?

• Go to the applicable booking details page.
• Select Cancel Booking.
• Confirm the cancellation.

Is there a booking completion requirement?

Yes. Trailer owners must accept and successfully complete at least 70% of the bookings they receive to maintain active account status.

Repeated cancellations may impact account standing.

For additional details, please review the Booking Cancellation by Owner Policy in Section 36 of our
Terms of Use.

If you have questions about cancellations, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Owner] [deposit-refund] Q: How can I issue a partial refund to a renter? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-issue-a-partial-refund-to-the-renter--181
Partial refunds may be issued if authorized by the trailer owner and must follow platform policy.

When Can a Partial Refund Be Issued?

• The trailer owner must approve the refund.
• The refund must be processed before the rental is ended in the system.
• Refunds are issued directly from the owner’s account through the booking page.

Important Limitations

• Booking fees, taxes, and Protection Package fees are non-refundable.
• The maximum refundable amount will not exceed 75% of the rental amount.
• If a refund is processed manually after the rental has been ended, a $25 refund processing fee will be deducted from the renter’s refundable amount.

How to Issue a Partial Refund

• Open the booking details page.
• Select the refund option (if available).
• Enter the approved refund amount.
• Confirm and submit the refund before ending the rental.
For more information about early returns or partial refunds, please review the Early Return Refunds Policy in Section 20 of our Terms of Use.

If you have questions about issuing a refund, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Owner] [account] Q: How Does the Toll Program Work? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Does-the-Toll-Program-Work--175
Once a trailer is enrolled in the Neighbors Trailer Toll Program, toll tracking is managed automatically during active rentals.

How It Works

• The trailer’s license plate is activated with toll authorities when the Owner begins the rental in the system.
• The license plate is deactivated when the Owner properly ends the rental.
• Neighbors Trailer collects toll charges directly from the renter.
During the active rental period, Neighbors Trailer assumes financial responsibility for toll fees associated with the enrolled trailer’s license plate.

What This Means for Owners

• You will not receive toll bills for properly started and ended rentals.
• You do not need to contact the renter about toll charges.
• Toll fees are handled directly through the platform.

Important

The rental must be properly started and ended in the system for toll tracking to activate and deactivate correctly.

If you have questions about the Toll Program or toll charges, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

Toll Authorities & Coverage Limitations

Neighbors Trailer’s Toll Program does not guarantee coverage for all toll authorities. In certain cases, toll charges may still be billed directly to the trailer owner.

Coverage limitations may apply depending on the toll authority, region, or international crossing.

Examples of toll systems where coverage may not be guaranteed include:

• 407 ETR (Ontario)
• 495 Express Lanes (VA)
• Chesapeake Expressway (VA)
• Elizabeth River Tunnels (VA)
• E-ZPass NJ (NJ)
• DelDOT (DE)
• Pocahontas Parkway 895 (VA)
• South Bay Expressway (CA)
• South Norfolk Jordan Bridge (VA)
• Certain toll plazas in Florida
• Other U.S. and international crossings
This list is subject to change without prior notice.

Important

If a toll authority is not fully supported under the Toll Program, toll charges may be billed directly to the trailer owner.

--- [Both] [deposit-refund] Q: How can I file a damage claim? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-file-an-insurance-claim--170
If damage, loss, or unpaid charges occur during a rental, you may submit a Deposit Deduction Claim when ending the rental.

Claims must be supported with documentation and photos.

When to File a Claim

You should file a claim if:

• The trailer is returned with new damage
• Equipment or accessories are missing
• There are unpaid rental fees
• There are other documented losses related to the rental
Claims should be submitted at the time you end the rental.

 

How to File a Deposit Deduction Claim

From the Neighbors Trailer App

• Select Bookings.
• Open the applicable booking under Current.
• Tap End Rental.
• Select the Deposit Deduction Claim option.
• Enter the required details describing the damage or loss.
• Upload supporting photos.
• Tap End Rental to submit the claim.

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select Bookings.
• Open the applicable booking under Current Bookings.
• Click End Rental.
• Check the Deposit Deduction Claim box.
• Enter the required information.
• Upload supporting photos.
• Select End Rental to submit the claim.
 

What Happens Next?

• The renter will be notified of the claim.
• The renter may review or dispute the claim within 24 hours of your submission.
• Neighbors Trailer will review the submitted information and make a determination based on platform policies.
 

NT Protect Protection Package Claims (For Damages Over $500)

If damages exceed $500, and the rental included the NT Protect Protection Package, you may file a protection claim in addition to your deposit deduction claim.

 

When to File an NT Protect Claim

You may file an NT Protect claim when:

• Verified damages exceed $500
• The renter purchased NT Protect at the time of booking
• The damage occurred during the active rental period
 

How to File an NT Protect Claim

• Gather supporting documentation, including:• Before-and-after photos
• Detailed description of the damage
• Repair estimates or invoices (if available)

• Go to the booking.
• Select File Claim
• Submit any additional documentation requested during the review process.
 

Important

• NT Protect claims are subject to review and verification.
• Coverage applies only to eligible damages occurring during the rental period.
• Failure to properly begin and end the rental in the system may impact protection eligibility.
If you are unsure whether a situation qualifies for NT Protect coverage, contact Neighbors Trailer Support before proceeding.

--- [Owner] [deposit-refund] Q: How can I recover damage costs that exceed the deposit? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-recover-damage-costs-that-exceed-my-deposit--168
