--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if my trailer is not returned on time? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-can-I-do-if-my-trailer-is-not-returned--166
If a trailer is not returned by the scheduled end date and time, you must follow documented communication and escalation steps before taking further action.

In most cases, late returns occur because the renter forgot to submit an extension request. However, all communication and actions should be handled carefully and documented.

 

Quick Action Checklist

>Confirm the scheduled return date and time in the booking.
>Send a message through the Neighbors Trailer message portal.
>Attempt phone or text contact if no response.
>Document all communication attempts.
>Provide written notice with a clear response deadline.
>Send a final notice before terminating the rental.
>Terminate the rental in writing if necessary.
>Contact law enforcement only after proper notice and documentation.

Step 1: Attempt Immediate Contact

If the trailer is overdue:

• Send a message through the Neighbors Trailer message portal requesting an update.
• Attempt to contact the renter by phone or text.
• Document all communication attempts.
If you do not have the renter’s phone number, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

 

Step 2: Provide Written Notice

If there is no response, send a written message giving a clear and reasonable deadline for the renter to respond.

Example:

“Your rental was due back on [date/time]. I have attempted to contact you and have not received a response. Please respond by [specific time] or the rental will be terminated and escalated.”

Always include a specific date and time.

 

Step 3: Terminate the Rental

If the renter does not respond by your stated deadline:

• Send a final written notice terminating the rental.
• Provide a short final deadline for immediate contact.
All termination notices should be documented in writing through the platform whenever possible.

IMPORTANT: Terminating the rental does not mean closing out the booking in the system.

Terminating the rental is a formal written notice to the renter that they no longer have the legal right to possess the trailer.

Do not close the booking until the trailer has been returned or the situation has been properly resolved.

 

Step 4: Escalate if Necessary

If the renter fails to respond after documented communication and deadlines:

• You may contact local law enforcement to report the trailer as stolen.
 

Important Legal Considerations

• Once reported stolen, the matter becomes criminal.
• You should stop charging rental fees after reporting the trailer stolen.
• Laws vary by state and jurisdiction. Some states require specific notice periods before a rental may be legally terminated and reported as stolen.
• Owners are responsible for complying with applicable local laws.
If you are unsure how to proceed at any stage, contact Neighbors Trailer Support before escalating the matter.

--- [Both] [damage-claims] Q: What are the 3 most important trailer safety tips? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/3-Most-Important-Safety-Tips-165
Before towing, take a few minutes to review these essential safety tips to help reduce the risk of accidents and equipment damage.

1. Make sure you have the right tow vehicle and equipment

• Verify your vehicle’s towing capacity.
• Use the correct hitch and ball size for the trailer.
• Confirm you have a brake controller, if required. If your vehicle is not equipped with one, consider using a wireless Bluetooth brake controller.
Using the proper equipment is critical for safe towing.

2. Understand the trailer’s weight limits and setup requirements

• Choose a trailer with enough weight capacity to support your load.• Weight Capacity = GVWR – Empty Weight

• Never overload a trailer.
• Follow the 60/40 loading rule: place approximately 60% of the load toward the front of the trailer and 40% toward the rear to maintain proper tongue weight.
When connecting the trailer:

• Ensure the coupler latch is open before lowering it onto the hitch ball.
• Securely close and lock the coupler latch.
• Attach safety chains (crossed underneath the tongue).
• Connect the light plug.
• Perform a full pre-trip inspection, including tires, lights, brakes, hitch connection, and load security.
Always double-check all connections before driving away.

3. Practice safe towing habits on the road

• Drive at a safe, controlled speed.
• Stay in the right lane when possible.
• Maintain extra distance from other vehicles.
• Take wider turns to avoid curbs and obstacles.
• Inspect the trailer and load at each stop.
• Use a spotter when backing up whenever possible.
These quick safety tips are a great starting point before towing.

For a more detailed breakdown of towing capacity limits, braking requirements, speed safety, and real-world examples, review our Ultimate Trailer Towing Safety Guide.

You can also watch our safety video: Prepare Your Rental | Neighbors Trailer.

--- [Owner] [cancellation] Q: How can a renter switch to a different trailer I have listed? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-a-renter-exchange-a-trailer--162
If a booking has already been accepted and the renter would like to switch to another trailer you have available, the exchange can be completed without canceling the booking.

The trailer exchange can be processed from either the renter’s account or the owner’s account.

There is no fee to exchange one trailer for another. If there is a price difference, it is based solely on the rental rate of the new trailer.

 

How to Exchange the Trailer

From the Website:

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select Bookings.
• Choose the booking ID to open the booking details page.
• Click Change Trailer.
• Complete the exchange process.
From the App:

• Select Bookings.
• Open the applicable booking.
• Tap Change Trailer.
• Complete the exchange process.
 

Pricing Adjustments

If there is a price difference between the two trailers:

• The renter will see either a refund or an additional charge during the exchange process.
• The difference will appear on the booking receipt as “Transferred Adjustment Amount.”
If you have questions about switching trailers or how pricing adjustments are calculated, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Renter] [damage-claims] Q: Am I responsible for tire damage? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Am-I-responsible-for-tire-damage--158
Responsibility for tire damage depends on the cause of the damage.

When is the renter responsible?

The renter is responsible if the damage occurred during the rental and was caused by use, including:

• Hitting a curb or road hazard
• A nail or puncture
• Overloading the trailer
• Driving at speeds beyond the tire’s rated limit
• Any impact-related damage
If the damage was caused by how the trailer was operated or loaded during the rental, the renter may be responsible for replacing the tire.

 

When is the trailer owner responsible?

The trailer owner is responsible if the damage was due to normal wear and tear, age, or improper maintenance, including:

• Tire is 3 years old or older
• Tire defects
• Low tread
• Improper installation
Tires should not exceed 3 years of age to help ensure safe towing.

 

How do I check the tire’s age?

You can determine a tire’s age by locating the 4-digit DOT date code on the tire’s sidewall.

• The first two digits represent the week the tire was manufactured.
• The last two digits represent the year of manufacture.
For example:
If the code reads 2522, the tire was manufactured in the 25th week of 2022.

 

Tips to help prevent tire damage

To reduce the risk of tire-related issues during your rental:

• Check tire pressure before departure.
• Inspect tires for visible cracks, bulges, or low tread.
• Avoid overloading the trailer (verify GVWR on the VIN sticker).
• Drive at safe speeds, especially on highways.
• Avoid curbs, potholes, and road debris when possible.
• Recheck tires during long trips or after driving several miles.
Taking a few minutes for a pre-trip inspection can help prevent roadside delays and unexpected expenses.

 

Important

This is a general guideline to help determine responsibility. Our Terms of Use may contain additional language that further define responsibility in specific situations.

If there is a dispute regarding tire damage, Neighbors Trailer will review the circumstances and supporting documentation before making a determination.

--- [Renter] [listing] Q: How do I create a booking? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-create-a-booking--157
Follow these steps to book a trailer rental on Neighbors Trailer:

 

Step 1: Search for a Trailer

• Visit NeighborsTrailer.com.
• Enter your city and state in the Location search field.
• Click Search to view available trailers in your area.
 

Step 2: Select a Trailer

• Browse the available listings.
• Choose the trailer that best fits your needs.
• Review details such as size, weight capacity, pricing, and pickup location.
 

Step 3: Choose Dates & Start the Booking

• Select your desired rental dates from the calendar.
• Choose your pickup time.
• Click Book Now.
 

Step 4: Complete Required Information

• Enter all required fields.
• Confirm your email address or phone number.
• Upload a photo of your valid driver’s license to complete identity verification.
 

Step 5: Enter Payment Information

• Enter your payment details.
• Select Pay to submit your booking request.
Your card will be authorized at the time of booking but will not be charged until the trailer owner accepts the booking.

You will receive a notification by text and/or email once the booking is accepted.

After acceptance:

• The trailer owner’s contact information will be automatically shared with you.
• If the owner has disabled automatic sharing, they will manually release their contact information.
 

Deposit Refunds

If the trailer is returned without incident, the deposit refund will be initiated after the rental is properly closed.

Please allow 3–5 business days for the refund to appear on your statement.

If you have questions during the booking process, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: How can I dispute a deposit deduction claim? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-dispute-a-deposit-deduction-claim--155
If a Deposit Deduction Claim is submitted, you will be notified by text and email. The notification will include a link where you can review:

• The amount requested
• Photos submitted by the Owner
• A description of the claimed damage or charge
Under our Terms, the trailer’s condition at pickup is established by the Owner’s pre-rental photos uploaded at the start of the Rental Period. If damage is present at return that was not visible in those pre-rental photos, it is presumed to have occurred during the rental.

If you believe you are not responsible for the claim, you must submit your dispute through the Platform within 24 hours of receiving notice of the claim.

 

What should I include in my dispute?

Because the rental condition is documented at pickup, you should provide evidence showing that:

• The damage was already present at pickup, or
• The claim is inconsistent with the documented rental timeline.
Strong supporting documentation includes:

• Timestamped photos taken before or at pickup clearly showing the area now claimed as damaged
• Messages exchanged through the Platform noting condition concerns at pickup
• Completed inspection checklists
• Any other relevant documentation (receipts, written statements, etc.)
If no dispute is submitted within 24 hours, the claim will be reviewed and finalized based on the available records.

 

How to review or dispute a claim

From the Web:

• Go to Dashboard
• Select My Bookings
• Click Past
• Select the relevant booking ID
• Scroll to Booking Activity and select Deduction Claim
• Click Contest Claim and enter your comments

From the Mobile App:

• Tap Bookings
• Select Past
• Choose the relevant booking
• Scroll to Booking Activity
• Select Deduction Claim
• Tap Contest Claim and submit your comments
 

How claims are reviewed

If a claim is disputed, the Neighbors Trailer team will review all submitted information from both the Renter and the Trailer Owner.

This may include:

• Pre-rental and post-rental photos
• Timestamped documentation
• Rental condition records
• Communication through the Platform
• Any additional evidence provided
If necessary, we may contact either party for clarification before issuing a final administrative determination.

 

Common reasons for deposit deductions

Deposit deductions are typically submitted for:

• Physical damage to the trailer
• Missing equipment or accessories
• Cleaning beyond normal wear and tear
• Late returns outside the agreed rental period
• Policy violations during the rental
To help avoid disputes, we strongly recommend:

• Taking clear, timestamped photos of the trailer at pickup and return
• Reviewing the trailer carefully before the rental is marked “On Rent”
• Communicating any concerns immediately through the booking platform

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I Don't See My Listing ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/I-Don't-See-My-Listing-151
You can check the status of your listing at any time by following the steps below.

From the Owner App

• Select More
• Select Trailers
View the status of each listing shown with a light green or red highlight

From the Web

• Go to your Dashboard
• Select Trailers
• Select Trailer List
View the status of each listing shown with a light green or red highlight

 

Listing Status Definitions

• Approved – Your listing is live and able to receive bookings.
• Pending – Your listing is under manual review and should be approved soon.
• Draft – Your listing has not been submitted for review yet.
• Rejected – Your listing did not meet minimum requirements. You may contact our customer support team for details on what needs to be corrected before resubmitting.
 

Important Tips Before Submitting Your Listing

To avoid delays in approval, make sure the following are completed:

• No contact information in photos – Do not include phone numbers, company names, or other contact details in trailer images.  If you are unable to remove contact information from photos, this will be done for you during the review process.
• Full address entered – Ensure your complete address is filled in under the Location field.
• Correct VIN – Enter the accurate 17-character VIN.
• Weight Capacity – List only the load weight the trailer can safely carry, not the trailer’s total weight.
• Profile & ID Verification – Your profile must be complete and ID verification finished.
If these items are missing, approval may take 1–2 days instead of 1–2 hours. Listings are reviewed during normal business hours only. Providing complete and accurate information helps your listing get approved as quickly as possible.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How It Works ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-It-Works-150
Neighbors Trailer is a peer-to-peer marketplace that connects trailer owners with renters in their local area. Owners create a listing with photos, descriptions, pricing, and availability, while renters search for trailers that meet their needs and submit booking requests through the platform. Once a request is approved, payment is processed securely and both parties can message each other directly to coordinate pickup and return details. After the rental is completed, funds are released to the owner and both parties can leave reviews to help build trust within the community.

Safety is built into every step of the Neighbors Trailer process. Secure, on-platform payments help protect both owners and renters, while verified accounts and transparent reviews promote accountability. Keeping communication and documentation within the platform provides a clear record of agreements, pickup times, and return conditions. Neighbors Trailer also offers support throughout the rental period to help resolve issues quickly and fairly, giving both owners and renters added confidence when sharing or booking a trailer.

--- [Owner] [account] Q: How do I leave a review for a renter? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-can-I-leave-a-review-for-a-renter--144
After a rental has been completed, Owners can leave a review for the renter through the Neighbors Trailer app or website.

Reviews help maintain a safe, transparent, and trusted rental community.

From the Neighbors Trailer App

Open the app and sign in.

• Select Bookings.
• Tap Past.
• Select the completed booking.
• Tap Add Review.
Submit your rating and comments.

 

From the Website

Sign in to your Owner account at NeighborsTrailer.com.

• Go to My Bookings.
• Select Past Bookings.
• Click the completed booking.
• Select Post a Review.
Enter your rating and comments, then submit.

 

Review Guidelines

Reviews help build trust within the Neighbors Trailer community. All reviews should be honest, factual, and based on the actual rental experience.

 

What to Include in a Review

We encourage Owners and Renters to share:

• Communication quality
• Timeliness (pickup and return)
• Condition of the trailer or vehicle
• Compliance with rental terms
• Overall experience
Reviews should be specific and based on firsthand experience.

 

What Not to Include

Reviews must not contain:

• False or misleading statements
• Threats, harassment, or abusive language
• Discriminatory or offensive content
• Personal information (phone numbers, addresses, etc.)
• Legal claims or accusations of criminal conduct
 

Fair & Accurate Reviews

• Reviews should reflect your direct experience.
• Retaliatory reviews are discouraged.
• If a dispute is ongoing, keep review comments factual and professional.
Neighbors Trailer may remove reviews that violate platform policies.

 

Reporting a Review

If you believe a review violates these guidelines, contact Neighbors Trailer Support. Include the booking ID and a brief explanation of your concern.

In the event of eligible damages, a $500 deductible applies.

--- [Both] [extension] Q: Is my trailer covered with the Protection Package between rentals? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Is-my-trailer-covered-with-insurance-between-rentals--124
No. The Protection Package only applies during an active rental period.

Coverage begins when the rental is properly started in the system and ends when the rental is properly closed.

The Protection Package does not provide coverage:

• Between bookings
• Non-extended rentals
• While the trailer is stored
• During maintenance or repairs
• During personal use by the owner
• If the rental is not properly started or ended in the system
Owners are responsible for maintaining their own insurance coverage for periods outside of active rentals.

If you have questions about Protection Package eligibility or coverage timing, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

For Protection Package coverage to apply, the individual picking up and operating the trailer must be the renter named on the booking.

If someone other than the named renter picks up or operates the trailer, Protection Package coverage may not apply.

To ensure eligibility and proper documentation, the driver must:

• Be listed on the booking
• Complete required ID verification
• Meet all renter eligibility requirements
If you have questions about driver eligibility or coverage requirements, contact Neighbors Trailer Support before releasing the trailer.

--- [Both] [listing] Q: What fees should I be aware of? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Booking-Fees-112
When booking a trailer on Neighbors Trailer, your total cost may include the following fees:

Trailer Rental Fee

This is the daily, weekly, or monthly rate set by the trailer owner.
The rental rate is displayed on the listing page before booking.

Refundable Security Deposit

The deposit amount is set by the trailer owner and is shown on the listing page.

The deposit is refundable after the trailer is returned without damage, loss, or unpaid charges. Refunds are initiated once the rental is properly ended in the system.

Booking Fee

Neighbors Trailer charges a booking fee to help cover platform operating costs.

• The booking fee is 10% of the rental fee, with a $10 minimum.
• This fee is non-refundable once the booking is accepted.

Deposit Processing Fee

A 3% deposit processing fee may apply.
This fee is non-refundable.

Protection Package Fee

A variable Protection Package fee may apply.
This fee provides rental protection coverage for both the renter and the trailer owner during the rental period.

Taxes

If required by your state or local jurisdiction, applicable sales tax may be collected at the time of booking.

Possible Additional Charges

Additional charges may apply if:

• The rental is extended
• The trailer is returned late
• There is damage, loss, or unpaid fees
• Toll charges are incurred (if applicable)
All fees are displayed during the checkout process before you submit your booking request.

If you have questions about fees shown on your booking, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Owner] [account] Q: How do I start a rental from my account? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Can-i-Start-A-Rental-from-my-account--103
Owners must begin the rental in the system at the time the trailer is released to the renter. This records the official start time and documents the trailer’s condition at pickup.

 

From the Neighbors Trailer App

• Open the app and sign in.
• Select Bookings.
• Tap Upcoming.
• Select the booking.
• Tap Begin Rental.
• Upload a minimum of four current photos of the trailer taken at the time of pickup.
• Confirm the current date and time.
• Enter any relevant remarks (optional but recommended).
• Tap Begin Rental to officially start the booking.

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select Bookings.
• Click Upcoming Bookings.
• Select Begin Rental, or click View Booking and then choose Begin Rental.
• Upload a minimum of four current photos of the trailer taken at the time of pickup.
• Confirm the current date and time.
• Enter any relevant remarks (optional but recommended).
• Select Begin Rental to officially start the booking.

Important

Starting the rental in the system documents the trailer’s condition at pickup and records the official rental start time, helping protect both the Owner and the Renter.

For trailers enrolled in the toll program, beginning the rental also activates license plate with toll authorities.

If the rental is not properly started, toll charges may not be recorded correctly. In that case, the Owner may receive the toll bill and be responsible for recovering those charges.

Always begin the rental at the time the trailer is released to the renter.

If you experience any issues starting a rental, contact Neighbors Trailer Support for assistance.

--- [Renter] [general] Q: How much weight can my truck tow? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-much-weight-can-my-truck-tow--93
To determine how much weight your truck can safely tow, you’ll need to locate your vehicle’s towing capacity.

You may find this information:

• On a sticker inside the driver-side door
• In your vehicle’s owner’s manual
• On the manufacturer’s website
The quickest way to find it is often to search online using your vehicle’s year, make, model, and engine type, along with the phrase “towing capacity.”

For example:
“2022 Ford F-150 5.0L towing capacity”

Towing capacity can vary based on engine size, axle ratio, trim level, drivetrain, and factory-installed towing packages.

 

Towing vs. Payload — Quick Formula Guide

1. Total Trailer Weight
Trailer Empty Weight + Cargo = Total Trailer Weight
Must be less than or equal to your Towing Capacity

2. Tongue Weight (Typically 10–15%)
Total Trailer Weight × 10–15% = Tongue Weight

3. Total Payload Used
Tongue Weight + Passengers + Truck Bed Cargo = Total Payload Used
Must be less than or equal to your Payload Capacity

Download our Towing Capacity Quick Calculator Card (PDF) to quickly calculate trailer weight, tongue weight, and payload before towing.

Example

If your truck has:

• Towing Capacity: 8,000 lbs
• Payload Capacity: 1,500 lbs
Trailer weight (loaded): 6,000 lbs
Tongue weight (10%): 600 lbs

If you have 350 lbs of passengers and 200 lbs of cargo:

600 + 350 + 200 = 1,150 lbs total payload used

You would be within both limits.

 

Important:
Never exceed your vehicle’s towing or payload ratings. Overloading can increase stopping distance, reduce steering control, strain your suspension, and create unsafe towing conditions.

If you’re unsure whether your vehicle is properly equipped to tow a specific trailer, consult your vehicle manufacturer or a qualified professional before towing.

Want a deeper breakdown of towing limits, payload calculations, tongue weight, and real-world examples?  Read our full guide: Can Your Vehicle Safely Tow a Trailer?

Before renting, always verify that the vehicle is properly equipped to tow the specific trailer you plan to use.

--- [Both] [general] Q: How should I distribute the weight in a trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Should-I-distribute-the-weight--83
For safe towing, follow the 60/40 rule when loading your trailer:

• Place approximately 60% of the total weight toward the front half of the trailer.
• Place approximately 40% of the total weight toward the rear half of the trailer.

What is tongue weight?

Tongue weight is the downward force the trailer places on the hitch ball of your tow vehicle.

For most trailers, proper tongue weight should be approximately 10–15% of the total loaded trailer weight.

Pro Tip:
Proper tongue weight is critical for safe towing. Too little weight on the tongue can cause trailer sway, while too much weight can overload your vehicle’s rear suspension and reduce steering control. Aim for balanced loading to maintain stability and handling.

Proper weight distribution:

• Improves stability
• Reduces trailer sway
• Increases braking control
• Helps protect your vehicle and trailer
Always secure your load properly and double-check balance before driving. If the trailer begins to sway, safely reduce speed and inspect your load distribution before continuing.

--- [Both] [general] Q: How do I know how much weight the trailer can hold? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-I-know-how-much-weight-the-trailer-will-hold--82
A trailer’s weight capacity can be found on the VIN sticker or a label located near the VIN plate. This sticker is typically placed on the trailer tongue or along the frame on the side of the trailer.

On the sticker, you will see the GVWR (Gross Vehicle Weight Rating).

What is GVWR?

GVWR is the maximum total weight the trailer can safely weigh when fully loaded. This includes:

• The trailer itself
• All cargo
• Equipment and accessories

What is payload (weight capacity)?

Payload capacity is the amount of cargo the trailer can safely carry.

You can calculate it using this formula:

GVWR – Empty Trailer Weight = Payload Capacity

This number tells you how much weight you can safely load onto the trailer.

Important:
The weight capacity listed in the online listing may not always reflect the exact manufacturer specifications. Always verify the trailer’s capacity directly on the VIN sticker before loading to ensure safe towing.

Never exceed the manufacturer’s rated weight limits. Overloading can cause trailer sway, tire failure, brake issues, and unsafe towing conditions.

--- [Both] [listing] Q: What size hitch ball do I need to rent a trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-size-ball-will-i-need--81
The required hitch ball size depends on the specific trailer you are renting. Most trailers use one of the following standard ball sizes:

• 1-7/8 inch
• 2 inch
• 2-5/16 inch
You can usually find the required ball size:

• Stamped on the trailer’s coupler
• Listed in the trailer details on the listing page
Always verify the correct ball size before pickup. Using the wrong hitch ball size can create an unsafe connection and may cause the trailer to disconnect while towing.

 

How do I check my hitch ball size?

To confirm your current ball size:

• Look for the size stamped directly on the top of the hitch ball (for example, “2” or “2-5/16”).
• Check the packaging or receipt if the stamping is difficult to read.
• Make sure you are installing the correct ball mount before pickup.
 

Ball Size vs. Receiver Size — What’s the difference?

• Hitch ball size refers to the diameter of the ball that connects to the trailer coupler.
• Receiver size refers to the square opening on your vehicle’s hitch (commonly 1-1/4 inch or 2 inch).
These are two different measurements. The receiver size determines which ball mount fits your vehicle, while the ball size must match the trailer’s coupler.

 

Pro Tip:
Make sure your hitch ball is properly tightened and torqued according to the manufacturer’s specifications. A loose hitch ball can create a dangerous towing situation.

If you’re unsure which size you need, contact the trailer owner through the booking platform before your rental begins.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: I Can't find my listing in Google search results.  What should I do? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Can't-find-my-listing-in-Google-search-results-79
New listings can take time to be indexed by Google and other search engines. Indexing timelines vary and are not controlled by Neighbors Trailer.

If your listing was recently approved, please allow time for search engines to crawl and rank the page.

Search engines may take several weeks to index and rank new listings.

In the meantime, try the following:

Search Google using a key phrase from your listing title.

Search using a key phrase from your title along with your city and state.

Keep in mind that rankings vary based on location, competition, and search history, and not all listings will appear on the first page of results.

If your listing does not appear after a reasonable indexing period, please contact our customer support team, and we’ll review it.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: What information should I include in the description for my listing? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-information-should-I-include-in-the-description-for-my-listing--75
Your description is one of the most important parts of your listing. Clear, detailed information helps renters feel confident and can increase your chances of receiving bookings.

Consider including the following:

Trailer Features

Highlight built-in features that make your trailer more functional or convenient, such as:

• Spare tire
• Winch
• Tie-down points
• D-rings or E-track
• Drive-over fenders
• Ramp door or side access door
• Electric jack
• Tools for changing a tire
The more specific you are, the fewer questions renters will have before booking.

Trailer Condition

Be transparent about the overall condition of your trailer, such as:

• New
• Like new
• Well-maintained
If your trailer is older, mention your maintenance schedule, recent upgrades, or any improvements that demonstrate reliability. This helps build renter trust.

Accessories & Add-Ons

You may offer additional equipment as optional add-ons. Examples include:

• Straps or chains
• Ball and mount
• Wireless brake controller
• Moving dolly
Clearly state what is included in the base rental and what is an additional charge.

Rental Requirements

Outline any requirements renters must meet, such as:

• Valid driver’s license
• Insurance requirements
• In-state or out-of-state usage limitations
• Signed rental agreement
• Required vehicle type (½-ton, ¾-ton, or 1-ton truck)
Setting expectations upfront helps prevent misunderstandings.

Availability & Scheduling

Let renters know:

• Days and hours the trailer is available
• Minimum rental periods
• Whether you allow same-day bookings or require advance notice
Providing thorough and accurate details helps renters feel confident and can increase your chances of receiving bookings.

Discount availability varies by owner. While discounts aren’t guaranteed, some owners may offer limited-time promotions. You can message the owner to ask if any discounts are currently available.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: What happens if there is an issue with the trailer during my rental? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-happens-if-there-is-an-issue-with-the-trailer-during-my-rental--73
If you experience an issue during your rental, please contact the trailer owner immediately through the booking platform so it can be addressed as quickly as possible.

Rental fees are not automatically refunded due to issues that arise during the rental period.

We strongly recommend thoroughly inspecting the trailer at pickup and taking clear, time-stamped photos of its condition before leaving. Prompt communication and documentation can help resolve concerns quickly and protect both parties.

 

What is considered an emergency?

• An emergency may include:
• Safety-related mechanical issues
• Brake, tire, or lighting failures
• Hitch or connection problems that make towing unsafe
• Any issue that makes the trailer unsafe or unusable
If you believe the trailer is unsafe to tow, stop using it and contact the owner immediately.

 

What is considered a minor issue?

• Minor issues may include:
• Cosmetic wear or pre-existing damage
• Non-essential accessories not functioning
• Cleanliness concerns
• Small operational questions
These should still be reported promptly so the owner can assist.

If you are unable to resolve the issue directly with the trailer owner, please contact the Neighbors Trailer support team for further assistance.

 

Pickup Checklist (Recommended Before You Leave)

Before departing with the trailer, we recommend:

• Inspecting the exterior for dents, scratches, or damage
• Checking tires for proper inflation and visible wear
• Confirming lights and signals are working
• Verifying the hitch is properly secured and locked
• Ensuring safety chains are properly attached
• Confirming the trailer jack is raised and secured
• Taking clear photos of all sides of the trailer
Taking a few extra minutes at pickup can help prevent misunderstandings later.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: What happens if I cause damage to the trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-happens-if-I-cause-damage-to-the-trailer--72
You are responsible for any damage that occurs to the trailer while it is in your possession during the rental period.

NT Protect coverage may apply to eligible damages subject to the terms of the protection plan.

After the trailer is returned, the owner may submit a Deposit Deduction Claim with supporting documentation, including before-and-after photos. The Neighbors Trailer team will review the claim and determine the appropriate amount, if any, to be deducted from your deposit. Any remaining portion of your deposit will be refunded.

If the damage exceeds $500, a formal damage claim process may be required.

We recommend documenting the trailer’s condition at both pickup and return to help prevent misunderstandings.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: What types of disputes will Neighbors Trailer Handle? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-types-of-disputes-will-Neighbors-Trailer-Handle--71
Neighbors Trailer operates as a booking platform and facilitator. While we are not a legal mediator between parties, we do review and manage matters directly related to:

• Rental fees
• Security deposits
• Deposit deduction claims
• Enforcement of platform policies
For damage-related claims, we follow a structured review process that includes evaluating submitted photos, documentation, timestamps, and communication between both parties.

As a neutral third party, our goal is to be transparent, fair, and consistent in every claim we review. With over a decade of experience in the trailer rental industry, we apply standardized guidelines to help ensure decisions are reasonable and balanced for both renters and owners.

Please note that disputes unrelated to platform fees, deposits, or policy enforcement may need to be resolved directly between the renter and trailer owner.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: When will my deposit be refunded after my rental? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/When-will-my-deposit-be-refunded-after-my-rental--69
Your deposit refund is initiated once the trailer owner confirms the trailer has been returned and the rental is officially closed.

After the refund is issued, please allow 3–7 business days for the funds to appear in your account, depending on your bank or card issuer.

If you do not see the refund after 7 business days, please contact the Neighbors Trailer support team so we can look into it for you.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What if I need to cancel due to an emergency? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-if-I-need-to-cancel-due-to-an-emergency--68
We understand that unexpected situations happen and plans can change. While emergency cancellations may not qualify for a full refund, we’ll do our best to help you work with the trailer owner to reschedule your rental when possible.

Rescheduling is subject to the following conditions:

• The trailer owner must be notified through the booking platform at least 24 hours before the original rental start date and time.
• The rental may only be rescheduled once.
• The new rental date must be within 60 days of the original rental start date.
• The trailer owner must agree to the rescheduled date.
If you’re experiencing an emergency, please contact the owner as soon as possible through your booking and reach out to the Neighbors Trailer support team if you need additional assistance.

--- [Renter] [deposit-refund] Q: Will I get a partial refund if I return the trailer early? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Will-I-get-a-partial-refund-if-I-return-the-trailer-early--67
Please review the following terms for partial refunds:

• Partial refunds can be processed if the trailer owner authorizes the refund. If the trailer owner approves a partial refund, they can issue the refund from their account.  The refund can only be processed prior to the trailer owner ending the rental. 
• Booking fees, tax and protection package are non-refundable.
• The maximum refundable amount will not exceed 75% of the rent amount.
For more information about early return or partial refunds, please refer to our Refunds Policy.

--- [Renter] [cancellation] Q: What is the cancellation policy? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-is-the-cancellation-policy--65
Refund amounts are based on how far in advance you cancel your booking:

• 72+ hours before the rental start time: 75% refund
• 48–72 hours before the rental start time: 50% refund
• 24–48 hours before the rental start time: 25% refund
• Less than 24 hours before the rental start time: No refund
• Same-day bookings: No refund
Please note:

• Platform fees are non-refundable once a booking has been accepted.
• A no-show is treated as a renter cancellation without notice and is not eligible for a refund.
 

How to properly cancel

All cancellations must be completed by the renter through their account by selecting “Cancel Booking” on the Booking Details page.

Requests made by phone, text, email, chat, or any other method will not cancel a booking.

 

Refund timing

If a refund is due, it will be processed within 10 days from the date it is approved. Refunds are issued to the original form of payment used at booking.

 

Our Cancellation and Refund Policy is part of our Terms of Use. By creating an account or booking a trailer, you agree to these terms.

 

If you'd like, I can also create a simplified visual version of this policy (great for mobile users) or make a more legally rigid version that mirrors your Terms page word-for-word.

--- [Renter] [payment] Q: What if a trailer owner asks me to pay additional money for the rental? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-if-a-trailer-owner-asks-me-to-pay-additional-money-for-the-rental--64
All rental fees and deposits are collected by Neighbors Trailer during the booking process to ensure a safe and secure transaction. Trailer owners are not permitted to request any additional payments or payment methods outside the platform.

--- [Renter] [listing] Q: What are the rental fees? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-are-the-rental-fees--63
Rental costs on Neighbors Trailer may include the following:

• Trailer Rental Fee
The daily, weekly, or monthly rental rate is set by the trailer owner and displayed on the listing page.
• Refundable Deposit
The deposit amount is set by the owner and shown on the listing page. This deposit is refunded after the trailer is returned without incident. The owner must mark the trailer as returned to initiate the refund.
• Booking Fee
Neighbors Trailer charges a booking fee equal to 10% of the rental fee, with a $10 minimum. This fee helps cover the operational costs of running the platform and is non-refundable.
• Deposit Processing Fee
A 3% processing fee is applied to the total rental amount. This fee is non-refundable.
• Protection Package Fee
This is a variable fee that provides rental protection for both the trailer owner and the renter.
• Taxes
Sales tax may be collected where required by state law.

--- [Renter] [account] Q: When will my credit card be charged? ---

At the time you submit a booking request, your credit card will be authorized for the total rental amount. This authorization confirms that sufficient funds are available but is not a completed charge.

Once the trailer owner accepts the booking, your credit card will be charged for the total rental amount.

Pending authorizations typically appear on your account for a few days, depending on your bank or card issuer.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How can I get more rentals?  ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-I-get-more-rentals---51
Increasing rentals comes down to visibility, trust, and responsiveness. Here are the most effective ways to get your trailer booked more often on Neighbors Trailer:

1. Set a fair and competitive price

Pricing is one of the first things renters compare.

• Review similar trailers in your area and price accordingly
• Adjust pricing based on demand, seasonality, or trailer condition
• Competitive pricing increases clicks and booking requests

2. Use high-quality photos to stand out

Listings with strong photos perform significantly better.

• Upload at least 4 high-quality photos of your trailer
• Show multiple angles and key features
• Do something unique to stand out (clean staging, trailer in use, good lighting)
• Make sure photos are clear, recent, and accurate

3. Complete your profile

Trust starts with a complete profile.

• Add a profile photo so renters know who they’re renting from
• Complete your listing details to reduce renter questions

4. Respond quickly to inquiries and bookings

Fast responses help you win more rentals.

• Respond within 1 hour during normal business hours
• Listings that respond within 1 hour between 8 am and 5 pm, Monday–Sunday receive priority placement in search results
• Turning on notifications can help you reply faster

5. Ask for reviews

• Reviews build confidence and trust.
• After a successful rental, ask renters to leave a review
• Positive reviews make future renters more likely to book
Consistent good reviews improve your listing’s visibility

6. Promote your listing outside Neighbors Trailer

External traffic can lead to more bookings.

• Share your listing link on social media platforms
• Post it on websites or community pages you moderate
• Let friends, family, and local groups know your trailer is available

7. Use coupon codes to attract renters

Discounts can help convert hesitant renters.

• Create a coupon code
• Share it on social media or include it directly in your listing
• Coupons are especially effective for first-time renters or slower periods

8. Keep your listing active and accurate

Active listings perform better.

• Update photos or descriptions occasionally
• Keep availability current
• Review pricing regularly to stay competitive
If you’ve followed these steps and still want help improving performance, our support team can review your listing and provide personalized suggestions.

Need help? Neighbors Trailer support is always happy to help you get more rentals.

--- [Owner] [how-to] Q: Do I have to pay income tax? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Do-I-have-to-pay-income-tax--50
Tax requirements vary by state, so we recommend checking the laws that apply where you live.

If your gross payments exceed $20,000 and you complete more than 200 transactions in a calendar year, Neighbors Trailer will issue you a Form 1099-K.

For more details about Form 1099-K and how it’s used, visit the IRS website:
Understanding Your Form 1099-K | Internal Revenue Service (IRS)

Neighbors Trailer does not provide tax advice.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How Do I Deactivate Auto Release of My Phone Number and / or Address? ---

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How Do I Get Paid for Loss or Damages? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Do-I-Get-Paid-for-Loss-or-Damages--48
How Do I Get Paid for Loss or Damages?

When a trailer is returned, select “End Rental” from the Current Booking page. At that time, you’ll have the option to withhold part or all of the renter’s deposit by selecting the Deposit Deduction Claim box and entering the claim details and amount.

You may deduct up to the total deposit amount set in your listing.
If the total cost of damages exceeds the deposit amount, note the full damage amount in the Deposit Deduction Claim and contact Neighbors Trailer Customer Support for next steps.

Deposit Deduction Claim Reasons

When submitting a claim, you can choose one of the following reasons:

• Damage
• Late Return
• Missing Add-On Item
• Other

Photo Requirements & Review Period

To support your claim, please ensure that photos are uploaded at both send-out and return to verify any loss or damage.

The renter will have up to 24 hours to review or dispute the claim.
Approved deposit deduction payouts will be issued along with your rental payout.

NT Protect Claims (Damages Over $500)

If damages from a verified Neighbors Trailer rental exceed $500, you may file an NT Protect claim by selecting the “File Claim” button on the booking details page for any On Rent or Completed booking.

NT Protect claims are reviewed by an adjuster and may take additional time to process before a payout is issued.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How Do I Delete My Listing? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Do-I-Deactivate-My-Listing--47
How Do I Delete or Deactivate My Listing?

You can deactivate or archive a listing from your account, but this should be done with caution. Only deactivate or archive your listing if you no longer plan to rent out your trailer.

Over time, your listing can build organic search rankings that help renters find you more easily. Deactivating a listing may cause you to lose those rankings. If your trailer will only be unavailable for a short period, it is recommended that you block dates on your calendar instead of deactivating the listing.

 

Deactivate (Hide) Your Listing

From the Mobile App

• Select More
• Select My Trailers
• Locate the trailer you want to deactivate
• Toggle the Visibility switch to turn the listing off

From the Web

• Go to your Dashboard
• Select Trailer
• Select Trailer List
Toggle the Visibility switch to turn the listing off

 

Archive Your Listing

If you want to fully archive the trailer instead of just hiding it:

Mobile App:

• Go to My Trailers
• Select More on the listing
• Select Archive Trailer

Web:

• Go to Trailer List
• Click the Action (3 dots) button for the listing
• Select Archive Trailer
Archiving or deactivating should only be used when you no longer intend to rent the trailer.

--- [Owner] [late-return] Q: Do I need GPS tracking on my trailer? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Do-I-need-GPS-tracking-on-my-trailer--39
Yes—absolutely. We strongly encourage all trailer owners on Neighbors Trailer to protect their trailers with GPS tracking.

GPS tracking helps:

• Recover your trailer in the event of theft
• Locate a trailer if it is abandoned or not returned on time
• Monitor where your trailer is located during and between rentals
Having GPS adds an extra layer of protection and peace of mind for your business.

 

Where can I purchase GPS tracking?

GPS devices are available from many providers, but we’ve done the research for you.

Neighbors Trailer has partnered with a GPS provider to offer owners a special discounted solution designed specifically for trailer tracking. In the near future, we plan to integrate this GPS solution directly into the Neighbors Trailer platform, allowing owners to track their trailers right from their account.

GPS device details:

4+ year battery-operated GPS device

$169 one-time cost

Includes 2 years of tracking service

Each additional year of tracking is only $15

For more information or to order GPS tracking for trailers, visit this link: GPS Tracking for Trailers · Neighbors Trailer

Are there tracking options I should avoid?

Some tracking devices are designed for personal items and may not provide the level of reliability needed for trailer monitoring or recovery.

Bluetooth-based trackers are not designed specifically for trailer security and may have limitations, including:

• Dependence on nearby compatible mobile devices to report location
• Inconsistent or delayed location updates
• Limited functionality in rural or low-traffic areas
• Notifications that may alert renters or third parties to the presence of the device
• No guarantee of continuous or real-time tracking
Due to these limitations, Bluetooth-based trackers may not be suitable as a primary tracking solution for trailers used on the Neighbors Trailer platform.

 

Disclaimer

Tracking capabilities vary by device, installation, coverage area, and service provider. No tracking solution guarantees theft prevention or recovery. Trailer owners are responsible for selecting and maintaining any tracking equipment used.

For more information about reliable GPS technology for trailer tracking, click here: GPS Tracking for Trailers · Neighbors Trailer

--- [Owner] [deposit-refund] Q: Why does Neighbors Trailer charge a service fee? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/Does-Neighbors-Trailer-take-a-commission-from-rental-transactions--34
Great question — and a fair one. The service fee funds the infrastructure that makes peer-to-peer trailer rental safe, protected, and trustworthy for everyone involved. Here's exactly what it covers:

• NT Protect™ Coverage — accidental damage & theft protection on every eligible rental, underwritten by licensed insurance partners
• In-App Damage Claims — if a trailer is returned damaged, with missing equipment, or unpaid fees, owners can file a Deposit Deduction Claim directly in the app or dashboard when ending the rental
• Verified Renters — renters are identity-screened before they can book, so owners know exactly who has their trailer
• Verified Owners — every trailer owner is identity-verified before their listing goes live on the platform
• GPS-Ready Rentals — owners can equip their trailers with GPS tracking through our partner program, giving you added location visibility during your rental
• Secure In-App Payments — encrypted transactions, no cash, no risk
• Toll Management — enrolled trailers have their toll fees automatically tracked and collected from the renter by Neighbors Trailer during the rental period, so owners never receive a toll bill or have to chase down charges themselves
• Platform Support — our team is available to assist with questions, claims, and rental issues through live chat, email, or [Phone number available upon request]
• Platform Development — ongoing improvements to keep your experience the best in the market
Think of it less as a fee and more as the price of renting with total confidence.

The service fee is 20% of the owner's rental revenue — it covers marketing, R&D, support, and platform operations. As an owner, you set your own price and stay in full control of your listing.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: How do I extend a rental? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/What-if-the-renter-needs-to-extend-the-rental--30
You can submit unlimited extension requests during a rental.  Extension requests may be initiated by either the renter or the trailer owner.

How to request an extension

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select My Bookings.
• If your rental has already started, select the Current tab. Otherwise, your booking will appear under Upcoming.
• Select the booking.
• Choose Extension Request.
• Enter the number of additional days you’d like to extend.
• Add a comment in the Remarks field.
• Select Send Request.

• Open the app and select Bookings.

• Select Extension Request.
• Enter the number of additional days.
• Add a comment in the Remarks field.
• Tap Send Request.
If you are the renter, you’ll be prompted to complete payment for the extension.

Once submitted, the other party will be notified and can choose to accept or reject the request.

If the current rental end time has already passed and the extension has not yet been accepted, the request may be manually reviewed and accepted by Neighbors Trailer Support.

Important note

Protection package coverage applies only to rental periods that are verified and fully paid in advance of your rental period through the Neighbors Trailer platform.

--- [Owner] [damage-claims] Q: How do I End a Rental from my account? ---

• Enter any relevant remarks.
• If there is no damage, loss, or unpaid rental fees, select End Rental to complete the process.
• If there is damage, loss, or unpaid rental fees, select the Deposit Deduction Claim option, enter the required information, and then select End Rental.
Once submitted, the rental will be marked as complete.

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select My Bookings.
• Choose Current Bookings.
• Open the booking and select End Rental.
• Upload a minimum of four new photos of the trailer taken at the time the rental is ending.
• Confirm the current date and time.
• Enter any relevant remarks.
• If there is no damage, loss, or unpaid rental fees, select End Rental to complete the process.
• If there is damage, loss, or unpaid rental fees, select the Deposit Deduction Claim option, enter the required information, and then select End Rental.
Once submitted, the rental will be marked as complete.

--- [Owner] [rental-management] Q: How do I start a rental from my account? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-I-start-a-rental-from-my-account--28
You can begin an active rental directly from your Neighbors Trailer account by following the steps below.

How to begin a rental

From the Mobile App

• Select Bookings.
• Open the booking and select Begin Rental.
• Upload a minimum of four new photos of the trailer taken at the time the rental begins.
• Confirm the current date and time.
• Enter any relevant remarks.
• Select Begin Rental to complete the process.
Once submitted, the rental will be marked as “On Rent”.

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select My Bookings.
• Open the booking and select Begin Rental.
• Upload a minimum of four new photos of the trailer taken at the time the rental begins.
• Confirm the current date and time.
• Enter any relevant remarks.
• Select Begin Rental to complete the process.
Once submitted, the rental will be marked as “On Rent”.

Why photos are required

Photos taken at the start of the rental help document the condition of the trailer and provide protection for both renters and owners in the event of a dispute.

--- [Owner] [general] Q: How do I share my pickup address and phone number with the renter after accepting a booking? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-do-I-share-my-pickup-address-and-phone-number-with-the-renter-after-accepting-a-booking--26
After you accept a booking, your phone number and pickup address are automatically shared with the renter—unless you have turned off automatic sharing in your Profile settings.

If automatic sharing is disabled, you can still manually share your contact information at any time after accepting a booking. There are two ways to do this: through the booking details page or the message portal.

Sharing contact information from the message portal

Once a booking is accepted, the following icons will appear above the chat input field in the message portal:

• Share phone number
• Share address
• Send photo or file
Select the appropriate icon to share your contact details directly with the renter.

Sharing your pickup address from the booking page

From the Mobile App

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select My Bookings.
• Choose Upcoming Bookings.
• Open the booking and select the three dots in the top-right corner.
• Select Share Location and enter your pickup address.
• Select Submit.

From the Website

• Go to your Dashboard.
• Select My Bookings.
• Choose Upcoming Bookings.
• Select the three dots under the Action column for the booking.
• Select Share Location, enter your pickup address, and submit.
Once shared, the renter will be able to view your pickup address and contact information.

From the Website

• Select My Bookings from the left navigation menu.
• Open the booking you’d like to review.
• Review the details and choose to Accept or Reject the booking.

You can update your trailer listing at any time from either the web platform or the mobile app. Follow the steps below for your device.

--- [Owner] [listing] Q: How Do I List A Trailer for Rent? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-Do-I-List-A-Trailer-for-Rent--22
Follow these steps to create a listing for your trailer:

Accessing the Add Trailer Menu

From the Web

• Select More
• Select Add Trailer

From the Mobile App

• Select Trailers
• Select Add Trailer
 

Create Your Listing

• Add a New Trailer• Click the “Add New Trailers” button at the top right of your dashboard.

• Create a Descriptive Title• Include key details like the trailer type, size, and year to make your listing eye-catching.

• Select a Category• Choose the category that best matches your trailer.

• Set Your Rental Rates• Enter competitive daily, weekly, and monthly rates.

• Write a Detailed Description• Use at least 200 characters to describe your trailer. Include all features, condition, and any other important details.

• Complete Trailer Information• Fill in the remaining fields, including whether you offer deliveries.
• If offering delivery, set your per-mile charge and delivery radius (the maximum distance you are willing to travel).

• Enter Location• Add your city, state, and full address.
• Only your city and state will be visible to renters before booking.

• Add Optional Accessories• Include add-ons like straps, ball and mount, or any other accessory or service you want to charge for as part of the rental.

• Upload Photos• Upload at least 4 pictures to showcase your trailer.

• Submit Your Listing for Review
Once you submit your listing, it will be reviewed before going live.  This ensures your listing is complete, attractive, and ready for renters to book.

 

Tips for creating a strong listing

A complete and detailed listing can improve approval speed and visibility in search results. We recommend:

• Writing a clear, descriptive title (include trailer type, size, and key features)
• Adding detailed information about dimensions, weight capacity, and included accessories
• Uploading high-quality, well-lit photos from multiple angles
• Highlighting unique features (ramps, tie-downs, winch, brakes, etc.)
• Clearly stating pickup instructions or special requirements
Well-optimized listings tend to attract more bookings and reduce renter questions.

 

Next, set up your bank account information so that you can receive payment for your rentals.

--- [Owner] [deposit-refund] Q: How much should I set for my deposit? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/How-much-should-I-set-for-my-deposit--16
While Neighbors Trailer can’t determine the deposit amount for you, most trailer owners typically set a deposit between $150 and $300.

You’re free to choose a higher deposit if you feel it’s necessary. However, keep in mind that setting a deposit too high may discourage some potential renters from booking your trailer.

--- [Owner] [payment] Q: When will I receive the payout from my rental? ---
URL: https://neighborstrailer.com/help-center-details/When-will-I-receive-the-payout-from-my-rental--14
Payouts are automatically initiated when the trailer owner ends the rental. 

Once initiated, funds may take 1–3 business days to appear in your bank account, depending on your financial institution.  If a Deposit Deduction Claim is filed, the payout process will be delayed by at least 24 hours.

Greetings,

We are notifying you that your account has been deactivated due lack of activity and non-compliance in accepting pending booking request(s). As a trailer owner, you are required to accept, reject, or reach out to the renter of a pending booking within 12 hours of the booking having been placed. Per our policies, you are also required to have a 70% acceptance rate on our platform.

In the event that your trailer is not available, Neighbors Trailer provides the tools for you to prevent your trailer from being booked or seen by potential renters on the platform. These tools are the active/inactive toggle for your trailer, which removes your listing from searchable results, and the block dates calendar, which prevents renter's from booking on specific dates.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Owner] [payment] Template: Payout Reversal Notice ---
This email is to notify you of a credit card dispute for booking ID ____.  

 

The bank decided to refund the renter their full amount.  Per the terms of our Owner Payout Policy which you can find in Neighbors Trailer Terms of Use, when a charge is disputed and the bank refunds the money, the trailer owner is not entitled to the payout. 



The payout in the amount of $___ will not be paid out to your account.  




Payout Reversal FAQ's




Why am I not elegible for a payout?

All money paid by the renter for the rental has been withdrawn by the credit card company.  Additionally, Neighbors Trailer is charged a credit card dispute fee which we cover.  Per our Terms of Use "Chargebacks" policy, you are not entitled to the payout if the chargeback is lost.  You can read more about our terms here: Terms | Neighbors Trailer




Does Neighbors Trailer respond to the credit card dispute?

Yes, we have an experienced team to handle this, and we review and respond to every credit card dispute.




Why did the credit card company decide in favor of the Renter?

Neighbors Trailer has a very clear refund and cancellation policy.  Unfortunately, financial institutions have their own policy that sometimes contradicts our  policy , and their  policy takes priority over our  policy.




How can I avoid credit card disputes?

Embrace our policies found here:  Terms | Neighbors Trailer
Ask the right questions before accepting a booking, such as, truck, brake controller, load, weight, etc.
Fulfill your commitment to the renter
Keep up with your trailer maintenance
Be present when the rental starts and ends

 

Please let us know if you have any questions.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Both] [onboarding] Template: Glad You're Here! Tips to Start Getting Trailer Bookings ---
Hi,

Welcome to Neighbors Trailer! We're so excited to have you on the platform and want to make sure you get off to a great start. Here are a few tips and helpful steps to set you up for success!

 Communicate Quickly with Renters Fast communication is one of the biggest factors in securing a booking! Renters appreciate quick responses and are much more likely to follow through with a booking when they hear back promptly. We recommend responding to all messages within an hour whenever possible. Here's how to access your messages:

From the Mobile App:

Open the app and select Messages from the bottom menu
Tap the conversation you'd like to respond to
Enter your message and tap Send

From the Website:

Select Messages from the main menu
Choose the conversation you want to open
Enter your response and click Send

Please remember that all communication should remain within the platform to ensure proper documentation and to protect both you and your renters!

 Always Follow Up — Even if the Renter Cancelled If a renter cancelled a booking request or their message went unanswered, it's never too late to follow up! Reaching out after a cancellation shows the renter that you are attentive, professional, and genuinely interested in helping them. A simple, friendly follow-up message can go a long way and may even encourage the renter to rebook with you in the future. Here are a few tips for a great follow-up message:

Acknowledge their cancelled request — Let them know you saw their request and that you're sorry you weren't able to connect in time
Express your interest in helping them — Let them know you'd love to assist them with their trailer needs in the future
Keep it short, friendly, and professional — A brief and genuine message is all it takes to leave a great impression
Invite them to rebook — Let them know your trailer is available and encourage them to submit a new booking request when they're ready

Here's an example follow-up message you could send:

"Hi [Renter Name], I'm so sorry I missed your booking request and message! 

I would have loved to help you out. 

If you ever need a trailer in the future please don't hesitate to reach out — I'd be happy to work with you. Hope to connect soon!"

 Accept Booking Requests Quickly Renters often have tight timelines, so the faster you accept a booking request the better! We recommend accepting or declining all booking requests within an hour whenever possible. Here's how:

From the Mobile App:

Select Bookings
Tap the booking you'd like to review
Review the details and tap Accept or Reject

From the Website:

Go to your Dashboard
Select My Bookings from the left navigation menu
Open the booking you'd like to review
Review the details and click Accept or Reject

Once accepted, the renter will be notified and the booking will be confirmed!

Please don't hesitate to reach out if you have any questions, we're here to help!

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Owner] [deposit-refund] Template: Action Needed: Your Rental Has Not Been Ended — Booking #[Booking ID] ---
Hi [Owner First Name],

 

We are reaching out regarding booking #[Booking ID], which was scheduled to end at [End Date]. The rental has not yet been marked as returned ("End Rental") on the Neighbors Trailer platform.

 

This delay creates several issues we want to make sure you're aware of:

 

• Renter Deposit: The Renter's security deposit remains on hold and cannot be refunded until you end the rental. Unnecessary holds on deposits can lead to disputes.

• Chargeback Risk: If the Renter has already returned the trailer but their deposit is not released in a timely manner, they may dispute the hold with their credit card company. Chargebacks result in fees that affect Neighbors Trailer and may impact your payout and account standing.

• Payout Delay: Your payout is initiated when you select "End Rental." Until then, your payout cannot be processed.

 

Per the Terms of Use, Owners must mark "End Rental" within 1 hour of receiving the trailer back.

 

If the trailer has been returned, please end the rental immediately in the app. If the trailer has NOT been returned and the Renter is late, please contact us so we can assist. If a rental extension is needed, please submit the request through the platform.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Renter] [deposit-refund] Template: Deposit Deduction Dispute ---
Hi [Renter Name],

We are writing regarding the Deposit Deduction Claim filed in connection with your recent rental of [Trailer Description] under Booking #[Booking Number].

As outlined in Section 26 of the Neighbors Trailer Terms of Use, the baseline condition of the trailer is established by the Trailer Owner's pre-rental photographs uploaded at the start of the Rental Period. Damage identified at the end of the Rental Period that was not visible in the pre-rental documentation is presumed to have occurred during the rental.

If you believe the claimed damage was pre-existing or incorrectly attributed to your Rental Period, you bear the responsibility of providing supporting documentation.

To formally dispute this claim, please submit the following within twenty-four (24) hours of this notice:

Timestamped photographs taken prior to or at the commencement of the Rental Period clearly showing the area(s) of the trailer now claimed as damaged
Any written communications exchanged with the Owner prior to departure noting the alleged condition
Any inspection checklist completed at pickup
Any additional documentation you would like us to consider (receipts, witness statements, dash cam footage, etc.)
A written explanation clearly outlining the specific basis of your dispute

Please reply to this email with documentation. Verbal disputes or off-platform communications cannot be considered under the Terms.

If a complete dispute submission to this email is not received within the required 24-hour window, the claim will be reviewed and finalized based on the available documentation in accordance with Section 25 of the Terms of Use.

Our review will be based solely on the evidence submitted by both parties and Platform records.

If you have any questions about the submission process, you may contact us through the Help Center.
