If your agreement allows and your counsel approves, you may add:

Continued possession of rental property beyond the agreed term without authorization may expose you to additional civil liability under applicable law.

Avoid direct criminal threats unless advised by counsel and appropriate in your jurisdiction.

--- [AUTO-REPLY-OK] [Both] [how-to] Template: Booking History Report ---
Greetings,

You can view and download your complete booking history at any time by running the Revenue Classification report. This report provides a detailed breakdown of your completed bookings and related revenue.

Here's how to access it:

From the Neighbors Trailer App

Open the Neighbors Trailer app and sign in.

Tap More in the bottom navigation.

Select Report.

Tap Revenue Classification.

Apply any available filters (such as date range) to refine your results.

View the report on screen or export/download it as needed.

From the Website

Go to NeighborsTrailer.com and sign in to your owner account.

From the main menu, select Report.

Click Revenue Classification.

Apply filters (for example, date range) to find the booking history you need.

View or download the report for your records.

Helpful Tips

Use date filters to quickly locate bookings for a specific month, quarter, or year.

Downloaded reports are useful for accounting, tax preparation, and performance tracking.

You can also find more information about this and other FAQs in our Help Center: Help Center | Neighbors Trailer

If you need any assistance, our Support team is happy to help.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Both] [payment] Template: Non-Compliance Start / End Rental ---
Greetings,


It has come to our attention that your account is non-compliant with our policy regarding the starting or ending of your rental for booking ID ______.  Please resolve this matter immediately.


As the trailer owner, it is your responsibility to manage bookings, including any date changes or extensions.  Failure to comply with this request will result in the forfeiture of your payout and/or a $25 daily fee for every day the booking remains open, per our Terms of Use.


Failure to comply with this request will result in forfeiture of your payout and / or a $25 fee for every day the booking has not been closed out per our Terms of Use.


Why is it important to end the rental when the trailer is returned?
There are many reasons you should end the rental immediately when the trailer is returned, but here are a few of the most important reasons. 
You are holding back the renter's deposit money.  This may have a negative impact on your review left by the renter as well as the reputation of the platform.
Expedite Your Payout - Your payout is automatically initiated when you end the rental and not until then.
Proof of Damages - Waiting to end the rental may make it difficult to prove damages were caused by the renter and not someone who used the trailer after the renter.
Proof of Rental Completion Date / Time - This will clear up any questions involving late return fees.


 We appreciate your compliance!

--- [AUTO-REPLY-OK] [Owner] [listing] Template: How It Works for Trailer Owners ---
Greetings,

Welcome to Neighbors Trailer!

We are happy to answer all of your questions about how the rental process works.  

What are the Trailer Owner Benefits? 

Free Listings - Create unlimited trailer listings.  Every listing is free and includes editorial review by our staff. This is your business! Set your own prices, deposit, and requirements.  Our platform provides tons of options for you to run your business the way you want.  We take 20% of each rental which means we only make money if you make money; it's a win for everyone. 
Free Advertising and Promotion of Your Listing - Every trailer owner benefits from the advertising and sponsorships paid for by Neighbors Trailer.  Our marketing team uses many techniques to continuously get more exposure through search engines, social media, trade shows, events, and more. 
Free Tools to Manage Your Bookings – The Neighbors Trailer software offers everything you need.  From communication with the renter, booking management, before and after picture uploads, deposit refunds, owner payouts, and much more.  
Resources – The Neighbors Trailer Owner Library contains everything a trailer owner will need, including: rental contract, how-to guides, maintenance guides, forms, FAQs and more.  Whether you are new to the trailer rental business or are a seasoned veteran, you will have everything you need.  
Free Credit Card Processing – Neighbors Trailer uses Stripe, one of the most trusted credit card processing companies in the world.  This service includes risk evaluation and dispute management.  If a credit card charge from your rental is disputed, Neighbors Trailer will go to work on your behalf to fight the dispute. 
Free Damage Claim Management – If your trailer is returned with damages, missing items, or returned late, you have the option to withhold up to the full amount of the deposit through Neighbors Trailer Damage Deposit Claim tool.  
Free ID Verification -  Every renter must complete ID verification during the booking process before they can complete the booking.  The ID verification process includes a selfie and document upload via CLEAR which is the same service offered at the airports.  For users who have a pre-existing CLEAR account, only a selfie will be required to process a booking.  
Free Owner Support - The Neighbors Trailer staff has over a decade in the trailer rental business.  We are here to help and support you with all things related to your business. 
Insurance included with every eligible trailer rental (free to our owners).




How do I list my trailer? 

There is a 1-minute video in the media section of the Library that will show you how to get started.  From the menu of your Dashboard, go to Library in the left menu, then select "How-to Videos" or you can watch it on Youtube: How To List A Trailer On Neighbors Trailer - YouTube 

 Also, check out: 10 Essential Tips to Make Your Trailer Rental Listing Stand Out




Is it FREE to list a trailer? 

It's FREE to list trailer(s) for rent on Neighbors Trailer.  Neighbors Trailer takes a 20% commission from the trailer owner's rental revenue for each transaction which goes toward our advertising, development, and administrative costs.  As a trailer owner, you decide the price to set for your rental.  Setting a fair price will increase the number of rentals you receive.  You can also rent out accessories using our "Add-ons" to increase rental revenue. 




Is there a way to avoid paying the 20% fee?

Yes, if you bring your own off-platform rentals and enter them in "My Reservations", you will receive 100% of your payout.  My Reservations allows you to enter reservations quickly with just 3 pieces of information from the renter: Name, phone, and email.  The best part is it's FREE for you to use and you will still receive all of the owner benefits.  WIth My Reservations, you can also use your own branding and your owner rental contract.  We do charge a 10% booking fee to the renter to cover our platform fees.

 

Does Neighbors Trailer have an App? 

Yes, you can download our Owner App from the Apple or Google Play store.  Please be aware that we have a Renter and Owner App, so be sure to download the correct one.   

 

Is there insurance coverage? 

Neighbors Trailer offers a protection package from NT Protect, a Neighbors Trailer company, underwritten by our licensed insurance partners.  You can find out more here: Help Center | Neighbors Trailer

 

How are damages to my trailer handled? 

Your primary recourse for damage is to withhold money from the deposit that you set when you create your listing.   If damages exceed the $500 deductible, an NT Protect Protection Package claim can be filed directly from your booking page.




How are damages proven? 

When you send out your trailer, you will upload 4 current pictures of your trailer through the send-out process in your account.  When the trailer is returned, you will upload 4 new pictures the same way.  In the event of damage, the pictures are reviewed to verify damage so that we can accept your Deposit Deduction Claim. 




How do deposits work? 

You set your own deposit amount when you create your listing.  If there is no damage when the trailer is returned, our software automatically refunds the deposit to your renter which they will see in their account within a few days.  The refund is initiated by you closing out the rental.  If the trailer is returned with damage, you will have the option to check a box for a "Deposit Deduction Claim" and enter the amount.  After approval, this amount will go to your bank account. 




Do I need GPS tracking on my trailer? 

Absolutely.  We strongly encourage all owners to protect their trailer with GPS.  GPS tracking will help with theft recovery, abandonment, and keep tabs on where your trailer is located.  Yes, your trailer may be eligible for our insurance coverage, but there is a deductible and some fees that may not be covered by insurance.  You will have more to gain by recovering your trailer immediately by knowing where it's located at all times.  

 

Where can I purchase GPS tracking? 

You can purchase a GPS device just about anywhere.  Avoid AirTag and the short term battery life devices.  We have done your research and testing for many years and have partnered with a GPS company that offers Neighbors Trailer owners a great deal.  In the near future, we plan to integrate their solution to the Neighbors Trailer platform enabling trailer owners to track directly from their account. 

You can order the 4+ year battery-operated device for only $159 and it includes 2 years of tracking service.  Each additional year is only $15.  Find out more and purchase your GPS here: GPS Tracking for Trailers · Neighbors Trailer 

 

Is there a rental contract? 

There is a rental contract that we provide to you.  You can access it from your account.  Just go to "Library" from the left menu and in the media section on top you will see Rental Contract.  If you would like a Word doc that you can edit, just let me know and I will send you one. You are also more than welcome to use your own contract if you prefer.

 

Are renters screened? 

Every transaction goes through a risk assessment during the booking process to detect and prevent fraudulent activity.  Our process uses thousands of signals to assign a risk score and automatically block fraudulent transactions from being processed.  In September 2023, digital ID verification was released as an additional layer of security. 

 

How does the rental process work? 

When you receive a booking request, you will be notified by email and SMS alert. Please note that the renter has put in their payment details, and their card is authorized at this time. Once you view the booking details, you will have the option to accept or reject the booking.  If you accept the booking, the renter is automatically charged. If you reject the booking, the renter will not be charged. You can also message the renter before, during, or after the booking is accepted or rejected. At some point prior to pickup, you will share the pickup location (address that you enter) and phone number with the renter or you can choose for the sharing of your contact information to happen automatically upon accepting a booking.  You can also request any needed documents from the Renter.   

 

How is the rental payment processed? 

All rentals must be paid through the Neighbors Trailer booking process on our platform.  We use Stripe which is a trusted 3rd party processing company used by millions of business including Amazon.  The rental fees are held in Stripe until you release the funds which is done by showing the trailer received.  Neighbors Trailer handles all credit card processing and associated fees.  

 

When do I receive the money from my rental? 

Payouts are automated by our internal programming and are initiated immediately when the "end rental" button is pressed. The money will reflect in your account in 3-5 business days. If the customer asks, their deposit refund takes 3-5 business days after the rental is ended, as well.

 

How does the handoff process work? 

Prior to your first rental, you will receive a set of instructions.  We also recommend that you go to the Library in your Neighbors Trailer account and Select the folder "Getting Started Guide" and read "Prepare for Rentals" and also take a look at the folder "Best Practices".   

You have full control of the rental process.  You can meet at your home, office, a public parking lot or you can even deliver and pickup at the renter's location.  You can choose to automatically have the pickup location sent to the renter when you accept the booking or you can manually release your contact information when you choose prior to the rental.  This option can be set by toggling the switches in your profile settings. You may have a rental contract for them to sign or you can use ours in the library under "forms" 




Can You Predict My Rental Success? 

Right now, is the best time to list your trailer due to the warmer season.  Generally, if your rental rates are competitive, and you have good pictures in your listing and you list all the sizes and details about your trailer, you will get a lot of rentals. Unfortunately, we cannot predict your success because there are too many variables.  Here are a list of things to consider: 

Demand for rentals in your area.  Highly populated areas will do better than rural areas. 
Demand for your trailer.  For example, a 16-24 ft trailer would be more popular than a 5 ft trailer.   
You will see an increase in rentals during warm weather conditions.   
Fair market rental rates.  Set your price at an average or slightly less than average price to be more competitive.  Check competitor rates in your area. 
Fair market deposit rate.  Check competitor rates in your area. 
If your trailer includes a winch, spare tire, or additional accessories, this will increase your rentals.  Accessories can be added to your listing as add-ons when you create your listing. 
Putting the right information in your listing, such as your allowed pickup times, will increase your rentals.   
If you follow our guidelines which can be found in the "Library" within your owner account, it will improve your success. 
Although, some trailer owners have seen bookings within 24 hours and many within a few days of listing their trailer, be willing to wait a few weeks to start seeing results from your listing.  The longer your listing is active, the better it will perform in search results.  As you receive customer reviews after rentals, this will also increase your rentals.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Both] [payment] Template: Payout Deduction Notice ---
Greetings,

We are contacting you to notify you of a $___ deduction in your payout for a circumvention or attempt to circumvent the platform with ____.  This deduction amount has been significantly reduced from the amount stated in our Abuse of Services Policy.


What is a Circumvention?
A circumvention is when you receive a booking or lead through the Neighbors Trailer platform and offer part or all of the rental services outside the platform. To maintain active account status with Neighbors Trailer, we ask that you not share direct contact information or attempt to circumvent the platform prior to an accepted booking.  You can read our Abuse of Services policy in detail on our Terms of Use page.  To protect our investments and be fair to other trailer owners, we enforce this policy so that we may continue to bring you qualified rentals.  We appreciate your compliance! 


What if the Renter wanted to see the trailer to make sure it would work?
All pictures and measurements can be shown in your listing or via message with the renter which improves accuracy of information being shared.


What if the Rental Didn't Happen?
Our Abuse of Services Policy is not contingent on the rental happening or not.   


Why Is It Necessary to Keep Rentals on the Platform?
Renting off the platform is extremely high risk for damage, theft and other liability.  
The Neighbors Trailer platform is safe and secure for all parties with many security measures in place; including ID Verification and credit card fraud detection metrics.
ID verification is not completed until the booking is processed.  You don't know who you are really communicating with on the message portal until the booking is processed.
A person who is willing to circumvent (cheat the system) is most likely willing to cheat you when they damage your trailer or don't return on time or at all.
We all have to abide by the same rules to be fair to all users.


Why Is There a Fee for Circumvention?
Neighbors Trailer invests a lot to bring trailer owners qualified leads.  We need your support and compliance to continue offering our services.


How Can I Increase My Profit Margins?
You can rebook the same renters or create new reservations for off-platform rental requests through the "My Reservations" portal and receive 100% of your rental rate. 

What are the Benefits of Using My Reservations?

1. You will receive your full rental amount shown in your listing
2. Your rentals will be insured (if eligibility is met per terms).
3. Credit card processing
4. ID verification
5. Claims management
6. Tax collection and filing
7. Owner booking management
8. Owner cancellation payouts according to policy
9. Coupon code management
10. Toll management

How Can I Access My Reservations from the Owner App?

1. Select the "More" button in the bottom right corner of the app.
2. Select "My Reservations"
3. To add a reservation, select "Add Reservation"

We look forward to helping you grow your rental business!

Partial refunds can be processed if the trailer owner authorizes the refund. If the trailer owner approves a partial refund, they can issue the refund from their account.  The refund can only be processed prior to the trailer owner ending the rental.

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Owner] [cancellation] Template: Cancellation Policy For Renters & Owners ---
Hey there! 


Thanks for reaching out. Below, you will find information regarding cancellations.


For pending bookings:
There is no cancellation fee if the renter or the owner cancel a booking. The charge for the rental amount is only on hold and not fully charged to the renter until the owner accepts it. After the owner accepts the booking, the cancellation policies take into effect due to us finaling the charge.


Cancelling Policy for Renters:


Cancel at least 72 hours prior to the start of your rental and receive a 75% refund.
Cancel 48 - 72 hours prior to the start of your rental and receive a 50% refund.
Cancel 24 - 48 hours prior to the start of your rental and receive a 25% refund.
No refund for cancellations within 24 hours of the start of your rental.
No refund for same day bookings.
Platform fees are non-refundable after the booking is accepted.
A no-show is the same as a cancellation without notice.
Typically, these cancellation policies will always take into effect, but we do take a look and review cases where the renter reaches out for an issue and the reason for cancellation was due to complications that resulted from negligence or actions from the owner. In this case, it would become an Owner Cancellation.


Cancellation Policies for Owners:


OWNER CANCELLATIONS FOR CAUSE

Owner Cancellations are only intended for unavoidable circumstances.  Trailer Owners are allowed up to 2 rental cancellations For Cause within a 6-month rolling window without fees.  Subsequent cancellations by the Trailer Owner will incur a fee of $50 if cancelled at least 7 days prior to the start of the rental or a fee of $100 if cancelled less than 7 days prior to the start of the rental.  

OWNER CANCELLATIONS WITHOUT CAUSE

Owner Cancellations Without Cause include; but are not limited to, any cancellation due to inaccurate trailer listing details, failure to perform adequate maintenance or inspections of the trailer prior to the rental that may cause the trailer to be unsafe, and failure to meet a customer at agreed time or location.  Owner cancellation Without Cause is subject to a minimum fee assessed to the Trailer Owner of 30% of the booking rental amount.

The Company will use its reasonable judgement to determine what is reasonable Cause for cancellation.  Fees are deducted from the Trailer Owner's future payout.  Any cancellation request after the rental has been started or sent out will be denied.  

Any owner cancellation with the intent to circumvent the platform could result in a $1,000.00 penalty fee.



Let us know if you have any further questions or concerns.

--- [AUTO-REPLY-OK] [Renter] [general] Template: Toll Enrollment Program ---
Greetings,

Thank you for reaching out.

We would be happy to assist you. In the event of the renter incurring a toll during the rental period, you can simply reply to this email and provide us with the toll bill, and we will attempt to charge the renter on your behalf.  Before you send us the toll bill, please be sure you have enrolled in our toll program.   Enrolling in our toll program reduces the chance of you receiving a toll bill with future rentals on our platform.  Our toll program automates the entire toll process and we collect toll fees from the renter so that you don't have to deal with it.  Enrolling in our toll program is completely free with no subscription or cost to you. 


Here are the steps to enroll in our toll program:

--- [REFERENCE-ONLY] [Renter] [extension] Template: Trailer Not Returned by Renter ---
Greetings,

Thank you for reaching out.

You should always process an extension request or ask the renter to process an extension request prior to the end of the rental period if you think the trailer won't be back when it is due.

If your trailer has not been returned by the end rental date and time, don't panic.  Almost 100% of the time when this happens, it's because the renter forgot to extend or possibly a case of irresponsibility.

If you are unable to get in contact with the renter and the trailer has not been returned on time, here are some steps you can take:

Contact the renter through the Neighbors Trailer message portal and ask when they will be returning the trailer.
If you don't receive a response, try texting the renter.  If you don't have their phone number, we can provide it to you.
If you don't receive a response, contact the renter again through the NT message portal and by phone / text and give a deadline for the renter to contact you. For example, "Your rental was due back at _____ date and time. I have reached out many times and have not heard back from you. I will give you until ___ time today to contact me or I will have to escalate the matter and terminate the rental."
If the renter doesn't contact you by your deadline, reach out in writing again and tell the renter you are now terminating the rental and give them a short deadline to contact you (maybe 1 hour) or you will contact the police and report the trailer stolen.
If you don't hear from the renter by the 2nd deadline, contact the police. 

It's important to note that when you report a trailer as stolen, it becomes a criminal matter, and you should no longer continue charging for the rental.  The laws are different in each state or jurisdiction.  In some states, the law may require you to give a certain amount of notice to the renter of the rental being terminated before they will allow you to report the trailer stolen.

--- [AUTO-REPLY-OK] [Owner] [listing] Template: How to View my Listing ---
Greetings,

Thank you for reaching out regarding your listing inquiry.

You can check the status of your listing by following these steps:

From the Owner App:
Select "More"
Select "My Trailers"
View the Status of each listing in the light green or red highlight

From the Web:
Go to your Dashboard
Select "Trailer"
Select "Trailer List"
View the Status of each listing in the light green or red highlight

Understanding what each status means:
1. Approved - This means your listing is live and can receive bookings
2. Pending - This means your listing is currently going through a manual review and should be approved soon.
3. Draft - This means your listing is still in draft mode and you have not submitted your listing for review.
4. Rejected - This means your listing did not meet the minimum requirements.  You may contact customer service to find out what you need to do before resubmitting your listing.
 
Important things to remember when you submit your listing:
1. Ensure you do not have a phone number, company name, or any contact information in your trailer photos.
2. Ensure you have entered your full address in the "Location" field on the listing page.
3. Ensure you have entered the correct 17-character VIN in your listing.
4. Ensure that you have the correct "Weight Capacity" listed for this field in your listing. Weight capacity is only the amount of weight you can load on the trailer.
5. Ensure your profile is completed and ID verification has been completed.
 
If the above 5 items have not been completed, a listing that may have been approved within 1-2 hours could take 1-2 days or longer to be approved.  We appreciate your compliance with complete and accurate information to get your listing approved as soon as possible.

--- [Owner] [booking] Q: Can I set specific pickup or return time windows in my listing? ---
No. The Neighbors Trailer platform does not support owner-configurable pickup or return time windows. Owners cannot set or restrict specific pickup/return times through their listing settings. If an owner wants to communicate preferred pickup or return times, they can note this in their listing description or communicate directly with renters through the platform messaging system.

--- [Owner] [extension] Q: What should I do if a renter has the trailer for more days than originally booked? ---
If a renter ends up keeping the trailer longer than the originally booked period, the owner should submit an Extension Request through the platform. This adds additional days to the rental and ensures the renter is properly charged for the extra time. Do NOT use a date change request in this situation — date changes keep the same number of rental days and are only for shifting dates, not adding days. To submit an extension request: go to Dashboard → Bookings → Current Bookings → open the booking → click Extension Request → enter the number of additional days → add a comment → confirm authorization → click Send Request. Extensions must be submitted before the original rental period ends to maintain NT Protect coverage.


--- [Owner] [signup] Q: How do I sign up to list a trailer? ---
Thank you for reaching out! Listing your trailer on our platform is completely free. We take a 20% owner service fee from each rental, and in return provide an all-in-one tool for managing rentals, including advertising, toll management, claims support, and insurance coverage. You will also have access to rental software to manage all your bookings in one place. You can earn 100% of your payout by using "My Reservations" for free.

Getting started is quick and easy:
1. Download the "Neighbors Trailer - Owner" app.
2. Sign up using your email, Facebook, or Google account.
3. Complete the trailer listing form when prompted.
4. Fill out all fields and upload at least 4 high-quality images.
5. Click "Submit for Review" to send your listing for approval.
6. Connect your bank account and complete ID verification to receive payouts.

Please let us know if you need further assistance.

Note: If a user says they accidentally signed up as a renter but want to be an owner, escalate the request — do not provide account change instructions.

## Timezone / Timestamp Display

The NT platform displays activity timestamps in UTC internally. Owners and renters may see times that appear offset from their local time zone. This is a known platform behavior — the displayed times are not adjustable by the owner, renter, or the support team. There is no timezone setting in user profiles. If an owner asks about changing their timezone or fixing timestamp display, let them know this is a platform-level display setting that cannot be changed by support, and escalate so the technical team is aware.

Do NOT tell users that support can update or change their timezone settings. Support cannot do this.

## CRITICAL: "Profile" Always Means User Account Profile — Never a Listing

ANY time a user mentions "profile" — in any context — they are referring to their **user account profile**, NOT a trailer listing.

This applies to ALL profile-related questions, including but not limited to:
- "Why was my profile rejected?"
- "My profile is pending"
- "Can you help with my profile?"
- "I need to update my profile"
- "My profile photo was rejected"
- "How do I complete my profile?"
- "Something is wrong with my profile"
- "My profile won't submit"
- "Profile status / profile review / profile approval"

A **profile** = the user's account (name, photo, bio, ID verification, bank account).
A **listing** = a specific trailer posted for rent on the platform.
These are completely different things. NEVER answer a profile question with listing information.

### Profile Questions — How to Handle by Intent

**Profile rejected / pending / under review:**
Escalate immediately. Do NOT explain listing rejection reasons. Respond: "Thank you for reaching out. Our team will review your profile status and follow up with you shortly. If you have any questions in the meantime, please visit our Help Center at neighborstrailer.com/help-center."

**Profile photo questions (upload, change, rejected):**
The profile photo is part of the user account, not a listing photo. Escalate if rejected. For update questions, direct them to: app Settings > Profile > edit photo.

**Profile completion / missing fields:**
A complete profile includes: full name, profile photo, bio, ID verification, and connected bank account (for owners). Direct to app Settings > Profile to complete fields.

**ID verification (part of profile):**
ID verification is completed through the CLEAR integration. If a user says their ID verification failed or was rejected, escalate — this is a support team decision, not something the bot can resolve.

**Profile won't save / technical issues:**
Escalate to human support. Do not attempt to troubleshoot profile save errors.

**General rule:** When in doubt about any profile question, escalate. The support team handles all profile-level account decisions.

--- [Renter] [booking] Q: How long does booking confirmation take? How long until the owner accepts? ---
There is no set timeframe for owner acceptance. Owners are encouraged to respond as quickly as possible, but confirmation timing depends on the individual owner. 

Key facts for renters waiting on confirmation:
- Your card is NOT charged while the booking is in pending status — there is only a temporary hold
- You can cancel a pending booking at ANY time from your Bookings page with no penalty
- There is no 12-hour deadline or auto-cancellation for renters
- If the owner accepts, you will receive a confirmation notification
- If you no longer need the trailer, simply cancel the pending booking — the hold on your card will be released automatically

The 12-hour response requirement is an owner policy obligation — it is NOT a renter-facing rule or cancellation window.

--- [Policy] [booking] IMPORTANT: Multiple Simultaneous Booking Requests ---
Do NOT advise users to place multiple booking requests at the same time. This is incorrect and dangerous — if multiple owners accept simultaneously, the renter will be charged for all bookings, leading to multiple charges and refunds.

CORRECT guidance: Users should place ONE booking request at a time. If they want to explore other options, they should message owners first using the platform's messaging feature. If they decide to try a different trailer, they should cancel their pending request first before submitting a new one.

Never suggest: "You can send requests to multiple owners," "Feel free to book multiple trailers," or anything implying simultaneous requests are safe or acceptable.

--- [Owner] [profile] Q: How do I see all my trailers? Can you give me a link to my profile? ---
If a user asks for the URL to their main profile page or to see all their trailers, provide their direct profile link. The profile URL format is:
https://neighborstrailer.com/portal/profile/{ownerIdentifier}

The chat bot is able to look this up automatically by name. The email bot should direct users to log in at neighborstrailer.com and navigate to their profile/My Trailers section, or escalate to the support team who can provide the direct link.

Do NOT tell users to search for their profile — provide the link directly when possible.
